1	pratītiḥ anyathā pratīyate rūpa asat nāma rūpeṇa para samvedanam samvedana gatiḥ pratipāditam abhāvāt aparam samāna antareṇa pūrva rūpam sakalam vastu pravarttate pareṇa anyena apara bhāvi pratipattiḥ svarūpa vyavahāraḥ samānam evantarhi paścāt apareṇa dṛśyate vedanam sambhavaḥ aparaḥ vyatirekeṇa bhrāntiḥ svarūpeṇa prāptam upalabhyate nna arthaḥ kathantarhi doṣaḥ pratīteḥ pratibhāsaḥ pramāṇam paraḥ pratibhāsa vedane pratīti spaṣṭa ākāra anyasya svarūpam pratibhāti varṇṇa śakyam athavā sattya bhāvaḥ paramārthataḥ īkṣyate kā vinā pratyakṣeṇa anya mātrakam kāla mātram kathat aparasya arthasya rūpasya anyat vyavahāra bhavatu sarva anyatra dvayam buddhiḥ dvayoḥ abhāve sambhavāt mātrāt kiñca kasyacid parasya yuktam svarūpasya artha iṣyate pratyakṣa udayaḥ bhaviṣyati pratibhāsanam pratyayaḥ sandehaḥ sattyam prāk bhavitavyam kinna cakṣuḥ pravarttanam varttamāna bhāvāt usti kalpanā pratīyamānam ekatā anavasthā vid samvedanāt pramāṇa padārtha kadācid parokṣa param pratibhāsate vidyate nahi prasaṅgaḥ tāyām pratibhāsanāt sarvasya sukha paraspara bhrānta vāsanā nīla kena mātreṇa vibhāgaḥ sthitiḥ kathañcid eka dṛṣṭa pratipannam mayā darśanam pratyetum bhedaḥ aspaṣṭa pratiniyata deśa rūpā idānīm asatti kathantasya grahaṇāt aparā samvedane dṛṣṭam balāt pratītau viśeṣaḥ mama kenacid samānaḥ udaya bhāj ūrthaḥ matiḥ pratipatteḥ samvittiḥ pratibhāsane prāptiḥ itara pratipattau asattya bhāve jñāyate pramā anumānena svena anyadā sakalaḥ svarūpe sadā abhāvaḥ sarvadā āsīt pratyakṣam sarvatra kevalam nyāyaḥ vṛthā atīta vikalpaḥ gamyate vyāpitā apratīteḥ sakala abhyāsāt vetti anumānam rūpaḥ ādinā samvedanasya pratyabhijñā avagacchati tvat vyavasthitiḥ mātrataḥ nittya yuktimat vittiḥ kasmāt apramāṇa bhāvinī korthaḥ anumānāt āyātam mātra kasya pratipādayiṣyate asattyam ātmā sarvam pratyeti uttaram pramāṇena paramparā vartti prasiddhiḥ sidhyati prasidhyati akṣa sākṣātkaraṇam sambhave vedana pratīyamānaḥ sambhavī saṅgatam vyartha avatāraḥ pūrvam paritoṣaḥ pratīta puras vastunaḥ tāyāḥ ayuktam anyatas darśane tathābhūta parama kriyā dṛṣṭeḥ vyatirikta am svayam grahaṇe yuktaḥ mātrakāt sakalasya parokṣam aparayoḥ vyavasthā kvāpi sutarām kalpanayā udayam prasaktam bhavataḥ niyamena tathābhūtam avisamvāda viṣayaḥ dṛṣṭasya ātma yuktā pratipannaḥ vṛttiḥ apratītiḥ yogaḥ ātmanā varttate abhyupagamaḥ vyāpi ti parisphuṭa śakyaḥ ekatva pratīyatām anumā koyam pratyakṣatā upalakṣyate anādi siddham adhyakṣa vyavahārāt apekṣayā parihāraḥ kathantad samvṛti kin samvādaḥ
2	arthaḥ abhiprāyaḥ darśayati bhāṣya abhiprāyeṇa idānīm sambhavati śakyate pūrvam sambandhaḥ antena avagamyate pūrva satyam bhaviṣyati kāraṇam āśaṃkya nāma kāreṇa kin ityādinā asmābhiḥ artha artham jñāna antaram asati bhāvaḥ siddham dvayena abhiprāyam vaktum darśitam sidhyati śabda prāk manyante anupapannam yāvat sambandha codayati pariharati mātram antareṇa darśitaḥ bhāṣyam prakaraṇāt dṛśyate anusāreṇa upapadyate jñāta evan upasaṃharati rūpeṇa pramāṇam vakṣyate antara itiḥ vādinām dhi saṃvid vivekaḥ vakṣyati ayuktam ubhaya uttaram bādhaḥ jñānam kalpanā kathañcid avaśyam jñātaḥ aparam avagatam yuktam prakāreṇa dūṣayati pakṣaḥ ubhayam śakyam asmākam manyate mā param bāhya rūpam iṣyate upanyasyati pramāṇa āpadyate draṣṭavyam buddhi kenacid apekṣāyām jāyate pratyakṣa āśayaḥ upapannam āpadyeta varṇitam siddhi buddhiḥ gocara śabdena dūṣaṇa para naḥ uktaḥ dvayam avagata matena ātmakam avasīyate āśaṅkya dūṣaṇam darśayitum kadācid darśayitavyaḥ yojyam darśayitavyam siddhānta gocaram tadvat arthāt nirākaraṇa ati anantaram paraiḥ abhidhīyate hetu upalabhyate ātmanā arthe uktā labhate avagantum vaktavyam adhikaraṇe vivṛṇoti bauddha kācid parastāt āśritam āhuḥ adhīna asambhavāt balena upariṣṭāt anyathā āśrīyate vakṣyāmaḥ kalpyate ātmānam āśrayaṇena bauddhaiḥ paraḥ mātreṇa tān āpādayati bodhaḥ vastu vādī laukikāḥ atyanta kasya upakramate abhipretya avagatā dharma jñāyate vadati etāvatā vakṣyamāṇa nirākaraṇam paścāt bahis mātra adhunā sarvam aṃśa apekṣayā kevalam caḥ samprati śakti darśayan anayoḥ anyat śabdāt vādinaḥ mate prathamam śabdaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ viśeṣaḥ avagataḥ apara nirākaroti upapadyeta taiḥ avatiṣṭhate sārdhena bhavat prāc upalabhāmahe āsīt āśaṅkate dvedhā sat anyatara abhidhānam svarūpa asyāḥ kena hetuḥ kiñ anupapattiḥ abhyupetya sūktam prakṛtam pāda tulya yad grahītum duṣyati nirākṛtam avasare doṣaḥ buddhau upanyasya prakṛta ākāram uttara ukte tasmin avadhāraṇe āśrayam itaretara su parihāraḥ siddha kasyacid sūkṣma vayam ubhayoḥ upapattiḥ mata lakṣyate kṛtā pada āpatteḥ nibandhanaḥ avidita purassaram prayogaḥ budhyate deśa yojayati vaktavyaḥ dvaya prāyeṇa upekṣya ucitam samānam śabdam ucyeta asmin itarathā pratyāha virodhaḥ pūrveṇa apekṣā sādhyamāne pratipādayitum vadanti vidita sūtrakāreṇa upapāditam viṣayā anumāna jāyamānam virodhāt ākṣepa bhāṣyeṇa siddhāntī arthayoḥ tathātvam avaseyam sāmarthyāt atiriktam sadbhāvaḥ ākhyāyate vārtika utpannāyām avāntara padam eka ādinā asmad prapañcayati
3	jñāna janya viṣaya jñānam kṛti janaka abhāvāt viśiṣṭa iṣṭa hetu anyathā jñāne vinā vācyam sādhana pramā viśeṣaṇa bhrama sādhya icchā jñānasya pravṛtti siddha kāraṇa rajata grahe hetuḥ gauravāt cikīrṣā āpatteḥ vṛtti grahaḥ vyabhicārāt ghaṭa bādhaka viṣayaka prakāraka sāmagrī māna dvārā pratibandhaka janyā sattvāt abhāva jñānāt janyam āvaśyaka prakāra anubhava aṃśe pratiyogi anugata kārya dhvaṃsa prasaṅgāt anumiti saṃsarga ādinā lāghavāt avacchedaka vyavahāra dhvaṃsaḥ viśeṣya bhāsate mātra vahni tādṛśa abhāvena dharma tava gocara avacchinna kiñca viśeṣa sattve asiddheḥ prayojaka asaṃsarga sākṣāt avacchedena dhī grahāt kḷpta rūpa bheda mā graha anubhavaḥ liṅga pāka bhramaḥ mātre sākṣātkāra ādāya niyamāt aśakyatvāt tṛṇa samaya pratyakṣa pravartakam nirastam ajanya yathārtha vaiśiṣṭyam ajanaka anantaram prāc adhīna āśraya yogya ayogya daśāyām paramparā agrahāt kālīna saṃnikarṣa jāti kṛtau jñāta anupapatteḥ etena ta aprayojaka svatas ka balavat pramāyām bādhāt viśeṣaṇam siddham prayojakam virodhi prati evañca anubhavāt bādhakam dhvaṃsasya vaiśiṣṭya avacchedakam ubhaya dāha indriya prāgabhāvasya pratibandhakaḥ samaye sambhavāt apramā atirikta kāraṇam tāvacchedaka kṛteḥ pratiyogika viṣayakam āgrahaḥ odana pāke mātrasya vastutas kalpanāt adṛṣṭa viṣayaḥ upāya āvṛtti tāvacchedakam sādhyam ananugamaḥ gata bhrame grāhaka kara rajate virahāt samūha upapatteḥ sthale ananugamāt tāyāḥ saṃbaddha tvañca asādhya āropaḥ mama prāgabhāva ananugata aviṣaya vyāpāra āśrayāt ananyathā vyabhicāraḥ bodhita asiddha kāmanā prathamam durita mūlaka svatantra mad adhikaraṇa bhinna sandhyā pratyakṣe tulya kṛtyā abhāvaḥ mānam siddhiḥ niyata agṛhīta anyonya mātram ajñānāt varti sādhanam samāna aniṣṭa raṅga anumita apāstam pramātvam eka pratyāsatti abhāvasya cākṣuṣa sākṣātkārasya pravṛtteḥ bhramāt pravṛttiḥ uddeśya jānāmi daśā anumiteḥ yogyatā arthi jñāte anvaya laghu itara nāśya vitti viśeṣaḥ bhramasya grahītum ati asamāna svarūpa janakam tvayoḥ śābda chedaka ekadā upādhi śabda upanīta lāghavena anumānāt āgrahāt nāśaka ananta viśeṣyaka prasaṅgaḥ prakṛte śukti bhojana sāmānya viṣaye viśiṣṭasya abādhita vṛṣṭi utkaṭa ahetu āyāsa bodhanāt sukha tulyam nāśe icchāyāḥ sādhanāt pūrvam anavasthānāt vyadhikaraṇa anutpatteḥ saṃbandha anumitiḥ cikīrṣāyām dvārāḥ pramāyāḥ anukūla pravṛttau pākasya pratibandhakam nānā viśeṣaṇasya phalaka niṣkampa avyāpteḥ anum īśvara apramāyām kāśī sakala
4	svabhāva svabhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ bhāva hetu bhāvasya vināśaḥ prāk antara vināśa hetoḥ paścāt kṣaṇika svabhāvasya nāśaḥ hetuḥ kriyā kasyacid ayogāt nāśa sthiti kṣaṇa kadācid bhāvānām bhāve anyathā artha karoti kārya apara nāma prasaṅgāt svayam janana apekṣā prasaṅgaḥ svabhāvena bhāvāt vināśasya sahakāri vastu utpattiḥ apekṣa abhāvāt atad utpatteḥ svabhāvataḥ avaśyam kiṃcid utpāda akṣaṇika sarvadā svabhāvam vināśe anyaḥ sāmarthyam sarvasya apekṣate kāryam nityasya āśrayaḥ kādācid sthira nityam kriyate avasthā abhāvaḥ utpannaḥ nāśasya pratyaya ātmanaḥ iṣyate ayuktam mudgara atiśayaḥ vai kutaścid krama sāmarthya akṣaṇikasya ātma sataḥ vināśam apekṣeta paraḥ upakāra bhāvam dharmā pratikṣaṇam antaram utpatti anapekṣa ahetuka lakṣaṇam kathaṃcid akṣaṇikaḥ avasthāyām kṛtaḥ kṣaṇe avasthaḥ kuryāt bhāvī virodhāt sarva bhāvi ahetu sambhavati naśvara kāla sthiteḥ prāc agni dharmaṇaḥ nitya antarasya abhāva nāśe sthitiḥ bhāvāḥ svabhāve kenacid upakāraḥ janakaḥ utpāde hetukaḥ samarthaḥ paraspara naṣṭaḥ sattā ka yuktaḥ para anya anapekṣaṇāt utpattau bhavana prati hetubhyaḥ kāṣṭhasya āśraya kāṣṭha rūpa janayet hetunā anādheya pratibandhaḥ yaugapadyābhyām vināśi kevalaḥ utpādaḥ karaṇāt kāle akṣepa tadvat anyasya tasmin hetubhiḥ eka niyamaḥ bhavan naśyati viśeṣasya apekṣam virodhi śaktiḥ avasthayoḥ yogāt ahetukaḥ kāṣṭham udaya doṣaḥ anavasthā janane hetavaḥ yujyate kṣaṇikam hetutaḥ saha abhāve mātra nirhetuka matam lakṣaṇa kevalam apekṣyate samarthasya aṅgāra kṣaṇikaḥ kartum upagame sthāpakaḥ akāraka hetuka kasmāt pūrva apekṣaṇāt bhavatu asambhavāt kevalasya apekṣaḥ utpanna anekāntaḥ ātmā atiśayam pṛthak bhāveṣu vinaśvara asāmarthyāt svabhāvāḥ nirapekṣaḥ apracyuta apekṣāyām sambhavāt apekṣya santānasya sambhavaḥ vastunaḥ tulyaḥ sahakāriṇā upakārakaḥ svarasa jātaḥ asthira anupakārāt deśa ahetoḥ niyama siddham brūmaḥ idānīm vinaśyet kṛtakaḥ sthita hetum virodhaḥ janaka sarvaḥ utpādāt abhāvasya kṣaṇasya karaṇa kṣaṇikānām upagamāt keṣāñcid yuktā jñāna vikalpaḥ hetūnām dharma eṣām nivṛttiḥ atiśaya vikalpa kṣamaḥ siddhāntavādi viśeṣaḥ kṛtakānām niḥsvabhāva bhavanam anapekṣaḥ janmanām pratikṣaṇa ajanakaḥ asāmarthyam kṣaṇikasya samartha virodhataḥ janayati indhana avasthānāt abhūtvā jananāt upayogaḥ sannidhi sannidhau kṣaṇikeṣu janakasya kapāla virahāt sattvam uttaram bhaṅga naśvaraḥ paraiḥ nivṛttau apekṣāyāḥ antarāt viśeṣa svatas anitya utpannasya krameṇa anupayogāt sahakāriṇaḥ yuktam athavā aviśeṣataḥ vaikalya apekṣi sahabhāva
5	cit arthaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ manyase vyāghātaḥ hetuḥ artha naḥ yuktam kasmāt kāraṇam antaram pratiṣedha abhidhīyate pratiṣidhyate artham brūmaḥ ayuktam bhavatā vaktavyam doṣaḥ vyāhatam sūtra pratipadyate sarvam pratiṣedhāt abhāvaḥ anabhyupagamāt asati prāpnoti kadā prasaṅgaḥ kasya uta mātram sūtram yuktaḥ anupapattiḥ kva aparijñānāt traikālya viṣayaḥ etena ahetuḥ uttaram bruvāṇaḥ bhavataḥ nivartate prāptam vaktavyaḥ kriyate upalabhyate pakṣe dṛṣṭāntaḥ anupapatteḥ ubhaya pratyuktam bhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ paśyāmaḥ bruvatā kāraṇa nāma anekāntaḥ vyāghātāt viśeṣa virodhaḥ sidhyati bādhate abhyupagamyate paścāt santi varṇayanti upādīyate dṛṣṭam upapattiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ abhāvāt viśeṣaḥ utpatti pramāṇataḥ bhāṣye anaikāntika anupapannam viṣaya vākyam eke kena abhidhānam pratiṣedhasya sādhanam antara mā tāni vyartham bhūt pratipadyase sambhavati bhāvaḥ pratijñā apare bhavān upalabdhi anartha pūrvam anivṛttaḥ antareṇa pramāṇam vai ekāntaḥ kila satyam nyāyaḥ pratiṣedhe vayam yāvat abhyanujñā arhati śeṣam viṣayam upapadyate sāmarthyam gamyate virodhāt bhavanti uttara arthasya ubhayam anupapannaḥ yāni anyat bruvate bhavatām pūrvavat vyatirekeṇa hetu ekasmin etasmin kā upalabhate pakṣa asiddheḥ pratiṣiddham avasthānam śakyam bhavatu niyamaḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ vācyam abhyupagamāt vādaḥ āśritya vaktum nivartyate āhosvit viruddhaḥ pramāṇāni pramāṇa pakṣaḥ bhavitavyam kāleṣu vartate nimitta vikalpa vyāhanyate śabdena siddhāntam bhāva āho asiddhiḥ praṣṭavyaḥ pratipādayati parihāraḥ etāvat ke nyāyena siddhiḥ bādhyate nimittam paryanuyojyaḥ sambhava abhyupeyaḥ nityam idānīm anaikāntikaḥ ādīni avasthānāt anya labhyate asiddhaḥ dharmaḥ siddheḥ nyāyam karoti adarśanāt vacanam pratijñāyate asmābhiḥ sāmānyāt pratipādakam vicāryate abhyanujñānāt anekāntāt bravīti anabhyupagame avatiṣṭhate vyatiriktam jñāpayati mayā ānarthakyam abhidhānāt śakyaḥ pratiṣedhyam bhavitum prasajyate abhyupagame asmākam nivṛtti dharma pravartate adoṣaḥ śabdasya sarva niyama vyāghāta sandihyate tādṛś pratyuktaḥ sādhayati anekaḥ ayuktaḥ abhyupagatam vijñāyate asambhavaḥ ekānta ubhayathā jānīte pratipadyamānena vyajñāyi triṣu anaikāntikī parihāram atīndriya anabhyupagata tulyam samānam brūṣe sāmānyam viśiṣyate ubhayoḥ bhāvānām bruvāṇena abhyupaiti pratipādayitum apramāṇam anyatra paryāyaḥ arthāpattiḥ eṣaḥ yathāśruti sarvaḥ pratyākhyānam pratiṣedhena abhaviṣyat apadeśaḥ upetya tantavaḥ sādhayanti tasmin asambaddham anupajāta anuyoktavyaḥ upalabdheḥ upādānam ādīn abhyanujñātam pratiṣedhati pratiṣeddhum pravartamānaḥ antare prati sūtrasya vākyasya yā bhāvam tulā anarthakam praśnaḥ vivādaḥ asmin hīyate mūrtimat vyāhanyeta bhavantaḥ vyākhyātaḥ prāptaḥ vyavasthitam vādinaḥ vastu kumbha
6	ākāra nīla grāhya artha jñāna grāhaka ākāraḥ jñānam ākāram viṣaya rūpa arthaḥ jñānasya vedanam arthasya buddhiḥ anubhavaḥ bāhya ātma buddheḥ ākārasya rūpam vāsanā buddhi anubhava grāhyam vijñānam saṃvid nīlam ākārā bāhyaḥ dhīḥ saṃvedanam ākāreṇa vijñāna su sārūpyam tasyāḥ jñānena bahis anubhūyate saha saṃvittiḥ pīta dvi bodha grāhyatā citra jñāne sārūpya vedya saṃvedana bāhyam vyavasthā viṣayaḥ arthena arthe samvedanam dhiyam grāhyaḥ ātmani grāhakam nīlasya dhiyaḥ ātmanaḥ grāhakayoḥ ātmā bāhye jñānāt niyamaḥ vijñāne anyathā yuktam niyamāt jñānayoḥ ākārāḥ saṃvitti ābhāsam vid sidhyati saṃvedanāt pratibhāsaḥ ākāre vijñānasya saṃvidaḥ samvedana vedane dhiyā prakāśate pratibhāsa phalam grahaṇa bāhyasya sthūla grāhyasya arthāt kevalam viṣayasya vedanāt abhāvāt vedana vedaka grāhakasya bheda nirākāra samanantara svayam matam mate grāhakaḥ para anyena ekam lakṣyate anyasya svarūpa iṣyate ādiḥ sārūpyāt mātra cakṣuḥ hetu arpaṇa anyā rūpeṇa ākārāt buddhyā ātmanā dhiyām aneka artheṣu antaram siddhiḥ muktvā tāyām ākāravat aṃśena bhūtaḥ upalambha anākāra sādhanam rūpaḥ siddham ajñāna nāma pratibhāsasya kasyacid bhedaḥ dhiyoḥ kalpanā meya paricchedaḥ vedyate uttaram sarvam avabhāsaḥ nirākāram aparokṣa dvaya abhinna dhī jānāmi hetuḥ pratikarma adhigatiḥ vedanā grāhye vyatiriktasya sarūpam grāhakāt anyaḥ iṣṭa ghaṭayati paramārthataḥ antareṇa aśakya sārūpye niyata pṛthak aṃśaḥ idānīm yuktā samvedanasya adhigateḥ antar vibhāvyate svabhāva vaśena ālambanam ubhaya āloka ālambyate saṃvitteḥ ghaṭa aparam saṃvittau pariccheda aniṣṭa aham ekaḥ vrajet gṛhṇīyāt saṃvidām jaḍa tulya āśritya vyavasthāpyate arthayoḥ anīla avabhāsinaḥ anubhavāt etena sarvasya vaśāt svarūpam darśanaiḥ nirbhāsam antara ābhāsaḥ anātma agrāhya sadṛśa udeti pratibhāsam prakāśa dṛśyate cetasaḥ saṃsarga artham sautra grāhikā rūpasya ālokaḥ jñānānām tādātmyāt niyāmakaḥ dvayoḥ pītasya siddhā iṣṭā utpadyate ābhāsa ākāratayā arthānām anākāram grāhyatām nirīkṣyate sūkṣma sārūpyeṇa paṭu nīlāt nīle avidyamānā yogyatā samvedanena upi vibhakta prasaṅgāt sya dvairūpyam vedanasya bhāsate grahaḥ svarūpeṇa avabhāsi gṛhṇāti saṃvidi vijñaptimātra anurūpa gṛhyeta nirbhāsaḥ doṣaḥ eka vivecanam pramāṇam ākārau vaicitryam īdṛśam kena yasyāḥ cetasā avedya lakṣaṇa svabhāvaḥ avibhāgaḥ janane śakti anubhāvyaḥ meyamāna pratibhāsena kṣamam ābhāsā kā gṛhyate aprasiddhitaḥ san adhīna bhidām viparyāsita bhūtasya
7	saṃbandhaḥ śabdaḥ eka vidhīyate gamyate bhaviṣyati śrutiḥ vidhiḥ arthaḥ śabdena anuvādaḥ brūmaḥ vākyam vākya vacanam artham vākyena vidhānam guṇa vacanaḥ karma vidhātum arhati śrutyā śaknoti saṃbandham bhidyeta saṃbandha prakaraṇāt prakaraṇam artha śruti guṇaḥ pakṣe anarthakam śrūyate bhavitum saṃbandhasya vidhāna saṃbandhe avagamyate antaram prāyaścittam prayojanam ubhayam prāpte śakyate upāṃśu haviḥ stuti vākyatā saṃbadhyate vacana vyāvartayati arthena lakṣaṇayā lakṣaṇā saṃbandhāt pūrṇamāsayoḥ graha pakṣam vākye yūpa rathantara vākyāt vidhīyeta anarthakaḥ vacanena arthavat saha prāptam kartum prakaraṇe dvau vidhāyakam darśa hāyanī nimitta lakṣaṇa vibhaktiḥ arthe strī śabda bādhyate ubhaya doṣaḥ nāmadheyam aṅgam saṃbandhi kuryāt homa juhoti vihitam vidhīyante dadhi nimittam karoti asati uta vidhi śakyam kartavyaḥ aṅga saṃbaddham vidhāne sāma anyat vatsa patnī avivakṣitam kriyate dravya saṃbhavati tuśabdaḥ stutiḥ avakalpate yāga codanā saṃyogāt saṃbadhyeta homaḥ asmin ekena jyotiṣṭomasya vratam bhedaḥ āmikṣā krayaḥ satyam vidadhāti vacane svaruḥ svarum vāravantīyam karmaṇi saṃyogaḥ nāma manuṣya evaṃjātīyakaḥ vidhānāt vivakṣitam etasya prayoga dhi vijñāyate yūpasya mātram krīṇāti annam kartavyam ubhayoḥ śabdam vacanāt kiṃcid pakṣaḥ yāgaḥ ekasmin upapadyate anyena saṃbhantsyate dadhnā pumān viśiṣṭaḥ balīyasī paśu prakaraṇa śabdasya aruṇa vākyatām sāmarthyāt vidhāsyati kṛtsna vaditum dvayoḥ vidhīyamāne vidhau eṣaḥ guṇena paśum prayojana kṛtvā dharmaḥ vidhāyakaḥ vidhinā saṃmārga itarathā arthā saṃbandhena vādaḥ pratyakṣam arthau sāmā ucyeta itarathāḥ bṛhat kraya prayojakam paśuḥ kratu ālambha revatīṣu yajati chāga arthāt abhāvāt ubhābhyām śakyaḥ kevalam prāpta viśeṣaḥ balīyaḥ vājapeya śravaṇam lakṣyate ārtiḥ aruṇayā śruteḥ saṃbaddhaḥ kalpyeta āghārayati aruṇā home vihitaḥ ekaḥ vivakṣyate nimitte chāgaḥ guṇāt vikalpaḥ saṃdehaḥ vājinam ubhau yūpaḥ paraspareṇa viśiṣṭam kṣauma vākyasya vatsaḥ draṣṭavyam yasmin āghāra vyāmohaḥ siddham śabdau brūyāt anuvādau nivītam rājā ārti jāghanī prakṛtāḥ ādīn etau nyāyyam tasmin ānarthakyam apūrvaḥ haviṣā samudāya rāja abhisaṃbandhaḥ viṣṇu homam ākāṅkṣati kalpayitavyam ālabheta śrutim homasya bhavitavyam vedi vinā ākāṅkṣam śrūyamāṇam niyogataḥ anūdyate prāya āghāram punātu purohitau skanne dhaviḥ sāmnaḥ aśva yajña viśeṣaṇam samāmnāyate upakaroti yā ānaya prāptaḥ tau manuṣyāṇām samāmananti avakalpeta prakṛtasya anuvāda vākyaḥ antareṇa bādhyeta anna
8	dravya guṇa dravyam pṛthivī rūpa guṇaḥ viśeṣa guṇāḥ eka sāmānya saṃkhyā samavāyaḥ āśraya artham karma guṇavat samavāyi kāraṇa aneka ākāśa tvañca guṇānām kriyāvat āśrita dravyeṣu samaveta paratva pṛthaktva vṛtti bhidyate dravyasya lakṣaṇam bhāvaḥ sādharmyam samavāyāt pṛthaktvam itarasmāt parimāṇa dravyāṇi apekṣayā samavāya saṃyoga dravye samāna karmasu lakṣaṇa paramāṇu aparatva guṇeṣu grahaṇam utkṣepaṇa jāti ādiḥ anyatra ādibhyaḥ vyavahāraḥ sadbhāve viśeṣāḥ padārtha vacanāt abhisambandhāt mūrta abhāvāt apara padam karmaṇām mahat antara guṇaiḥ sāmānyam diś buddhi nimitta kāraṇam nitya ādīni dravyāṇām vaidharmyam nirūpaṇa eṣām itarebhyaḥ kṣiti yeṣām sattā saṃyukta samavāyena vivakṣitam asādhāraṇa vyavahāra akāraṇa dravyavat pañcānām viśeṣaṇam ātma vyavaccheda anye anāśrita parimāṇam śabda karmāṇi śabdasya viśeṣaṇa nirūpaṇam idānīm sūtram viśeṣaḥ guṇasya trayāṇām yogaḥ padārtheṣu aparatve darśayati śabdaḥ dvi nirguṇa vibhu arthaḥ manyante niṣkriya samavetam artha ārambhakāḥ kāla dharma āśrayaḥ asamavāyi saṃjñā parama bhāvāt ukte apekṣam vidyate jñāyate karmabhyaḥ arthañca ākāśasya antāḥ vaiśeṣika adhikāre saṅkhī para ekatva yogi samavetāḥ upalakṣitaḥ ārambhaka vākyam nirāsa parīkṣā aparam asamāna abhāvaḥ astitva saṅkhyā siddham manaḥ param guṇān kriyā prakaraṇam nava etena samavetānām aṇu ādikā samavāye ekaikaśas anyeṣām antaram asmad dravyā tāni adravya jñānam ūhyam guru asambhavāt upalabdheḥ vibhāga aviśeṣaḥ jñāpana tvā antya samavetaḥ pratiṣedhāt pañca prasaṅgāt vaidharmya jātīya satya abhidhānāt adravyam ākāśe sambhavāt uktāni guṇī vyabhicāraḥ manasām dravyebhyaḥ pūrvam m grāhya abhidheya abhyupagame sat pūrvakāḥ pṛthivyāḥ antyāḥ mūrtiḥ paraspara bhavanti ṣaṇṇām utpattau apākaja sparśavatām avirodhi vyāvṛttam labhyate ekaika sāmānyāni tvan padārthāḥ kāryya sūtreṇa āśrayasya ātmanām sārva svarūpa vartate parāpara yāvat padārthānām tvat navānām sparśavat anupalabdheḥ viśeṣavat abhidhānam nityeṣu niyamena hetu dvandvaḥ śabdena vakṣyāmaḥ vipṛthaktva pratipādana vṛttiḥ anuvidhānāt vega guṇena dvividham pūrvavat pañcasu āśaṅkya vaidharmyāt parīkṣāyām vilakṣaṇa pratiniyata vibhāgāḥ ādibhiḥ tvāni satā vidyante ekam avasare ākāśaḥ sarvatra yasyāḥ keṣām āśritāḥ pariśeṣāt yathāsambhavam eteṣām abhyupagamāt rahita vartamānāḥ bhidyante avasara vyākhyeyam aprasaṅgāt mūrtta vibhāgau svarūpam gatānām nimittam vegavat bhāvi āśritam siddhāḥ vyabhicāra vyākhyātaḥ itaretara sadbhāvaḥ vyatiriktam gandha antānām tasyāḥ abhisambandhaḥ ātmani āśritānām
9	sādhya dharma pakṣa hetuḥ dharmaḥ hetu hetoḥ dharmi sādhana asiddhaḥ viruddha dharmī dharmiṇi pakṣaḥ pakṣe dharmasya asiddha lakṣaṇam sādhye anaikāntikaḥ viruddhaḥ anyatara vyāptiḥ sādhyaḥ anaikāntika dharmiṇaḥ eka avinā arthaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ lakṣaṇaḥ vyāpti lakṣaṇa mātra artham uktaḥ atyaya vipakṣāt tri vṛttiḥ vipakṣa siddhaḥ hetvābhāsāḥ dṛṣṭānta sādhyam siddha deśa dharmeṇa vipakṣe siddhau anvaya anyatra viśiṣṭaḥ bhāva vyāptaḥ pratijñā pakṣasya apakṣa nirdeśaḥ dharme avyabhicārī anumeya ubhaya prakaraṇa darśayitum sādhanayoḥ dharmiṇī sādhanam āśraya sadbhāvaḥ san cākṣuṣa vacanena anumeye kṛtaka niyataḥ rūpa bhāvaḥ sattvam asati pratibandha vṛtti hetum vipakṣaḥ ityādinā abādhita sāmānyena hetau liṅgasya sādhyasya vastutas dṛṣṭāntaḥ sambhavaḥ sarvasmin tridhā anyathā viparyaya asat gamaka pratihetuḥ ādiḥ dvau dṛṣṭānte hetvābhāsa etena anumeyaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ prakāraḥ lakṣaṇasya niyatam abhāvāt viparīta apadiṣṭaḥ aṃśena upadarśana samudāya apekṣayā viśeṣaḥ bādhā vṛtteḥ vipakṣayoḥ tasmin pratipakṣa viṣaya lakṣaṇe vartate labhyate pratihetu sādhanasya avyabhicāriṇaḥ kāla asiddhasya vivakṣita tulye anumeyena ābādhita darśitaḥ abhāve dharmatā deśe upacārāt siddhe niścitaḥ sambaddham asiddham apare āśrayaḥ sambhava sādhyena vyāpaka mātram anyataraḥ vacanāt svabhāva sādhyate pradarśyate asiddhau niyama sandigdha samānaḥ asiddhi avinābhāvaḥ siddheḥ sāmarthyam anvayaḥ asādhāraṇa abhāvaḥ dharmiṇā sādhane viparītaḥ darśayan viparīte dharmam asambhavāt saṃdigdha rūpam viruddhasya apadiṣṭa avadhāraṇena vyāpta asiddhe sandehe saṃgrahaḥ kasmāt vivakṣitaḥ aviśiṣṭaḥ liṅgam tulyaḥ dharmayoḥ pṛthak śabdena tanmātra sāmarthyāt siddhi prayoge pramāṇena iṣṭaḥ sambhavati padam vipakṣasya siddhiḥ viparyaye samudāyaḥ prasiddham jātīye prayogaḥ aṃśa asan darśayati upadarśyate hetvoḥ vyāptim dharmiṇoḥ samyak sandigdhaḥ gamakaḥ dharmya darśitam avadhāraṇe vyāpteḥ asapakṣaḥ hetvābhāse jijñāsita anvite avyabhicāri sambhave abhipreta paramārthataḥ viparītam sādhayitum ekaḥ bhāvayoḥ vivaraṇam viṣayaḥ anubandhaḥ vyabhicāraḥ nirastaḥ niścayaḥ upadarśanam aprasiddhaḥ sarvatra bhāga sajātīye sādhanāt alakṣaṇam dvaya sajātīyaḥ vyatireka pradarśana siṣā mātre vyāptyā siddham ṣaṣ vyavaccheda ubhayam vikalaḥ prayojaka vyadhikaraṇa anirākṛta bādhāvinā uktena asattva pakṣayoḥ prayogasya trirūpaḥ triṣu viparyayeṇa bhavatu udāharaṇa samāna hīna prabhedaḥ trividhaḥ dvayam dvitīyaḥ savyabhicāra savyabhicāraḥ anapadeśaḥ ekena asiddhiḥ sādhakaḥ udāharati lakṣaṇena dvipada avinābhāvi bahis nāma apadeśaḥ avadhāraṇam dharmavān anumāna vivakṣā pratihetoḥ sādhanaḥ anayoḥ vacanam sādhayati asapakṣe viṣāṇi
10	sādhya pratijñā śāstra doṣaḥ sādhanam virodhaḥ sādhyam sādhana iṣṭa bādhā hetu pakṣa siddha asiddha dharmi sādhyaḥ dharmiṇaḥ dharma sādhyate siddhaḥ śāstram viruddhaḥ pakṣaḥ iṣṭaḥ svayam virodha bādhanam dharmiṇi abhyupagama viruddha sādhane siddham iṣṭam artha vādinā sādhanāt hetuḥ bādhane abhyupagamaḥ sādhayitum asiddham vacana nirddeśaḥ dharmī anyathā uktaḥ vādinaḥ iṣṭasya abhyupagamāt hetoḥ para guṇa dharmaḥ sādhye dṛṣṭānta viparyaya siddhasya hetunā anitya virudhyate dharmasya sarva bādhāyām aprasiddha sādhyasya bādhanāt siddhe bādhyate sarvasya udāharaṇam asādhya asiddhaḥ sidhyati pramāṇena asiddhe ākāśa āgama icchā doṣa parasya siddhena viśeṣaṇam rūpeṇa nirdeśaḥ vāc ukteḥ śabde sādhanasya śabdaḥ lakṣaṇam uktiḥ virodhe dvitīya asiddhasya dṛṣṭānte pratijñayā samudāya pakṣasya āgamaḥ icchayā virodhasya ācāryeṇa prasaṅgaḥ bādha sādhayati siddhānta asādhana sāṃkhyasya asiddhau abhyupagatam bauddhasya nirākṛtaḥ śabda iṣyate śāstre nyāyaḥ pārārthyam asaṃhata īpsita nyāya sarvatra anumāna ubhaya dharmiṇī abhyupagata etena pramāṇa dharmiṇam parihāraḥ kena prasaṅga vāda hetvoḥ sarvam virodhena anirākṛtaḥ mātreṇa kṣatiḥ doṣavat ātma bādhaḥ parihāra uktyā īpsitaḥ virodhī dvāreṇa lakṣaṇena prati asādhyam abhyupagataḥ vacanena nirākaraṇam saha aniṣṭa sādhakaḥ asādhanam sādhanena viruddham viśeṣaṇaḥ prāha prasajyate viśeṣa vighāta ukti ananvaya pareṇa vivādaḥ sādhyayoḥ prasiddhena kevalaḥ nirdeśyaḥ artham siddhau bādhakam sāmānyena siddhiḥ asat śāstrasya kṛtaka āśraya saṃhata prasiddhaḥ upanyastam vādī anyatarasa pratijñāyāḥ abhyupagame arthasya tulya vivāda upagama pratijñātvam bādhite virodhayoḥ ādiḥ pratibandhaḥ kiñca mātrasya arthaḥ sādhayet dṛṣṭaye dṛṣṭāntayoḥ sthitiḥ parihāreṇa prakṛta vādi ayuktam dharmiṇā śaśī śāstreṇa vacanam śāstreṣu mātram sattyam uktau pratijñām abahis abhyupagatasya antarīyaka siddhyā prasiddha bauddhena idānīm arthāḥ viśeṣyaḥ prasiddhasya pratipāditam ātmā avyāpti kṛtya doṣeṇa kṛtā upagamāt abhidhānāt yuktam svadharmi adoṣaḥ abhimate nirākaraṇe vādya abhyupāyaḥ abhyupeta svarūpa samudāyaḥ mātra asambandhaḥ vadan svatantra mataḥ dharmya sambhave asiddheḥ ananvayaḥ caitanya nirākaraṇa bhūtaḥ vicāra anyasya vacanayoḥ pratijñayoḥ anuktau tvepi upagame pratiṣidhyate athavā puruṣa nirākaraṇāt vyāptam anapekṣam no śayana sādhitaḥ kevalam janaḥ aniṣṭam gatam sādhyā anuktam viśeṣaḥ su upagamaḥ dharmavati śakyate yuktaḥ prativādinaḥ upātta upanyāsa vacane anutpādya sādhayan pūrvavat arthe prasādhyate hetum bādhanī svayaṃgrahaṇam sādhanaḥ abhyupagamya paraḥ anāśrayaḥ
11	kārya kāryam kāraṇa sāmagrī śakti bīja kāraṇam sahakāri mṛd śaktiḥ kāryasya aṅkura upādāna janana viśeṣa utpattiḥ eka antara cakṣuḥ hetu janayati śakteḥ sahakāriṇaḥ kāraṇāt śāli utpattau kāraṇasya vijñāna janaka svabhāva utpādana ghaṭa bījam viśeṣaḥ utpadyate utpāda pratyaya kārye kāri atiśaya jananam yogya kāraka kāryāt pūrva sahakāriṇām saha paraspara samanantara antaram rūpa sāmagryāḥ janayanti ekasmāt janakam aṅkuraḥ avasthā anantaram kṣaṇa darśanāt sāmarthyam utpatti jātīya viśeṣasya ekam utpatteḥ piṇḍa kāraṇānām bījāt kāryāṇām santāna pratyekam janane abhāvāt apekṣayā bhāva samāna bhāvāt kṣiti janya mantra bījasya anyat ghaṭasya anyasya bhinna manaskāra udaka viśeṣāt aṅkurasya kulāla anantara jāyate viśiṣṭa vijñānam avāntara karoti kāryeṣu rūpam kāraṇāni śaktayaḥ jātīyam tāsām paṭa samarthāḥ dṛṣṭam upādānam tantu vilakṣaṇam śaktīnām ātmakam sarvam janyam pariṇāma vijātīya kevalānām saṃsthāna sadbhāve niyamāt vijñānāt ādibhyaḥ kāraṇena sāmarthya lakṣaṇam sarvadā śaktim avasthāyām yava svabhāvam bhāvena sarvatra upasarpaṇa svarūpa kāryāṇi jananāt kasmāt aneka ghaṭaḥ yogyatā pratiniyata dṛśyate parasparataḥ utpādanam pratiniyamaḥ viśeṣam cakṣu anutpattiḥ satsu gomaya tasyāḥ niyamaḥ antare vilakṣaṇāt hetoḥ kṛt daṇḍa kṣetra vijñānasya sahakārī santati karaṇe janmani samartha vyāpāraḥ vijātīyāt mṛdā utpādaḥ krameṇa utpādāt janikā kurvanti niyata bhāvānām anuguṇa salila kāribhyaḥ utpādayati kāraṇeṣu yā kārakam ekasya anyonya sahita pūrvam sāmagrya vema itara sāmagryā vaikalye niyamena nityam bhāvaḥ vailakṣaṇyam vyūha vyaktāt vilakṣaṇa utpadyamānam kācid janakaḥ lakṣaṇasya iṣyate viśeṣāḥ jātīyasya pratyayaiḥ lakṣaṇa vicitra sāmarthyāt śālūka janakāḥ śaktam anumīyate janma hetūnām yad kriyā śaktimat sahitam santānaḥ sākalyam utpadyeta kulālāt anvaya pariṇāmaḥ vyāpārāt pṛthak jātīyāt yathāsvam aṅkuram upajāyate kevalāḥ utpādayanti dṛṣṭā āloka kalāpasya sāmagrīm janayet samarthaḥ avyavadhāna janyate kāraṇe bhāve antyasya piṇḍāt prādurbhavati phala sahitāḥ anutpatteḥ svabhāvaḥ atiśayaḥ utpādane abhinna vaikalyāt kāryaḥ prasaṅgāt utpannam upayogāt anya hetuṣu ātmikā aṅkurayoḥ ati anyeṣu dṛśyante kalāpaḥ nāla pūrvakam kṛta kā kāryatvāt pratyayāt lakṣaṇāt akāraṇa prati apekṣya pratyayānām samartham samagra patita kāryeṇa mṛdaḥ suvarṇṇa svabhāvebhyaḥ lābhaḥ kāriṇaḥ anyā janye sannidhāna atīndriyā apāye piṇḍasya karaṇa viśiṣṭam prabhava sāmagryām prathama pūrvaka samudāya kāraṇayoḥ kārī vyatirekābhyām
12	nāma alam ati dṛśyate mā arhati vayam ittham bhavitum vastu mātram sādhu śabda pakṣe kā bhaviṣyati nūnam anupapatteḥ uta saṃbhavāt ācakṣate kiṃcid kṛtam vaktum su matiḥ adya yuktam patham kṛtaḥ eṣā sūkṣma brūmaḥ asaṃbhavāt kila upāya kāmam padārtha panthāḥ asādhu satyam varam saṃbhavati sarvathā pratīti bhavān rūpam bhavatu kalpanā pratyabhijñā avakalpate tasyām kṛtā prati sakala śakyate samaye siddham prasaṅgena asyāḥ kva pakṣaḥ grahaṇa vācaḥ vyākaraṇa aho siddhaye anayā ucitam vistareṇa abhyadhāyi jātam kiṃca asmābhiḥ svarūpa avatarati asmin paṃca siddha kathā ucyatām bahu pūrvam avasaraḥ tadānīm vaktavyam doṣaḥ velāyām kathyate āstām idānīm yuktiḥ nipuṇa avagama nibandhanaḥ mātra param nija jāti kasya pāda kadācid niyata bhāti nipuṇam vyavahāra bhavat hanta kācid naḥ kauśalam jana avasare vārtā vistarataḥ vidaḥ akhila bhūmiḥ tiṣṭhatu darśita abhūt enam prathamam amī athavā aaha cintyatām hṛdaya mama asāṃpratam pratyabhijñāyāḥ atiśayaḥ īdṛśam kena kathitam anupapannam atiśayam tasmin prakāra vyākaraṇam mahimnā bhavantaḥ mateḥ sāṃpratam cintyam vadana darśanāt upalabhyate bhavadbhiḥ vadanti vyākaraṇasya ātmanaḥ pratyaye niyama nirṇītam samasti paśyāmaḥ sādhubhiḥ vyavahāraḥ sthitam svarūpam ākhya gatvā kṛta atyantam prabhṛti udāhṛtam mate bhaṭṭaḥ durupapādaḥ atiśaya janaḥ bāḍham kāraṇam niyamaḥ kecid kutastyaḥ prabhavati vidmaḥ kevalam abhihitam pravṛtta mayā āhuḥ nayana nītyā tattvam vartmanā pratītiḥ śata gṛhyatām īkṣikayā eti kaiścid m durghaṭam asyām upadeśa spṛśati abhidhīyate upeyate vṛddha śūnya nijam vapuḥ samanantaram asmad janmani puṃsaḥ citram viśeṣaḥ balāt sahasā kalpanam saṃpratyayaḥ anupraveśa paryālocanayā aśakyatvāt avādi jarat yogi adhunā eṣaḥ darśitam rahita sannidhāne abhyupagatam avaśyam sādhāraṇam kalpate itara dhruvam nara jagat durghaṭaḥ nikara sthite anupalambhāt prakriyā asi evañca kam anavagata bhāraḥ ādinā kartum āste vartinaḥ avagamyate tava vyavasthita lakṣaṇe kuśa saṃpadyate kalpayitum karaṇam sarvatra dīrgha sahasra yā dūṣitam racanā avagati turaga īdṛśaḥ sādhavaḥ vistaram bhāvam kalpyate iyān kāri upayāti anyaiḥ bhaveyuḥ avadhiḥ kalāpa tathāvidha varṇanam bāla gamyaḥ varge avacchinna aprayojakam kutra aham anuvarti parisphurati bhavatā lokaḥ alīka dūram apāya mārgaḥ yukti vakṣyāmaḥ avidita durāśā viracita coditam bhaṅga
13	vidhi pravṛtti vidhiḥ artha phala vidheḥ svarga niyogaḥ sādhana niyoga arthaḥ puruṣa adhikāra antara pramāṇa pravṛttiḥ liṅā viṣaya nā bhāvanā upāya kāma śabda cā vākya aṅga sādhya yāga kartavya pravartaka anyathā phalam pravartate pravṛtteḥ apekṣa svarūpa kārya kriyā kāmya loke niyojya vyāpāraḥ bhūta avagamāt puruṣaḥ prayojana viniyoga vidhau viṣayaḥ niṣedha avagamyate codanā kartavyatā adhikāri karaṇa vede karmma adhikāraḥ niyogasya abhāvāt pravṛttau avagamaḥ nivṛtti anuṣṭhāna pravartanā pratyavāya apūrva apekṣita kāmaḥ vidhinā pravartakam arthe niyogāt gocaraḥ bhāva pratipatti kārye prayoga pravartakaḥ siddheḥ liṅa hetu anya anuṣṭhānam pratīteḥ iṣṭa nitye ātma adhikārī yogya siddhiḥ śabdāt pravartanam preraka phalasya mātra antareṇa nibandhanaḥ karma bhavatu preraṇā kalpanā prīti ananya evā māna bhāvanām aṃśa saṃbandha kuryāt ādiḥ arthā antarā preraṇa matam kāla vāda hetuḥ viśeṣa sākṣāt phale prayojanam abhidhā mātram satyam kratu avivakṣita śruteḥ śreyaḥ vacaḥ yathāśakti apūrvam vidhīyate pravartana pravarteta siddhaḥ aṃśe artham svādhyāyaḥ upāyaḥ vartamāna dvāreṇa vidhānam yajeta pravartayati niyoge pramāṇam kāmanā phalavat icchā siddha tattva sāram avagata parāḥ bhāvanāyām svādhyāya karmmaṇaḥ pravṛttaḥ vaiyarthyam apekṣā mukhena vidhayaḥ avaśya anuṣṭhāne nivṛttī vyāpāra dṛṣṭa viśeṣaḥ sāmarthya vaiyarthyāt sarvatra arthitā apravṛtta arthavāda śāstra prādhānyam pravṛtta prasaṅgaḥ rūpa upāye anuṣṭheya sambandham vyāpāre niṣedhaḥ niyuktaḥ kartavyam apravṛtti anaṅga arthāt adhyayana ceṣṭā adhikārāt upayogi lakṣaṇaḥ niyujyate nimitta viśiṣṭa pada siddhārtha anyatas upāyam upadeśaḥ avagatiḥ liṅarthaḥ pratibhā avabodhaḥ nindā kāryya vidhāyaka prayoktṛ śabdasya apekṣatā niṣṭhaḥ apekṣāyām anapekṣita siddhe anyat upāsana adhikāre alam siddhi vidheya pratipatteḥ ājñā pravṛttyā arthī pūrva āhuḥ dhātu pramāṇakaḥ apuruṣa pratipattiḥ akaraṇe svargasya samīhita hita pramāṇaka prekṣā upadeśa pravarttate viśeṣaṇa viniyogaḥ apekṣate puruṣam śruta kasya kāryam parihāra niyogataḥ pratyayāt apravṛtteḥ nivṛttyoḥ paraḥ viṣaye brahma anuṣṭheyaḥ vedāntānām kāryaḥ nirūpyate niyojyaḥ nañaḥ vṛthā anutiṣṭhati sāmarthyam phalā abhyupāya labhyam karttavyatā pravarttanā vidhim rūpaḥ loka asaṃbhavāt nibandhana prāpti bhāvanāyāḥ prekṣāvatām vārtam anyā pratīyate niṣṭha śabdena pratīti vakṣyate tasyāḥ śruti kuru tṛpti adhikāreṣu śaktiḥ sambandhe sāmarthyena vākyāt coditaḥ niṣedhayoḥ prakaraṇa ittham anapekṣa adhikārā
14	eka aneka ekam rūpa ekasya bhedaḥ bhinna nānā bheda rūpam vastu svabhāva ekaḥ paraspara dharma ātma abhinna ekatra anekam rūpeṇa vastunaḥ ekasmin bhedāt ekena bhede viruddha ātmanā bhinnaḥ anya antara dvayoḥ dvi dravya prasaṅgaḥ ekasmāt virodhaḥ svabhāvaḥ parasparam prasaṅgāt abheda bhinnam dvaya rūpasya bhedena abhedaḥ paryāya ātmanaḥ rūpaḥ abhinnam ātmakam virodhāt pṛthak tau rūpe ekā lakṣaṇa ātmaka bhedasya ekatva iṣyate bhāvaḥ syātām abhinnaḥ sarva svabhāvasya bhāva yogaḥ antaram anekaḥ anyathā dvayam kathañcid bhāvāḥ paryāyāḥ dharmi anyaḥ ananya citra anekasya yujyate ekatvam avasthā ayogāt yugapad ubhaya dharmaḥ ātmā tābhyām adhyāsaḥ anekatra abhede rūpayoḥ syuḥ yuktaḥ atad anekena dravyāt dharmiṇoḥ abhāva para vṛtteḥ bhedam yogāt bahavaḥ dravyam saṃsargaḥ bhedānām sakṛt vyāvṛtti antarasya anyonya paryāyayoḥ abhinne ekaika dve abhibhava bhedāḥ ātmānam sarvathā yuktam sarvatra bahūnām bhinnānām kenacid rūpāṇām sarvasya ghaṭaḥ svabhāvena samudāya abhedāt svabhāvam tvepi bhavataḥ vyavasthiteḥ pratyekam sambhavaḥ bhidyate anupraveśaḥ saṃsthānayoḥ sarveṣām svabhāvāt aparasya anyasya bhidyante kathaṃcid abhinnasya yoge itaretara vastunī sthitau ātmakaḥ śrutiḥ aṃśaḥ kārya bhāvasya bhinnāḥ hīyeta iṣṭam arthānām kalpita virahāt kalpanā samāveśaḥ abhyupagamāt vastuni saṃjñā aviśeṣāt vyavasthā ātmani abhāvāt doṣaḥ bahuṣu pariṇāma anekasmāt bhūte eṣām bhedataḥ adoṣaḥ sambandhāt adhyāsa saṃsarga vyapadeśaḥ dharmī viśeṣayoḥ upagamāt śabdena tāyāḥ upi vikalpa kalpanayā nānātvam hāneḥ tāyām artha paryāyāṇām abhedasya dvitīyasya virudhyate bhāvāt aparaspara abhyupagamya ayuktaḥ asmāt abhedam dharmma draṣṭavyaḥ vai dvitīya svabhāvāḥ ekaikam anyena sāmāna atyantam anyatra prasajyeta ghaṭasya bhinnayoḥ yau svarūpeṇa avirodhaḥ sarve dvau tādātmya adhikaraṇya imau kiñca dharmiṇaḥ adhyāse aikātmye ekaikena dūṣaṇam upagame ucyeta samānaḥ avasthitam niyata svabhāvau prāṇānām pūrvavat viśvam dravyasya anyonyam śleṣa tvayoḥ yogakṣema vācyaḥ prasaṅga adhyāsāt rasayoḥ ātmanoḥ lakṣaṇaḥ sthite vācinī abhyupagamyate vyāvṛttiḥ virodha yujyete tasmin viṣayau bhoktṛtā udbhava ekasyām bhinne abhyupeyate nānātva paramārthataḥ dharmau dravye kalpanāyām bhinnā ākārau pratipattiḥ śrotṛ svabhāvānām paryāyaḥ ātmakāḥ yayoḥ pratibhāseta nimittaḥ paryāyatā aparā parihāreṇa āt ekāntena dharmeṇa kasmāt anugāmi dharmayoḥ kalpitaḥ āśrayāt āśaṃkamānaḥ ekārtha adhikṛtya svabhāvayoḥ bhāvyam bahu ekatvena anartha aṃśa uktaḥ
15	vastu artha vikalpa sāmānya sāmānyam viṣayaḥ anya lakṣaṇam kriyā rūpa śabda rūpam vastuni viṣaya apoha vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇa arthaḥ vikalpaḥ atad vikalpasya vastunaḥ avastu apohaḥ buddhi ākāra maṇi vyāvṛttiḥ vikalpānām jñāna rūpeṇa vijātīya vikalpena kalpita ākāraḥ anartha buddhiḥ viṣayā rūpasya vidhi vyāvṛtta saṃketa tasyāḥ arthe keśa lakṣaṇe sāmānyasya viṣayam vyāvṛttam dhiyaḥ lakṣaṇasya buddhau sāmarthya vāsanā kalpanā adhyavasāyāt adhyavasāya vikalpāḥ darśana parama kriyām kāri pṛṣṭha jñeya viṣayāḥ adhyavasāyena bāhya adhyavasāyaḥ nīla āśrayeṇa śabdānām dhīḥ bhrānti pāramparyeṇa sarvatas sat gocaraḥ āropita vyavaccheda tathābhūta śrutiḥ pratibhāsa sākṣāt śabdena śabdasya āśritya viṣayasya jñāne pratibhāsate ākārasya pratibhāsinaḥ abhāvāt anyat buddhyā vyavahāra asat pratibhāsi artheṣu pravṛttiḥ arthasya dṛśya bheda bhāvinaḥ eka sāmānyena ākāreṇa paramārthataḥ vastūnām vikalpayoḥ ekīkṛtya pratīti sāmānye darśayan vaśāt prabhāyām pratiṣedha pratibhāsam vikalpikā ago vyavahāraḥ vikalpe śabdāt svabhāva sajātīya vyāvṛttasya anyatra vastutas sarvā vikalpaiḥ bhedena mātra svarūpa anādi paramārtha upādāna pratibhāti saṅketa kriyāyām ayogāt sphuṭa buddheḥ kṛt bhāva samāropita pratibandhāt nāma kalpitasya tattva viṣayeṇa tadvat āśrayaḥ jñānena gocarāḥ vyāvṛttyā arthikā abhinna nirvikalpa abhidhāna arthau kiñcana ādiḥ nimittam kasmāt arthāḥ arthāt pratibhāsā kalpitaḥ vikalpyau vyāvṛttau su vācyaḥ gateḥ manyate rūpaḥ pratyabhijñāna vyāvṛtteḥ taimirika rūpāṇām vyavasthā viṣayāt svabhāvam bhedinaḥ pravṛtti bhrāntiḥ iṣyate pratītiḥ adhyavasāyī śabdāḥ sādhyām athavā uktā pravṛtteḥ vṛtteḥ aṃśa yojanāt teṣu ālocanā grahaḥ jananāt matam kevalam pratipattiḥ adhyavasīyate śrutau pravartante kāriṇaḥ asādhāraṇa bhedaḥ kathantarhi vyavacchedaḥ avācya spaṣṭa tathāvidha bhinnam yojyate pratibhāsasya sādhāraṇa bhāvān pratibhāsaḥ vikalpam nīlam yad abhāve tvābhyām pratibhāsanāt vikalpā yojanā bhāveṣu aviṣayaḥ āropitam siddhitaḥ svabhāvena dvaividhyam samāśrayāt dhvaniḥ vāstava bhāve yogya adhya pāramārthikaḥ pradhāna aspaṣṭa svarūpeṇa saṃketaḥ lakṣaṇaḥ ābhoga ātad abhedena śabdaiḥ prabhā doṣaḥ utpatteḥ dvaya yogyaḥ ta śūnyayoḥ apratibhāsanāt vyavasthāpyate pratibaddhaḥ kārya asphuṭa ahita kenacid abhedinaḥ abhāva cetasaḥ yojana arthā anurodhataḥ apohe vyavahartāraḥ anurodhāt netra adhyavasāyam avyabhicāriṇī vikalpāt ābhāsa anveti arthinām pratibaddha adhyakṣa bhrāntyā nirvikalpaka bhrānteḥ ātmanā niṣṭhā sambandhāt abhiprāya pratibhāse varṇṇa nibandhanam upādānaḥ niveditam bhūta abāhya ābhānti niṣṭheṣu prakīrtitam sadṛśam sūcitam
16	anumānam liṅga dhūma agni liṅgam deśa sambandha dhūmaḥ anumāna agniḥ anumīyate sambandhaḥ anumeya dṛṣṭam vyāpti liṅgasya avinā agneḥ liṅgi dhūmasya sāmānyatas darśanāt eka anumānena dhūmāt anumāne pratyakṣa liṅgāt viśeṣa viśiṣṭaḥ dṛṣṭa dṛṣṭvā anumānāt dhūmam pūrvavat sāmānyena viśeṣeṇa agninā pratipattiḥ viśiṣṭa sāmānyatodṛṣṭam dharma grahaṇam anumānasya kāla pūrvaka darśana deśaḥ parvata pratyakṣeṇa sambandhasya darśanam agnau agnimān agnim śeṣavat ādinā upalabhya viṣayam pūrvam liṅginoḥ pūrvakam gamaka vyāptiḥ mātram nadī dṛṣṭaḥ liṅgena liṅge antara anumeyaḥ dhūmena sāmānya kāle sambandhi grahaṇa sambandham dhūmayoḥ pūrva viśeṣaḥ gati anumeyam anyatra megha vṛṣṭi pratyakṣataḥ liṅgini grahaṇāt vṛṣṭiḥ pradeśa parokṣa anyathā pratipadyate saha gamakam liṅgī deśasya adṛṣṭa anagni gamya anumita pratyakṣaḥ gatiḥ dārṣṭa pradeśe sambandhe atīndriya dharmi liṅgataḥ mahānasa arthāpattiḥ pāṇḍu antare vyabhicāri liṅginaḥ vyāpteḥ pratyakṣam vinā pāvaka pratibandha dahana sarvatra trividham sambandhinaḥ sāmānyam anumātum varṣa viśeṣe anumāpayati aṅgam mātra vahniḥ dṛṣṭasya śakyate darśanena sāhitya śabdena deśe pratyakṣā dharmeṇa parvataḥ laiṅgikam anumā viśiṣṭasya bhaviṣyati deśī sāmānyasya avagamyate dvividham viśeṣam dhūmavat gamayati abhau vahneḥ dharmī pūra vyāpya liṅgatā vṛkṣa pradeśaḥ sambaddham tārṇa pratipattau abhāva sāhacarya agnimat ādibhiḥ adṛṣṭam vahni mātrāt avadhāritam viśiṣṭam tadānīm anumīyeta sambhavati avinābhūtam anumiti apekṣayā upalabdhā parāmarśa tadvat udaya avinābhāvaḥ tri anumāya jala vyāpaka prāk aliṅga saṃyogi mat sattā anumāsyate prasiddhaḥ anumitiḥ gṛhītvā vyabhicāraḥ udāharaṇam dṛṣṭāt niyataḥ viśeṣasya jātam bhūyas niyamam janayati vyabhicārāt parāmarśaḥ anagnau anumimīte pravartate pipīlikā dhūme gṛhītaḥ pratibandhaḥ dṛṣṭā candra dhūmavān viśiṣṭe avinābhāva anumāpakam indhana bhūta vartate aprāṇiṣu vṛṣṭimat anavagatam gamyaḥ ananumāna deśam upari avagataḥ dharmiṇaḥ pratītau sambandhī anumānānām prāptiḥ pakṣe vyāptau samudra upalambhāt vyāptaḥ anagniḥ anupapattyā arhati anumeyasya gṛhīta apratyakṣa upalabdheḥ sāhityam avinābhauvi avinābhāvasya mātreṇa liṅgaḥ upalabhyamānam anumīyatām niyamaḥ viśeṣayoḥ upalabdha anumitam gamakaḥ anyadā pratyakṣatas vidā pāramparyeṇa ananumeya jñāta udayaḥ pratītiḥ uttara anuminoti kṛttikā pipīlika vyāpyāt viśiṣṭena śeṣaḥ bhāvi paśyati pratīyate anupalabdha gamayet iṣyate liṅginī pūraḥ nidarśane sāmānyatodṛṣṭa anumānataḥ viśeṣāṇām avagamaḥ dharmaḥ evaṃvidha antarāt avinābhāvi trairūpya pratipattuḥ kathyate apratyakṣasya bhavitum ubhayam apratyakṣaḥ caśabdaḥ
17	pramāṇa pratyakṣa anumāna pramāṇam anumānam pratyakṣam anumānasya pratyakṣeṇa viṣaya prameya anumānena pratyakṣasya prāmāṇyam antara siddhiḥ āgama viṣayaḥ pramāṇena apramāṇam artha viṣaye vastu viṣayam pramāṇasya anumānāt anumāne abhāvāt bādhakam parokṣa siddheḥ bādhaka lakṣaṇa bādhyate apramāṇa antaram anumānayoḥ sāmānya bala antareṇa loka viśeṣa pratyakṣāt grāhi siddham pramāṇāt pūrvaka pramāṇāni siddhau bādhita anavasthā pratyakṣataḥ pratyakṣe adhigata pramāṇānām prāmāṇya aprāmāṇyam itara viruddham sādhaka siddhi anadhigata āgamasya āgamena gṛhīta āgamaḥ sādhanam prameyasya liṅga prasiddhiḥ pravartate pramāṇataḥ ayuktam virodhaḥ vyavahāra pramāṇaiḥ anyathā pravṛttam pratibandha paricchede vyavasthā viruddha pūrvakam arthāpatti parokṣe prameyam virodha asambhavāt sambandha prasiddham para viṣayasya kāla apratyakṣa sarva anabhyupagamāt sambhavāt anumānataḥ siddha māna kṣaṇika lakṣaṇam asiddheḥ apekṣa bādhya āgamayoḥ avaśyam nirāsaḥ mūla itaretara sambhave pramāṇe ayogāt pravṛtteḥ apramāṇāt yuktam darśanāt saṃplavaḥ aprāmāṇya tri kasyacid śāstreṇa virodhe pratyakṣaḥ parokṣam asmad bhāvāt pratipatteḥ vṛttam vyavahāreṇa abhyupagamāt sādhakam mānam pratyakṣatas paraspara pratyakṣena mūlam mātra pratipatti dvaya prati grāhakam grahaṇa prāmāṇye virodhāt sādhayati avagamyate anupapatteḥ ekam pratipattau sādhanasya anumānābhyām antar āśraya prasiddha abhyupagamaḥ apekṣam dvaividhyāt viparīta pramā adhigamāt sadbhāve adhyakṣa pariccheda abhyupagantavyam prasiddhi sambhavati antarbhāvaḥ tvā āhuḥ pravṛtta gantṛ iṣyate pratipādayiṣyate svarūpasya prasaṅgaḥ pramāṇeṣu meya anyasya anuṣṇaḥ aprāmāṇye arthe yogi siddhyati prasaṅgāt abhāve ābhāsa siddhasya paricchedaḥ aviṣaye apramāṇasya liṅgam bhāvinā antarataḥ liṅgena avisaṃvādāt dvaividhyam bādhyamāna vinā pravarttate sambhavaḥ dvaividhya vṛttiḥ matam tṛtīya dvayam śāstram asiddham niṣeddhṛ aitihya āgamābhyām tvayā antarāṇām vācaḥ sāmānye bādhakasya balavat sadbhāva anumeya balīyaḥ aprasiddheḥ atīndriya no dūṣaṇam vidhātṛ apratyakṣam nara antarbhāva grāhiṇā parigraham pravartitum traividhyam siddhyā prāk āgamāt pratyakṣā pratipādita bhāva sādhana anyena upamāna jātam aśakyatvāt anyatas nivartayati sāmarthya adhigantṛ apramāṇena pravarttakam prāmāṇyasya pravṛtti niścayaḥ siddhe anumānañca gocare abhāva vyavasthāpyate grahaṇe abhyupagame pratipāditam pariśeṣa bādhyam anapekṣam dvividham adhigantum adhigama prāmāṇyāt grāhyaḥ prakāra pravarttaka itarat saṅkhyā sthitam agniḥ upalambhāt vastuni vyāpti andha prasiddheḥ adhigamyate prāpaṇa ātmakasya sāṃvyavahārikam su sadbhāvaḥ uttara parokṣasya bādhane āgamaiḥ pravṛttena adhigatiḥ kṣaṇa anyaiḥ parijñānam śiraḥ adhigate asaṃbhavāt avisaṃvādaka dṛṣṭānta pratipādanāya dūṣitam
18	īśvara kartṛ īśvaraḥ ghaṭa kārya śarīra sarva siddhiḥ kṣiti jagat asmad īśvarasya sarvajña viśeṣa buddhimat ayuktam adṛṣṭa pūrvaka prasaṅgāt buddhi sanniveśa prasaṅgaḥ āśraya icchā kāryam yuktam abhāvāt viśeṣaḥ kiṃcid kāraṇa upādāna mātreṇa kulāla upalambhāt siddhau nimitta sarga aviśeṣe nitya kasyacid darśanāt siddheḥ kartā saṃsthānam acetana vaicitryam sthāvara puruṣa saṃsthāna sādhanam aviśeṣāt anupapatteḥ sarvasya īśvare mṛd anyathā dṛṣṭam dṛṣṭānta antareṇa cetana vinā asiddham karma cetanā upapatteḥ sāmarthyam sambhavati siddha kāryasya sarvam adhiṣṭhātṛ kṣaṇika upalabdheḥ sarveṣām asiddha ādiḥ jagataḥ śarīrasya aśarīra bhagavataḥ sthitvā anya ati siddham siddhyati asiddhau abhijña sadbhāvaḥ sāmarthya vaicitrya kāryatvasya sidhyati īśvareṇa kartṛka anyasya pūrvakam bhuvana tanu āśrita sadbhāva kāryatva ananta alam vistareṇa upalabdham kāryatvam etena abhyupagame akartṛ karttṛ vyāptam asiddheḥ sarvatra keṣāṃcid kalpyate pakṣe anumīyate pravṛttiḥ paramāṇu viśeṣeṇa asiddhiḥ sarvajñaḥ siddhaḥ viśiṣṭa sadbhāve kriyā akāraṇam anumānam adhiṣṭhātā dṛṣṭāntaḥ niyama adhiṣṭhita iṣyate kṛta kartum prasiddhasya vilakṣaṇa anīśvara niyata sambhavāt vivāda kartṛkam vicitra aiśvaryam kāryatvāt anyeṣām aśarīrasya prāsāda pramāṇam adhiṣṭhitam viśeṣāt dṛṣṭānte samasta anumāneṣu bāla dṛṣṭa mukta vakṣyāmaḥ anavasthā balena upalabhyate ādibhiḥ icchayā prasajyate sanniveśaḥ ātma abhyupagamāt pravartate śarīram asambhavāt krīḍā abhyupagantavyam anaikāntika kāraṇam avasthāyām śakyate vṛkṣa prāṇinām pūrvakatva utpādana upapadyate viśeṣam vyāpāra utpatti kumbhakāra pūrva pravṛtteḥ anupalambhāt mātram paramāṇavaḥ anabhyupagamāt racanā virodhāt icchataḥ dūṣaṇam pravartante viśeṣāṇām samartha bhagavān nimittam karoti asarvajña ādinā svabhāva kartuḥ asat sādhya nirmāṇa upakaraṇa pāṇḍu acetanaḥ niratiśaya paṭa loka nityasya pralaya tādṛś uccheda abhāvaḥ karaṇe vicitram mātrāt kṛtam pratyuktaḥ upacāreṇa kṛtaḥ pratiṣedha bādhita matam samarthitam daṇḍa sādhyate utpattau aiśvarya mātrasya karmaṇām acetanānām sādhye sādhyam kartāram iṣṭam abhyupagantavyaḥ samānam dharma tvā anaikāntikam acetanasya jñāna ādya ekasya svābhāvika para bhedena samarthaḥ adhiṣṭhitāni sādhane yuktā toya svatantraḥ aviśeṣeṇa kartāraḥ vyāpi anupapannam karttā aviśeṣa prāṇi anuvidhāyi itaretara adhikaraṇa niyāmaka yādṛś jñaḥ upacaya hetu karaṇa avyatireki preraka parameśvara pṛthivī abhipretam kenacid ātmanām cetanaḥ svātantryam yeṣu vādinām kalpanayā cetanasya niyamaḥ akartā hīna pratiṣiddham valmīkasya icchām kāryyam svābhāvyāt viśeṣe hetūnām upapattau vikārasya
19	kasmāt puruṣa sattva pradhāna prakṛti puruṣasya pradhānam puruṣaḥ rajaḥ buddhi antara antaram ayuktam tamaḥ prasaṃgaḥ prakṛtiḥ guṇa buddhiḥ pañca prasaṃgāt pradhānasya sargaḥ pariṇāmaḥ bhūta mahat vikāra dharma matam avyaktam kārya anyat vyaktam kiṃca vṛtti buddheḥ guṇānām tattva pravartate rūpa pravṛttiḥ vṛttiḥ viṣaya prakṛteḥ bhāva śabda kāryam śakti avasthā bhoktṛ sattvam kāraṇa mahataḥ bhogaḥ ādyāḥ pravṛtteḥ vyakta prakāśa kāraṇam prāc sukha pariṇāma anupapatteḥ siddham kaivalyam ahaṃkāraḥ avyakta nimitta lakṣaṇam artham eṣām saṃghāta saukṣmyāt tuṣṭiḥ pradhānāt vikāraḥ aniṣṭam draṣṭṛ acetanam karaṇa utpadyate anupapannam pravṛtti mahān buddhau kālam labhate tamasaḥ bhāvena vikṛtiḥ ṣoḍaśakaḥ tanmātrāṇi vaktavyam nimittaḥ tanmātra pūrva rūpam śayana sama puṃsaḥ pṛthivī vikārāṇām tamasām vṛttam karmendriyāṇi prati sarva paraspara atiśaya bhogya ākhyaḥ brūmaḥ ahaṃkāra ādibhiḥ aṅga buddhīndriyāṇi vyaktasya dṛṣṭā satyam arthaḥ sarvam sapta āpannam triguṇa tanmātram nivartate parama prāk prāptam moha anupapattiḥ aprakṛti adhyavasāya darśanāt ācāryaḥ ārambhaḥ śarīra siddhiḥ vāc strī sūkṣma indriya liṅgam bhoga puruṣam bhoktā prasava śaktiḥ tuṣṭi indriyāṇi viparyaya kṛtvā bhedāḥ etasmāt kṣaya anekāntāt satkārya abhyupagamāt sattvasya siddhi caitanya sūkṣmam abhyupagamyate upapadyate viparyayāt sāṃkhya puruṣayoḥ rūpā prakṛtīnām rajasaḥ kaivalya ānarthakyam laghu svarūpa bhūtāni aśakti parimitam bhūtam avasthānam kintarhi ṛṣeḥ bhedānām mātraḥ pumān mātram asmi antareṇa prabhṛtīnām mūlaprakṛtiḥ ātmaka puruṣeṇa viśeṣa itaretara mātra vikṛtayaḥ antarasya ahaṅkāraḥ puruṣāṇām ekādaśa apadiṣṭam guṇāḥ vṛttim pradhāne vyūha vaiśvarūpyam upakāri jijñāsā kiṃcid tasyām ācaṣṭe ahaṃkārāt avikṛtiḥ kāla citi dṛṣṭam ittham kṣīra adoṣaḥ parikalpanā viśeṣāḥ mahābhūtāni prāṇa aviśeṣāḥ vimokṣa sāmarthyāt vikṛti aviśeṣa autsukya avasthām saṃghātaḥ avaraḥ pariṇata abhimāna eṣā kṛtaḥ kṣīrasya paṅgu ātmānam aṅgi sākṣi sanniveśa daśadhā pariṇāmāḥ sannidhāna parimāṇāt ādibhyaḥ sarūpam iyattā acetana parimāṇam sāmya gaṇaḥ akartṛ pariśeṣataḥ parvaṇaḥ prakṛtayaḥ avasthitam vibhu vaiṣamyam bhūtānām vārṣa vipratipatteḥ athavā dṛśyam saṃkalpa saṃsarati traya tadvat karaṇam yuktam indriyāṇām vyavasāya upadiṣṭam māhātmya dṛś upalabdhiḥ siddheḥ prakāśya bhāvam upanipātāt vaiṣamya vāyavaḥ karaṇasya idānīm cetanaḥ prāṇinaḥ gamanāt pūrvasmāt prāpnoti ahaṅkāra ācāryāṇām pañcabhyaḥ yogāt kurute avasthāyinī pariṇamate tamasā vadhāḥ avasthāna vyūhaḥ abhidhīyate
20	śabda artha śabdaḥ śabdasya śabdāt vācya arthaḥ vācaka sambandha artham sambandhaḥ śabdānām arthayoḥ arthe śabdena anyathā pratītiḥ saṅketa samaya saṃketa śabdāḥ śabde vivakṣā śabdam go pratipattiḥ vācakaḥ arthasya icchā arthāpattiḥ pratīti sambandhasya abhidhāna abhidheya samayaḥ saṃketaḥ antara pūrvikā abhāvāt vyavahāra artheṣu anupapattyā saṅketaḥ vācyaḥ niyamaḥ antareṇa kalpanā prayoga arthena puruṣa pratipatti śakti vaktuḥ vṛddha pratipādaka prayogaḥ vyutpattiḥ sambandhāt prayogāt mātra vyutpatti gavā balena saṃjñā śābda pratipādayati upapadyate pramāṇa gāvi aśabda pratipadyate sāmarthyāt loke dṛṣṭaḥ śabdaiḥ abhiprāya sambandhe pratipattau śaktiḥ pratītau anvaya viśeṣe lakṣaṇaḥ śrutaḥ arthāpatti āpattiḥ kṛta kāle punaruktam samayasya vaśena śabdeṣu vyavahārāt dāha pratīyate ukte śrotuḥ niyama anyatra prayoge pratītim prasiddha gāvī pratīteḥ abhidhā prasiddhaḥ hetuḥ nāma anurodhinaḥ svābhāvikaḥ saha vyavasthā vyatirekābhyām vācyam prayuñjate saṅketasya prati śabdān vivakṣayā arthāpattyā agṛhīta prayujyate samayam arthaiḥ akṛta viṣayā anumānāt jīvati vaśāt hasta sambandham darśanāt vācakam saṃketam vacana arthāt vyavahāraḥ svābhāvika mleccha vāc pratyāyana śravaṇāt viśeṣa pratipādana pratyaya prasaṅgāt gauḥ antare śravaṇa itas kṛtvas abhidheyaḥ avagamaḥ saṅketam anupapattiḥ uccāraṇa vyatireka abhidhāne pratyāyaka bhāva vaktṛ śabdebhyaḥ icchāyāḥ phalaḥ antaram pratipadyante samayāt vyāpriyate abhidhāyī pratīta arthau uktaḥ prasaṅgaḥ lokataḥ kācid yogyatā sāmarthya pravṛtti vācakāḥ avācaka vyapadiśati pratipādyate ṛte karaṇa śakteḥ gamayati kṛte yadṛcchā avaśyam vivakṣāyām vyāpāraḥ antarīyaka arthavān avyutpanna deva puruṣaiḥ yogya vivakṣāyāḥ yogyāḥ saṃketāt uccaritāt niyame śakyate kalpanāyām saṃketena pratipadya udāhṛtā pratyāyakaḥ puruṣeṇa avagama mātram ceṣṭayā vyapadeśaḥ datta ayuktam avinā bālāḥ ati abhiprāye pratīte avagatiḥ prayuktaḥ pratipādakaḥ nānā abhidhāyi saṅketena vācakayoḥ nimitta prasiddhi gṛhīta yuktā avagantum vivakṣātaḥ vāci sthaḥ abhidhatte arthavat apaśabdaḥ vṛddhebhyaḥ yogyatām dṛṣṭā prayoktā nyāyena paryāya prayogasya janayati sārtha kā aniyata śrutāt vaktā nimittam upāyaḥ etad prathama vācyasya goṇī arthāpatteḥ sambandhāḥ sāmarthyam tiraścām dṛśyate apekṣate bhājaḥ anupapadyamāna vyutpanna nimittavati vācyānām ceṣṭā pratipadyāmahe prasiddhiḥ prayujyante arthānām svabhāvataḥ apekṣi sambandhi megheṣu śakyaḥ prasiddham pratipattuḥ sarvatra abhidhānasya vācinām devadattaḥ anupapadyamānaḥ sambaddha vācye jñāpana paśyāmaḥ pratipattā anyam pratyeti sambhavaḥ anupapannaḥ saṅketāt vivakṣām śrotra kaiścid vyavahārāya dhāvati
21	rūpa jñāna prakāśa ākāra ātma jñānam ayuktam vijñāna svarūpam para prakāśaḥ vijñānam saṃvedanam jñānasya ātmā bodha svarūpa artha ātmanaḥ ātmaka rūpam upapadyate antara prakāśate antaram prasaṅgaḥ saṃvedana ātmānam jñānena viṣaya ātmani āhosvit arthaḥ kriyate rūpeṇa prakāśaka eka sattā pradīpa svayam santāna ātmakam vijñānasya ātmanā utpādyate saha saṃvedya ajñāta ghaṭa arthasya janaka dahana aviśeṣāt anupapattiḥ antareṇa vyatirikta phala svabhāva janya prakāśakam arpaka atad utpādya hetu prakāśe utpannam aprakāśa prāpnoti bhūtena vyāvartate lakṣaṇa asattvam tādātmye s ayogāt rūpiṇaḥ abodha saṃvittiḥ svarūpasya pakṣe jñāne jñeya prakāśakaḥ nīla jñāpyate vaktavyam avadhāraṇam anya sarva janakatvā ubhayam jñānāt ajñānam itas jñāta mātra anyat āpadyate arthayoḥ samāna saṃvedyate vedyate āho astitvam nayana pratīyate prakāśasya avyatiriktam prasaktam mātreṇa janyate upādāna tādātmyam prakāśanam utpādaka satī nāma tāttvikaḥ vyatirekāt vijñānena svarūpāt anyasya prakāśam prakāśya vedyam prakāśyate saṃvedyam rūpasya parasya avijñāna jñāyate atāttvikaḥ janakatva jñānayoḥ ātmikā avyatirikta prasajyate saṃvid asva apadiśyate atiśayena anavagateḥ kena pradīpaḥ svasmāt abhyupagame sita vijñānāt aśakya dahanasya bodhāt ajñātaḥ tādātmyāt anupapatteḥ saṃvedanasya svasya avyatirekaḥ ekam bhāvaḥ upajāta vidyate asaṃbhavāt sambaddhaḥ svabhāvam yogi sambandha antare gṛhīti avyatiriktā tādātmyena abhyupagamyate utpādanam saṃvedanena vyavasthā vedya jāte bodhasya ekasya buddhau abhinna virahaḥ prakāśane bhāvāḥ viditam anabhyupagame pratibhāti upalambhasya vedanam prakāśamānaḥ vetsi abhyupagamāt avyatiriktaḥ sambandham abhiprāyāt piśāca prasaṃgaḥ kāle utpattiḥ bhāvānām jagat sarvasya cha bhinna labhyate nivartate prakāśayati prāptā anyaḥ meya dṛṣṭiḥ upalabdham tādātmya anyā āloka antarasya jam dīpa sattvam anupapannam bhavat iṣyate ātmakena pakṣīkaraṇam utpādita ātmanoḥ anavasthā pāryate vaḥ prakāśayet ā upajāyate avadhārita rūpāt bhavatu prakāśā gṛhṇāti vaktavyaḥ saṃvedane aho avabhāti upalambha virodhāt astitva anupapattau bhavatām adhikaraṇa janakatvena sitā śaknoti anupajāta vedyaḥ saṃvittau āvirbhāvaḥ anabhyupagamāt datta saṃbhavati anupapannaḥ mate vyavasthita jāḥ pratanyate anativṛtteḥ uta anayā vyavasthitiḥ vivecyate vilakṣaṇa jñātaḥ utpāde pratikarma avirala pradīpāt aprakāśāyām saṃviditam svīkaraṇam upalambhe gīyate paryavasitam ātmasāt avabodhasya hīyate rūpāḥ pratyuktam gṛhyate svarūpeṇa prakāśanāt pūrva kā svam utpādayati svabhāvatayā jaḍa alam ākārāt kāraka svabhāvā dūṣaṇam avasīyate ja rūpā
22	duḥkha tattva karma sukha duḥkham sukham avidyā mokṣa brahma mokṣaḥ ātma janma apavargaḥ saṃsāra śarīra pravṛtti jñāna bhoga bandha apavarga nivṛttiḥ karmaṇām brahmaṇaḥ sarva jñānāt phalam doṣa ātmā phala kleśa ānanda jñānam tapaḥ mukti nitya vidyā pravṛttiḥ artham mithyājñāna rāga niḥśreyasa ātmanaḥ yoga adharma saṃsāraḥ kṣayaḥ mithyā sukhasya kṛta abhāvāt puruṣa nivṛttau karmāṇi ucchedaḥ akṛta ānandam sarvam mithyājñānam duḥkhasya muktiḥ jīva anādi anādiḥ niḥśreyasam mokṣe muktasya deha nivṛtti naraka priya pāpa upāyaḥ hāna pretyabhāvaḥ kṛtam apāye upabhoga upabhogaḥ āhuḥ kṣaya vividha muktaḥ vipāka śravaṇa uparamaḥ atyanta nāśa heyam ātyantika mokṣam abhāvaḥ bandhaḥ apāyaḥ brahmaṇi parama hetu vidyayā heya dharma karmaṇaḥ anye iṣṭa duḥkhe manyante bādhanā nivṛtteḥ artha bhayam upabhogāt īśvara prāyaścitta aśeṣa ucchedāt maraṇa aniṣṭa viditvā apuruṣa karmaṇā kecid duḥkhena āśayaḥ mukta apavarge vipākaḥ tattvam vairāgya abhyāsa sādhana puṇya bhogaḥ uccheda adhyātma ānandaḥ sukhe nāśe nivartate kṣīyate sampadyate anubandhāt atyantam para śruteḥ nimittam sukhī dharmāt arthaḥ abhyāgama bhogāt hānam pravartate jñānena abhayam mucyate yogaḥ kṣayāt nityam ciram viśuddha viṣaya uddiśya viveka kṣīyante parīkṣate upabhogena upaśama prapañca śubha aśakya dhyāna prāptiḥ śruti vidvān mithyājñānasya paramātma abhāve viyogaḥ nāśaḥ tattvataḥ kāma avasthānam vipākasya utpanna avasthāyām dvāreṇa anupapattiḥ karoti apavargam adharmau adhigama śama jñānasya svarūpa mala samādhi ātmani amṛtam vyādhi vai ātmanām anubandhaḥ pīḍā pratyātma loka avidyāyāḥ yama santateḥ śrūyate ātmānam pretya jñātvā tasmin śuddha sambhavāt kasmāt saṃsāre viyoga śravaṇāt phalasya santoṣa śrotavyaḥ avidyayā vimokṣaḥ svarga saṃsāri mantavyaḥ aśarīram mokṣasya samyak brahmā paramātmanaḥ kalpa bhāvanā kāya buddhi adhigamaḥ āpnoti upāyena jīvānām parikṣayaḥ nikhila rūpam indriya maya kleśasya kleśāt pratisandhānāya ātyantikaḥ jñātavyaḥ bhogena yāvat āvartate mahā janmani moha janitaḥ ucchede vidaḥ saṃsārasya amṛta anantam kṣudh viṣa virodhaḥ ātmānaḥ syām kṛtasya vipākam śoka avaśyam anurūpaiḥ apriye nididhyāsitavyaḥ duḥkhi śāmyati viśuddham yoginaḥ bhūtāni brahmacarya hānasya upāye nimittaḥ santati abhuktam nāśam naraḥ pravṛttaḥ uparama aikātmya anuṣaṅgāt prakṣayaḥ akarma śrutiḥ avāptiḥ bhūt anirmokṣaḥ manana ādibhiḥ doṣāḥ advitīyam bhasmasāt
23	kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ kāryam kāraṇam bhāva abhāve svabhāva bhāve dhūma bhāvāt dhūmaḥ kāryasya pratibandhaḥ kāraṇe abhāvāt gamaka vṛkṣa anvaya hetuḥ agni śiṃśapā svabhāvaḥ hetu janya kāraṇasya vyatireka niyamaḥ tādātmya anyathā hetau vinā kāraṇāt gamya dhūmasya niyama bhāvasya kāraṇayoḥ kāraṇena sāmagrī indhana akārya janyaḥ avaśyam avyabhicāraḥ tādṛśaḥ tādātmyam abhāvaḥ antareṇa janaka svabhāvasya tādṛśa svabhāvāt utpatti niyamāt avinā nimitta avyabhicāra antarasya artha tādṛśasya dahana agneḥ vyabhicarati sambandhaḥ gatiḥ bhavataḥ sarvathā bhāvitā vyabhicāraḥ viśeṣa kārye pratibaddha naimittika atad vyabhicārāt anyasya anyatas darśanāt anyaḥ apratibaddha gamakaḥ bhāvam niyata janma vahni vyāpakasya bhāvi bhāvena vyāpyasya pratibandha adarśanāt svabhāve asati kāryatva anya kāryāt avyabhicārāt śakra pratibandhe ahetu svabhāvaiḥ svabhāvam lakṣaṇaḥ tau aṃśena agniḥ sakṛt adhīna gamakam vṛkṣaḥ avinābhāvaḥ pratibandhāt hetumat kāryayoḥ utpatteḥ tanmātra akāraṇa vyāpaka tādṛśā anyādṛśāt sambhavaḥ bhavan lakṣaṇam kāryeṇa anagni nimitte hetoḥ sāmānyayoḥ utpattī niyamena iṣṭam akāryam tādātmye gamyate bhavat vahneḥ taiḥ ātmanaḥ akāraṇasya kāryatā sambhavāt nibandhana apekṣayā vyatirekābhyām kāryā saṃyogi kāryatvam uktaḥ niyāmakāt vahniḥ parasya sambhave vyāpya svabhāvayoḥ hetavaḥ kasmāt sarvaḥ pratibandham dvidhā iṣyate satsu abhimata adhūma udāhṛtiḥ kadācid pratibaddhaḥ gamyaḥ kāraṇā nibandhanam dharmaiḥ agnau bhasma sattā sambhavati dahanaḥ vyabhicārasya anuvidhānāt vyabhicārī vyāpakam yāvadbhiḥ bhavanam jalam vastutas akāraṇam antara gamayati avinābhāva dvau avinābhāvi ahetuka gamyasya bhāvau utpattyoḥ sādhanaḥ abhau antare anyasmāt vyabhicāra sidhyataḥ janmanaḥ tāyāḥ dhūmāt niyamasya arthāt samam siddhi dṛśyate nivartayet buddhī tasyāḥ viparyaye abhāvena yasmin samudbhavāt sannidhānāt niyatam nibandhanaḥ vyabhicāre bhāvinaḥ parasparam dṛṣṭaḥ tathāvidha ahetukaḥ vyāpakaḥ asambandhaḥ abhāvasya bhāvyam yujyate viparyayau dhūmam gamye kalpanāyām tādṛśam hetuka pāvaka nimittasya anāgatasya abhavataḥ avaśyaṃbhāva martyena samagreṇa niścetum tābhyām gamakāḥ kāraṇābhyām tādṛśāt antarīyaka svayam dharmaḥ nivartamānam niyojyatām utpattibhyām svabhāvena pratyuktā dharmāṇām avyabhicārataḥ adhīnasya bhāvābhyām aparaḥ utpattiḥ bhaviṣyati athavā niścīyate hetunā anupalambhābhyām kāraṇañca bhavanti prasaṅgāt upalambhe vyāpake anāyatta ātādṛśa śiṃśapām vadhaka anupalambha tathābhūtaḥ rasāt saṃsiddhiḥ gamyam vyatirekiṇaḥ anurodhini hutabhujaḥ anartha anāśvāsaḥ janitaḥ anubandhi jāyeta sāmānya vadhya abhāvābhyām atiprasaṅgaḥ vikāra anyeṣām agnim nimittāt śiṃśapa svam araṇi vyapadeśe
24	jñānam pramāṇam pramāṇa lakṣaṇam lakṣaṇa phalam pratyakṣa pratyakṣam prameyam viṣaya artham artha phala viṣayam prameya jñāna sat jñānasya arthaḥ pramāṇāni indriya anumāna samprayoga viśeṣaṇa anyat utpadyate sannikarṣa lakṣaṇasya sāmānya lakṣaṇe jam iṣṭam pramīyate animitta pramāṇasya svarūpam liṅga samprayogaḥ pramāṇe avyapadeśyam vidyamāna sādhanam vijñānam ātmakam pramitiḥ pratyakṣasya grahaṇam pūrvakam viśeṣaṇam lakṣya trividham upalambhana janma buddhi lakṣaṇāt avyabhicāri lakṣyam pramātṛ ityādinā indriyāṇām pramātā animittam adhigamaḥ avyapadeśya rūpam svarūpa sarvam śabdaḥ hāna pramāṇānām viśeṣya dve utpannam darśanam viśeṣa upādeya labhyate vyavasāya pramā lakṣyate antaram śābdam anumānam sūtram samprayoge phalayoḥ samākhyā vyākhyātam karaṇa vyapadiśyate adhigama pṛthak kāraṇam vyavaccheda ālocana pariccheda anye heya upamāna iṣyate uktaḥ darśayati ja laiṅgika etāvat viṣayaḥ prameye anumānayoḥ kṛtvā jñānāt saṃprayoge mātram prameyāṇi idānīm pūrvaka sūtre nirākaraṇa yuktam nimitta ati adhyavasāyaḥ lakṣaṇena upayujyate anantaram ayuktam jñāne arthe prāk niścaya vaktavyam ābhāsa jñeyam satyam ātmaka dvividham siddha dvayam jñāyate samyak vyapadeśya ābhāsam adhigame asati nirāsa nirdiṣṭam sādhakatama padam nirdeśaḥ laiṅgikam avi sannikarṣaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ saṃprayogaḥ puruṣasya avyabhicārāt karaṇam vipratipatti vācyam vyapadeśyam upekṣaṇīya vaśāt anumāne sannikarṣāt svabhāvam prasajyate asādhāraṇam avyāpti prameyaḥ sūtra janakam yadābhāsam pramāṇāt prativiṣaya param liṅgi darśitam upekṣā saṃkhyā avadhāraṇa śābda etena upādeyaḥ tāni pratyakṣe buddhiḥ janitam prāmāṇyam saṃśaya trīṇi vivakṣayā sūcayati janyate pramiti ācakṣate īdṛśam ākhyātam ārṣa ātma phale pūrvavat vibhāga nirvikalpam pakṣe sidhyanti satsu trayam prameyāḥ doṣaḥ mādhyasthya heyaḥ viśeṣaṇāni anuvādena viṣayasya anubhava kathanam upalabdhi nirdeśa sannikarṣasya avyāptiḥ pramātuḥ anarthakam vyabhicarati lakṣyasya loka śeṣam yogaḥ sattām vyatiriktam apramāṇam hānam ekam prāpnoti boddhavyam tasmin jñānānām anumānasya abhimatam śabdena janmani upādāna apare asatī atiprasaṅgaḥ avadhāryate jñāpayati sūtrāt arthasya prati sakala avasara śabdāḥ samprayogāt kila pramāṇeṣu taiḥ prameyasya varṇitam apramāṇa vyabhicārāt buddhayaḥ utpatteḥ prameyayoḥ dvidhā niścayam kurvat upalambhanam vyartham athavā ajñāna sthitam mṛgatṛṣṇā phalasya caśabdaḥ niścayaḥ samāna vigrahaḥ vidyā vyavacchinnam prādhānyāt alakṣaṇa prāmāṇya dvitīyam atulyam kaiścid aparīkṣā kāraiḥ pareṣām kevalam sāmagrī nirdiśati vyudāsaḥ utpanna padena pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ pratipadyate vyudāsa prasiddha sūtrasya prastha etad
25	sarva nirvāṇam śūnyatā ārya bhāvānām bhagavatā svabhāvaḥ vidyate bhāvāḥ lokaḥ svabhāva bhāva śūnyam dharmāḥ sarvam pratītya śūnyāḥ grāhaḥ śūnya skandha māyā dharma dharmāṇām niḥsvabhāva śūnyatām bhaviṣyati santi nirodhaḥ tathāgataḥ svabhāvena aśūnyam ubhayam paśyati yujyate dharmān tathāgata saṃbhavati kasya upādāya svabhāvam śāśvata dṛṣṭayaḥ bhagavān viparyāsa sūtre kiṃcid svabhāvataḥ śūnyaḥ upapadyate mahā deśanā prapañca jāyate vijñeyam bhavatā anta śubham buddha avidyā niḥsvabhāvāḥ pratītyasamutpāda nirvāṇa upamam buddhaḥ bhāvaḥ anyat saṃskṛta mṛṣā paramārthataḥ aśubham duḥkham parama bhikṣavaḥ jarā dharmaḥ apratītya pratītyasamutpādaḥ bhava nāma vineya hetu satyam anupādāya antam nirodha prajñāpāramitā bhāvam bhaviṣyāmi madhyamaka viparyayāḥ aviparīta moṣa samāḥ buddhānām niḥsvabhāvam yujyante nirodhāt para utpāda kṛtvā sattva anātmā dṛṣṭi satyānām koṭiḥ jātu śāśvataḥ jagat kevalam idānīm samudayaḥ kleśa bhāveṣu niyatam rūpam tattvam ratna aham saṃskṛtam śūnyatāyām prathamaḥ nirudhyate niḥsvabhāvaḥ marīci pūrvam deva etāḥ kasyacid niravaśeṣa ime abhāvāt vistaraḥ uccheda loka pratyaya lokasya niruddhe avidyamāne yathāvat bāla lakṣaṇam carame kāśyapa pratītyasamutpādam pratipādayan bhagavan asmākam svabhāvasya darśanam pi phalāni saṃbhavanti vayam buddhaiḥ pratibimba putra no param śūnye saṃsāra sarvathā deśitam tathyam kaści vyayaḥ dharmeṣu kalpa catuṣṭayam upamāḥ nyāyena prasajyate viparyāsaḥ caturṇām prahāṇam mārgaḥ anantavān anutpannāḥ pratibādhase sarvi tathatā viparyayaḥ āryāṇām deśitaḥ abhāvaḥ catvāri dvaya abhūvam tvayā nu saṃskārāḥ phala śivam tathāgatasya artham pratītyasamutpādasya adhvani bhavān sarve brūmaḥ asaṃskṛtam subhūte tathāgate upamaḥ aṅkuraḥ anyathātvam jana abhāva maraṇa nirmitaḥ apara paśyanti tattva vyaya bhagavatām yā pādaiḥ paratantra parikalpita dharmāṇa viparyāsāḥ dharmam mithyā upalabhate anuccheda anutpāda mama bhāvān abhidhātavyam ahetutaḥ aśāśvataḥ prabhavanti saṃtatiḥ śubha tān antavat darśana citta aniruddham astitvam vāda skandhānām udaya jāti bhagavataḥ jānati jāyati nirmitakaḥ saddharmaḥ uhyate vidyati bhadanta pariniṣpannaḥ kalpanā śānta kleśānām prahāṇa eṣā niḥsaraṇam śāśvatam vyavasthāpyate ācārya pratītyasamutpanna ācāryaḥ svatas vidyante śūnyeṣu udayaḥ cakra saṃsāraḥ loke aśāśvata nirodhasya nāstitvam anantam vistareṇa antavān samam pratipad paratas prajñapti kadāci mañju saṃghe vadāmi svapna astitva atyanta asati saṃkleśa san dharmakam anutpannam samyak mārgasya śāntam pūrva maraṇāt avatāra avatāre sārdham
26	indriya pratyakṣam pratyakṣa jñānam kalpanā akṣa artha viṣaya manaḥ jam mānasam vikalpakam jñāna sannikarṣa vikalpaka vijñānam aparokṣa viṣayam akṣam nirvikalpaka indriyasya pratyakṣasya indriyam cakṣuḥ vikalpa ja indriyeṇa apoḍham arthaḥ nirvikalpakam mānasa viṣaye viṣayaḥ apratyakṣa śabda vijñāna vyāpāra jñānasya jā artham arthe gocaraḥ grahaṇam vikalpaḥ spaṣṭa vyavasāya utpadyate anindriya rūpa sannikarṣāt iṣyate manasā sākṣāt grāhi avikalpaka vyapadeśaḥ pratyakṣaḥ sannikarṣaḥ pratyakṣeṇa yojanā yogi matiḥ avikalpakam smaraṇa viśeṣaṇa apratyakṣam apoḍha pratyakṣatā smṛti vyavasāyaḥ akṣasya gauḥ abhra pratyakṣe manasaḥ jñāne adhyakṣam abhilāpa grahaṇa īkṣate utpannam anumāna vṛtti vyapadiśyate rahitam cakṣuṣā sarva parokṣa sākṣātkāri viṣayasya lakṣaṇam bāhya arthasya ātmakam saha ālocana pramāṇam indriyāt anuvidhāyi artheṣu kāraṇam gṛhyate grāhyam vikalpasya paścāt vyāpāraḥ yogya anirdeśyam andha akṣaja bāhye gṛhṇāti vyāpārāt sākṣātkaraṇa anantara sarvam pravartate sarvathā dvi cākṣuṣam samanantara yuktam sukha saṃsarga vṛtteḥ prati mānasasya sāmarthyam avikalpa smārtaḥ antam mānasaḥ vijñānena ābhāsam tasmin smārta pravṛttam udbhavam anapekṣa catuṣṭaya padena anyathā nirvikalpasya pratyakṣatām sahakāri śrotra yojana avabhāsi jasya mātra apratyakṣaḥ atīndriyam prathama vijñānasya buddhau vikalpena vikalpakaḥ añjana grāhya sādhanaḥ kapittha aparokṣam ityādinā asmad dhiyaḥ sāmarthya smārtam āhuḥ viśeṣaḥ pratyaya sambandha sannihita gocaram ābham vikalpam anubhūyate viśeṣaṇam vṛttiḥ indriyayoḥ vikalpakasya vyavasāyam sahakāriṇā upahata darśanāt bhrānti nirvikalpa smṛtvā jāti pratyeti vyavasāye lakṣaṇa taimiram apekṣam atīndriya bāhyeṣu upajāyate surabhi janitam anuvyavasāyam viṣayeṇa akṣāṇām akṣāṇi akṣaḥ anumānikam utpadyamānam utpattau sahakārī dṛṣṭam je anvaya upaghāta pratyakṣā apekṣā prāk kurute sannipāta saṅketa asat avikalpanāt nimīlita vyāpāram aindriyam pratyātma m abhipretam jāḥ vijñāne vikalpane prasaṅgaḥ viṣayīkriyate vyavasāyasya vikalpake ābhāsā anuvidhānāt janmanaḥ bhinna prativiṣayam pratigatam bālānām grahaṇena saṃvedanam vi indriyā grahaṇe smaraṇam jāyate grāhī ādinā granthaḥ vartate agrahaṇam avikalpya īkṣeta timiram anobhyām avikalpakāḥ kalpanāyāḥ pratyakṣāt adhīna grāhyā vyatirekābhyām atīta cakṣuṣaḥ kathaṅ vicāraka gocare pravṛtta prasaṅgāt aviṣaya vyavadhāna prastāvaḥ śabdaḥ pratyayaḥ vyavahitaḥ avasīyate kevalam jāyante gṛhītvā dvividhaḥ vācyam asādhāraṇam kṣamam dhiyām anya sandhānam vikalpāḥ sambaddha prathamam manyate niścayaḥ grahaṇāt asādhāraṇena badhira jñānānām viśeṣyayoḥ viśeṣaṇasya anakṣaja dhīvat nikarṣāt ākāram
27	arthaḥ anyaḥ viśeṣaḥ puruṣaḥ viṣayaḥ dharmaḥ yam uktaḥ svayam paśyati ādiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ ātmā artham nāma enam ekaḥ anyena rūpaḥ vyatiriktaḥ doṣaḥ san pratyayaḥ idānīm aham pratipadyate arthasya siddhaḥ bhūtaḥ nava aparaḥ lakṣaṇaḥ gataḥ mayā avagamyate sarvaḥ yasmin anyasya tasmin samarthaḥ āśrayaḥ kena jānāti dṛśyate kasya itaraḥ svabhāvaḥ kṛtaḥ paraḥ mātram ātmakaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ kasyacid kaścana ātmānam yuktaḥ praiṣa gamyate śakyam prāptaḥ pūrvakaḥ vaktum viparītaḥ rahitaḥ anya imam saṃbandhaḥ tattvam karoti loke pravartate nyāyaḥ tvayā cetayate śakyate śabdaḥ kambalaḥ adhyavasyati āśritaḥ param upalabhyate upalabhāmahe arthe viśeṣam manyate arhati eṣaḥ satyam bhavān upalabhyamānaḥ aparādhaḥ buddhau sannihitaḥ bāhyaḥ yādṛśaḥ brūyāt tādṛśaḥ vidyamānaḥ praiṣaḥ itas sataḥ gamyaḥ avaśyam naḥ vācyaḥ dvitīyaḥ jñāyate āhuḥ kambala avyatiriktaḥ śabdasya icchati sambandhī prakāraḥ puruṣam ādikaḥ āpadyate praśnaḥ apekṣaḥ vayam prayujyate upalabhate vai tava deśe śakyaḥ anyam kutaścid antargataḥ upāttaḥ pratipadyamānaḥ laukikaḥ draṣṭā prayuṅkte bhavitum asan darśanam pratyayam asmin kiṃcana svāmī samādhiḥ avadhāryate brāhmaṇam pūrvaḥ deśaḥ vyavahāraḥ nityaḥ samānaḥ bravīmi vikalpaḥ kevalam tāvatā anupapanna anubhavati tathābhūtaḥ gṛhītaḥ upadiśyate naṣṭaḥ bhavatā vibhajya kenacid kañcid anyāni puruṣa upari aparedyus ātmīyaḥ upajāyate ceṣṭate māṇavakaḥ saṃpratyayaḥ sidhyati abhihitaḥ abhidhīyate adhyāropya ātmanā bhāgaḥ udara sthitaḥ dṛṣṭvā adrākṣam arthāt ātmīyam vacanasya mārgaḥ pramāṇaiḥ rāja viśiṣyate dvividhaḥ abhisambandhaḥ antaraḥ anyasmin vivakṣitaḥ upalabhya avagacchāmaḥ sambadhyate āhosvit dharmam madhyama kumbham bhavan lakṣyate yad atikrāntaḥ upapannam arthānām tādṛśam vyapadiśati prathamaḥ asmān prati asati aduṣṭaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ tasmai īpsā vacanīyaḥ vibhāgaḥ āsīt anyedyus nivartitaḥ praiṣya śreyān kurvan prabhṛti sambandhinam arthī kṛtā etau vyapadiśyate jāyamānaḥ kambalāḥ budhyate manāḥ āśrayam ubhayam dveṣṭi niṣedhanam mūḍhaḥ parīkṣyate praśna abhyupagataḥ anye pitā apramāṇakaḥ saṃbandhāt cakāsti putrasya kalpaḥ ādinā prasiddham parityajya kumbhasya navaḥ etasmāt icchet avagacchati smarati avatiṣṭhate upalakṣitaḥ samayena jñātvā pūrvedyus yāvān kiṃkṛtaḥ āyata janiṣyate preṣyate saṃyunakti śrotuḥ eṣitavyaḥ prasiddhaḥ tadvat dahyate uktasya ajānānaḥ anurodhī me padārthasya vyavahāre kaṃcid abhiprāyaḥ yau putraḥ yajñadattaḥ ajñāsīt anyasmai avināśī vyāmohe asmākam sādhanaḥ anavadyam mayam spṛśāmi kumbhaḥ vidyamāne prakāreṇa upādadānaḥ yajñāyudhī
28	phalam svarga phala yajeta kāmaḥ karma darśa yāgaḥ pradhāna guṇa yāga aṅga svargaḥ arthaḥ aṅgam paśu agnihotram juhoti apūrvam kratu puruṣa śrūyate kāmasya yāgena juhuyāt karmaṇaḥ yāgasya pradhānam dravya yāgam pūrṇamāsābhyām dravyam gamyate pūrṇamāsa śeṣa śākhā artham agnihotra kartavyatā apūrva prati kuryāt kāla phalavat yajati kāma kartavya bhāvaḥ itikartavya svargam kriyate prītiḥ avagamyate tṛtīyā karmaṇi antare phalena saṃbandhaḥ bhūtam aṅgāni yāge vidhīyate vrīhi prīti paurṇamāsyām nāmadheyam kartavyaḥ bhāvayet uta prokṣaṇa dadāti karmāṇi dvitīyā devatā prādhānyam śabdaḥ codanā brahmavarcasa kartavyam pūrṇamāsau amāvāsyāyām apūrvasya kṛtvā dharmāḥ vidhiḥ phale phalasya prayāja yajiḥ prayoga śrutiḥ putra yaji brūmaḥ tāni vājapeyena citra arthāni prāptam sāṅgam upakāraḥ jit pradhānāni prayogaḥ puruṣaḥ prayojanam mātram yāvajjīvam guṇaḥ vidhi arthāḥ vaidikī bhūta puruṣasya bhūtaḥ śeṣāṇām aihika bhāgi svārājya āgneya prayoge sadyas viśva sve abhisaṃbandhaḥ somena codyate itikartavyatā kāle bhaviṣyati dṛṣṭa karmaṇoḥ vacanāni vṛṣṭi saṃbandhāt adṛṣṭam dohanena dṛṣṭam nāmadheya svarge grāma dharmaḥ antaram vidhyantaḥ śruti kālaḥ anyat karmaṇām paśavaḥ tasmin amāvāsyām udbhida niyogataḥ adṛṣṭa puruṣam evaṃjātīyakam pakṣe laukikaḥ śabdena śrūyante kāmāya prāpte yāni śaknoti kāmena doṣaḥ citrayā juhūḥ prastarasya śākhayā śrutam vihitam bhūtāḥ akarma vacana viguṇam eṣām evamādīni niyamaḥ juhotiḥ codanāyām arthinaḥ adhikriyate phalāni loke arthi pratihomaḥ yajeḥ homāḥ bhavanti niṣpatteḥ sarva laukikī bhavya prajāpati śruteḥ pratyakṣaḥ pūrvaḥ kriyā bhūtā upadeśaḥ iṣṭvā sāyam yāvat kṛṣi vacanaḥ prayāje prayuktāḥ cayanena cikīrṣyate prastare viśvajitā upadiśyate parṇa aṅge evamādi paurṇamāsīm hotavyam citrā amāvāsyā ādibhiḥ sarvam abhyupāyaḥ abhinirvartayitum dāsyati bhāva abhyāsaḥ saurya kalpyam yajate vrīhīn bhūtāni vaiśyasya śākhāyām upasaṃhartum phalānām abhinirvartya māsam sauryam vai prātar nirvapet homaḥ upakuryāt upakaroti śakyate abhinirvartayet apūrvayoḥ viprayoge paurṇamāsī saṃskāreṣu siddham svargasya arthe artha nidhanam pradhānataḥ yāgāt kiṃcid sama kāmayate prokṣati pratyartham vartate bhāvam śruta saṃjñakam dvitīya dadhnā guṇam iṣṭyā ślokam vijñāyate jyotiṣṭomena dadyāt hīḥ nimitte agnihotrāt praṇayet saṃpattiḥ upakārakam nyāyyam śeṣaḥ dhi bhavitum ubhayam coditam mātre saṃstutiḥ śrutena nirdiśyate saṃskāraḥ saṃdehaḥ ādīni bṛhaspati eṣaḥ anantaram vidhayaḥ agnihotrasya kalpyaḥ
29	anupalabdhiḥ abhāva upalabdhi upalabdhiḥ anupalabdhi anupalabdheḥ lakṣaṇa abhāvaḥ upalambha anupalambhaḥ svabhāva dṛśya upalambhaḥ upalabhyate anupalambha viruddha vyavahāra asat śīta siddhiḥ anya anupalabdhyā anupalambhāt pratiṣedha anupalabdhau bhāva vyāpaka prāptasya yogya upalambhāt sādhyate abhāvāt pratiṣedhaḥ hetuḥ viṣaya abhāvam yā vyavahāraḥ upalabdheḥ āvaraṇa prakāra prāpta kārya adṛśya prasajya hetu vivikta sidhyati prayogaḥ abhāvasya sat niṣedhaḥ paryudāsa abhāve upalambhasya virodhaḥ siddhaḥ sattā sādhayati jñāna kāraṇa tasyāḥ uktā anupalambhena nivṛttiḥ upalabdhau anyasya upalabhyamāna upalabdhyā upalabhya vyavahāram sparśaḥ upalabhe anupalambhe vyavahārasya pratiṣedhyasya dhruva pratyakṣa anupalambhanam sādhane antara asattā niṣedhe anupalambhasya anupalabdhim pramāṇa uktaḥ antarasya satyām virodha viparyaye roma bhāve upalambhe anyeṣu lakṣaṇaḥ dṛśyasya sādhanam asiddhiḥ vastu prayujyate anyatra dṛśyaḥ kāraṇasya ayogāt anyā bādhāyāḥ siddhau viṣayaḥ paryudāsaḥ sarvatra ātmaka niścaya deśa tādātmya sādhanī san sādhayet bhāvāt pratiṣedhasya yogyatāyāḥ rūpa niścayaḥ niṣedhya darśana gatiḥ prāptam hetoḥ asan hetau asiddheḥ viruddhasya harṣa svabhāvaḥ vyāpakayoḥ āvaraṇam saha pradeśa anavasthā pratiṣedhya jñeya sattvam vastuni parihāra svayam viṣayasya kevalam nimitta sādhye vṛttyā siddheḥ vyāpta anupalabhya nañaḥ ghaṭa kācid asyāḥ kasmāt satsu nāstitvam sādhikā viruddham upalabhyasya anupalabdhī nivṛtti abhāvena dṛśye siddhim vyāpya trividha avikala nivṛttyā apratipattiḥ siddhi gamikā santi vyāpakasya pratipattṛ sataḥ anupalabdhitaḥ adṛśye lakṣaṇā pradeśaḥ arthānām anavasthāna salila anupalabhyamānam agneḥ upalabhyamānasya rūpam sthita atyanta asattvam anupalambham pramāṇena rūpā prāptiḥ ghaṭaḥ dhūmāt prasidhyati romaharṣa adṛśyasya anupalambhataḥ pratiṣedhe prayoga yāthātmya siddhā upalambham darśayitum nivṛtteḥ abhimatasya mātram sattayā yukta siddhyā bhāvaḥ pratyakṣaḥ asattva anupalabhyamāna mātra pradeśe pratipatti anupalambhanāt stha viruddhaḥ etena pratiṣedhyāt draṣṭavyam vidhi phalā piśāca sāmarthyāt siddha sāmarthyāni vyavahāre anupalabdhyoḥ viṣaye virodhi pratibandha ekasya an upalabdhim pramāṇam prasaṅgāt eka smāryate vyavahārān kāle avaśyam prāpteṣu upalabhaḥ dṛśyam anyathā sadbhāva paraḥ astita upalabhyamāne prakārā anyaḥ svabhāvayoḥ veditavyā virodhasya prayogataḥ deśe sambhavāt sarva pṛthak aniścaya kāraṇāni sākalyam piśācaḥ anupalabdhaḥ trividhaḥ prabheda sadbhāvāt tuṣāra prakāraḥ sādhanāt aprasādhakaḥ upalabdhyoḥ bhāvayoḥ caturvidhā vyavahārāya viruddhayoḥ sannihita vahneḥ yāvān adṛśyaḥ jñātṛ niṣedha bādhana itara sākṣāt pratyakṣataḥ virodhāt kenacid yogyatā eṣā traya upalabhyeta
30	cit kva iṣyate vastu pratīyate matiḥ dhīḥ śabda vinā naḥ buddhiḥ kiñ yā prasajyate vācya kalpanā gamyate arthe vidyate eṣā prati asādhāraṇa kena yujyate pūrva kalpyate yogya prāk mātra bhinna buddhi cana ṛte iṣṭam śakti bhedaḥ kathan jāyate sarva candra kaiḥ ke vṛttiḥ dhruvam mṛṣā dṛśyate vāryate anya kathyate apohya anyaḥ avastu siddha abhāve tulya śaktiḥ apoha kasya eṣām sampratīyate sambandhaḥ taiḥ dhi abhāvataḥ nityam vastuni rūpeṇa sambandha tādṛśī śakta siddham anyat ādibhiḥ tava anyathā aṃśa tadvat cetasām niṣedhaḥ sarveṣām artha sambhavaḥ samam upajāyate bādhaḥ nu pratyakṣa dṛṣṭa śaśini varjanāt asmin nāma pūrvam virudhyate siddhe yādṛśī caitra mama loka bhedena kalpane bhedataḥ anyaiḥ śābda apohaḥ asyāḥ kadā prakalpyate vana bhaviṣyati upayujyate sarvaḥ kalpitam śabdayoḥ tulyam yāvat vādinām vaḥ saṅgatiḥ dvayam siddhā diśā vācyam vadet upapadyate adhīna nirākriyā sadbhāvaḥ nirūpyate yogyam mātreṇa uktā śūnya sambandhe puṃsām nirālambana gamyatām rūpam adṛṣṭa ātmā asambhavaḥ sidhyati avakalpate apohyam sthite vaktum prāc anumānataḥ apohena apramāṇa anayā akṣa go bodhakam prakalpate ātmanā vācyaḥ yogyatā vastunaḥ anyā duṣyati tādṛś etasya īdṛśī sāmānya aśakti tāyām saṃśrayam pratyabhijñānam bādhyate prasiddha sthitaḥ sarvam sat gṛhyate sthitiḥ nāśi sthitam sadā sādhyate anyonya kā dhiyā vijñānam tāvatā śruteḥ jñāte doṣaḥ yuktiḥ sarvathā sarveṣu sannidhi jāti arthataḥ abhidheya kalpayet ittham vijñāte abravīt paścāt ajñānam gamya bādhanam varṇeṣu sarvatra paraiḥ kevalasya anyatra pratirundhānaḥ abhidhīyate prasiddhitaḥ bhidyate bhāvinī pracakṣate vacaḥ yādṛś vācyā varṇyate sidhyet bodhanam avatiṣṭhate antaraiḥ apohasya aṃśaḥ sāmānyāt tvataḥ rūpataḥ aṅga iṣṭā buddhīnām nirālambanatā matim udāhṛtam lakṣayet sarvaiḥ viruddha asādhāraṇam niṣedha śabdaiḥ nitya aśakta anumā śūnyatā sarvasya velāyām eka kīrtyate varjitam abhidhāsyate ajñāte vāci teṣu yadvat vṛkṣa āhuḥ parīkṣyatām sphuṭam druta dṛṣṭam upagame buddhau pareṣām dvayoḥ upalambhanam pūrvatra santam nirūpaṇam avagamyate buddhyā svarūpataḥ kalpanam tvayā hetukam apodyate nirūpitam nna niṣedhāt kṛtaḥ etad niyamyate ajñāna kīdṛś agaḥ anivāraṇam bodhaḥ sādhayiṣyate eteṣām dṛṣṭāntaḥ anveti śaśinaḥ naṣṭe vyabhicāritā ucyeta bādhanāt vādibhiḥ aviśeṣeṇa buddheḥ samā ekā vṛtteḥ
31	sāmānyam vyakti sāmānya jāti go sāmānyasya viśeṣa vyaktiḥ jātiḥ vyakteḥ pratyaya jāteḥ viśeṣaḥ ākṛti vyaktau anugata vyaktīnām anuvṛtti gauḥ vyāvṛtti saṃsthāna sāmānye vyaktayaḥ samāna eka vyāvṛtta sarva vyaktiṣu piṇḍa ākṛtiḥ śabda buddhiḥ vyāvṛttiḥ sāmānyena pratyayaḥ vyañjaka jātau śābaleya aśva sarvatra viśeṣeṣu viśeṣāṇām antare anugama gavā jātim vyaktim śāvaleya sāmānyāt vartate ākṛteḥ iṣyate bhede jātīnām vyaktam jātayaḥ abhāvāt anugatam viśeṣāḥ vṛtti vyakta anugamaḥ pācaka mātra āśraya viśeṣe viśeṣasya pratīyate anuvṛttiḥ hetu anya suvarṇa yogāt vṛttiḥ svarūpa piṇḍe gatam vinā viśeṣayoḥ vyaktyā anyatra pratyayasya prativyakti rūpa viśeṣam padārthaḥ teṣu nimittā yā svarūpam buddhi abhāve abhinna tāsām antaram vyaṅgya kriyā bāhuleya vyaṅgyam tāsu pratītiḥ abhinnam pratipiṇḍam rūpam kasmāt bhinneṣu antara vāha anyā sattā tulya piṇḍeṣu śakyam ākāra tadvān ākṛtim yogaḥ vyāvṛtteḥ avayava antareṇa viśeṣavatā upalakṣaṇam anyena vyajyate vyaktyoḥ gatiḥ darśanāt niyata bhedāt tadvat sambadhyate tasyāḥ śukla pratīti vyaktaḥ gām sambhavati pratyabhijñānam ākṛtau anuyāyi khaṇḍa viśiṣṭeṣu anuvṛtta sāmānyeṣu antarāt viśeṣāt yayā ekam ananvayāt viṣaya apacaya sāmānyāni tadvatoḥ saṃsthānam vyaktibhyaḥ brāhmaṇa jātyā nibandhanam samānāḥ vyaktī vilakṣaṇaḥ vartamānam anuvṛtteḥ jātitaḥ atyanta upalakṣaṇa anvayi anyat viśeṣeṇa vyatirekeṇa svatas anavasthānāt dṛṣṭā vastu sādhāraṇa vyatiriktam viśeṣau yoga karkā hetuḥ prasaṅgataḥ avamarśaḥ atad ekasyām vedya anekatra parasparam vācya adarśanāt sambandhāt mahā sāmāni tāḥ antareṣu abhedāt lakṣaṇam viśiṣṭa asāmānya piṇḍānām vyaktibhiḥ asambhavāt doha nibandhanā bhinna abhivyaktiḥ asiddham jātya vyañjikā sarvathā tulye ādhāreṣu antya yuktam nimittam sāmānyavataḥ piṇḍasya nimittaḥ avāntara saṃpratīyate jātimat aśakya padārtha viṣaye antarālam piṇḍena vyañjakaḥ āsīt ānantyāt prasaṅgaḥ varga gāvaḥ naḥ sajātīya sambandhi bhinnam keṣucid viśinaṣṭi gavake śābaleyaḥ sthitam nitya aṃśa viśiṣṭānām ghaṭa adṛṣṭe upalakṣitam vyaktitaḥ prasaṅga abhede etena bhinnā viśeṣebhyaḥ tādātmyam vyāvṛttī āśrayaḥ arhati saṅkara bhedeṣu prāṇi viśiṣyate kathañcana abhidhāne kaṭaka tadvataḥ sāsnādi ānantye ekabuddhi sāmyāt bhavitum adbhutam aho nirviśeṣam sāmānyayoḥ vyasana jñāna śūnye grahaṇe pratyabhijñānāt gata viśeṣitam citam deśe śabdāt viśeṣābhyām ātmaka gamanāt abhivyaktam ātmakeṣu upajāyamānena vyāvṛttam viśeṣaṇa anvayāt varṇa pratyekam goḥ darśane rucaka ekā mṛd brāhmaṇaḥ
32	jñānam artha rajata jñānasya jñāna candra rajatam ālambana ālambanam bhrānta udaka pratibhāti khyātiḥ viparīta jñāne bhrāntam viṣaya śuktikā bhrānti kalpanā bhrāntiḥ bādhaka asat prasaṅgāt deśa viṣayam ākāra anyathā nirviṣaya dvi udakam avisaṃvādi jala abhrānta atīta anya avyabhicāri ayuktam ākāraḥ prāpaka nirviṣayam samyak abhra avidyamāna grāhi anurodhena viparyayaḥ ākāreṇa abhāvāt antara vijñānasya arthasya jñānena bādhā śuktau keśoṇḍuka keśa pratīyamāna vibhramaḥ śuktikāyām viveka vijñānam jñānānām marīci bhramaḥ pratibhāsanāt kāla pratibhāsaḥ sarva pratibhāsa śukti rajatasya pravṛtti anāgata prāptiḥ nirālambanam satta kriyā vyabhicāri pūrva mithyājñānam prāptyā sādṛśya prāpnoti bādhyate mithyātvam anyat pratibhāsā ayathārtha bādhakam jñāneṣu timira prāpti sāmarthyena mithyā toya asambhavāt avabhāsate viparyaya asatya asattvam smṛti apratibhāsanāt gṛhīti pīta anyatra akhyātiḥ khyātau anta pratītiḥ doṣāt nimitta viṣayaḥ ātma bāhya saṃvṛti bādhya satya uttara jñānāt pratibhāsi cakṣuḥ bādha prāpakam anālambanam khyāti ubhayoḥ saṃvādaḥ pratibhāsāt yuktam bhrāntau gṛhīta virodhaḥ vijñāna prasaṅgaḥ tikta vyavahāra avisaṃvādaḥ jñānayoḥ abhyupagame sambhavati rūpa avabhāta śuktiḥ abhrāntam vidyamāna upapadyate mātra alaukika bhrānteḥ abhyupagamāt bhrāntasya atasmin saṃvidaḥ vyabhicārāt rūpā utpāditam nīla antareṇa aviśeṣe bhāvi utpanna kasyacid abādhyamāna pratīyate arthinaḥ vijñāne śaṅkha ākārā utpannam marīcayaḥ śukteḥ ālamba atiprasaṅgāt ayogāt rahita vartamāna ākāram bhūta avidyamānam pramāṇa alaukikam sattā upakāraka ākārasya calana asattvāt ajanakasya tāttvika āropyate salila anyasya avivekaḥ avabhāsa ajanaka adhyavasāyasya utpatteḥ vāstava vyabhicāritā khyāteḥ taimirikasya toyam vibhinna nihita kena antare avidyamānaḥ saṃvedanasya anupapatteḥ virodhāt janitam samāna sāmarthyāt laukika āpadyate pāramparyeṇa avidyamānasya pratyaya aṃśa anabhyupagamāt janakam mithyātva vipra abhāva aspaṣṭa cakṣuṣā sarvam ja abhyupagantavyam viṣayasya rūpeṇa pradarśitam tādātmya eke anumeya abhāve pradarśaka doṣa vidyamānam avabhāti sarvatra pratyaye ati avabhāsi avasthita ālambanasya upapattiḥ rūpam bhrāntitaḥ saṃvittīnām pratibhāsate kālam nimittāt evamādi viśeṣāt apahāra agraha janita aviśeṣāt sat vyavahārasya āyātam akṣaja samānam antam abhāvaḥ prāpyate vaśāt arka kṣaṇika bhrama jñāpyate utpādya marīciṣu nirākariṣyamāṇa upārūḍham upalabhyate artham upalambhāt agrahaṇāt anarthakam yogi grāhiṇī mātram arthaḥ vibhramam paricchidya apramāṇa udakasya apahāraḥ grāhiṇaḥ puras pratibhāsasya kiṃcid yujyate pratyakṣam ākāre gṛhyate bādhakena sambhavāt
33	anvaya vyatireka vyatirekaḥ prāṇa nivṛttiḥ anvayaḥ abhāve abhāvaḥ abhāva hetoḥ nivṛtti vipakṣe hetuḥ mātreṇa bhāva jīvat vyāvṛttiḥ niścayaḥ kevala vipakṣāt ātma vyatirekī vyatirekayoḥ sidhyati
