nivṛttau vyatirekau adarśana vipakṣa siddhiḥ vyatirekasya asiddheḥ hetu vyatirekābhyām sandigdha gatiḥ pakṣāt gamakaḥ sattvam vyāvṛtteḥ ādiḥ gamaka niścita śrāvaṇa vyāvṛtti asati ātmā vyatirekiṇaḥ anvayī abhāvāt ghaṭa bhāvaḥ pratibandha ātmaka mukhena sarvatra pakṣe abhāvam vyatirekam vyatireki nivṛtteḥ anvayasya vyāptiḥ ātmanaḥ vaktṛ sādhya abhāvena dvayoḥ asataḥ sarva pratibandhaḥ darśana vyatireke śeṣavat anyathā gamayati vyabhicāri nivṛttyā vastu nairātmya vyāvṛttyā abhāvasya tādātmya siddhaḥ vacana avi aprāṇa sandigdhaḥ nirātmakam prasaṅgāt bhāve mātrāt nivṛttim vidhi pratiṣedha niyama śarīre pakṣa pakṣaḥ ekasya sandehāt astitā virodha sattva vyāptyā anayoḥ vyabhicāra avyabhicāraḥ vaidharmya adarśanāt śarīram ātmakam anvayena vyatirekāt sandigdham sādhana pratibandhe ādimattva niyamena nairātmyam vyabhicāraḥ tasmin ācāryeṇa asatsu sādhanam adṛṣṭi adarśane ayogāt uktaḥ sādhye atiprasaṅgāt vṛttiḥ darśanāt pratīyate abhāvayoḥ pramāṇa niṣedhaḥ asiddhau pratiṣedhaḥ asattvam sarvaḥ anyatra vacanāt sandeha ekatra niścitaḥ saṃśayāt asat avyatirekaḥ anvayinaḥ vṛtteḥ vṛtti virodhaḥ tābhyām asiddhā vyāvṛttam sambhavāt anvayam avīta siddham mātra avaśyam sandigdhā sattā antareṇa vyatirekitā dvitīyam bahulam sādhanasya pratiṣedham asādhyāt saha sambhavati sandehe adṛṣṭeḥ tau vipakṣaḥ vyāvṛttaḥ tṛtīyam sarvasya niṣidhyate anvayi gamyate iṣyate anaikāntikaḥ darśane abhicārāt tathāvidhasya saṃśayaḥ vastunaḥ sandehaḥ asambhavāt saṃdeha vipakṣeṇa vi vaktā anupalambhāt ubhaya asiddhiḥ sattvasya prāptā nairātmyena nibandhanam vyāpti mātrasya siddheḥ sattāyām aparasya niścaya sambhavaḥ niyata antarīyaka aniścayāt niyame avyabhicāritā sāmarthyāt siddhā vipakṣayoḥ kiñca yā aikāntika gamakam ākṣipati aprameya naḥ bhāj niṣedha lekhya avirodhāt eṣṭavyaḥ avipakṣa kṛtam nāma darśanīyaḥ vṛttyā ādimattvasya gamayet nirātmaka ekāntena viparyaya viśeṣe ātmakāt vyatiricyate agamaka san avyāvṛttiḥ nairātmyāt ekānta vidhānam vyatirekeṇa pratiṣedhena apratibandhāt apratipatteḥ abhāvau avinā sidhyet sādhyena vinivarttanam siddhe adarśanam nivarttaka niścaye asattva anaikāntika niyamaḥ avyatireke adarśanābhyām vacanam abhāvābhyām nyāyaḥ vyāpaka niścayam iṣṭā ākṣipyate vidhiḥ sarvatas putra vyāpinaḥ aparaḥ anuvidhāyi śābdaḥ etad ekena niścite pakṣāsa gateḥ sambhavat nañarthaḥ mūka vyāvṛttim antarīyakaḥ dharmiṇi vyāpteḥ pakṣīkṛta ātmani kāraṇāt virodhasya anugama ādimattvāt kevalam adṛṣṭau
34	sādhya vyāpti vyāpya vyāpaka abhāva pakṣa vṛtti vahni upādhiḥ vyāptiḥ dhūma dharma vyabhicāra adhikaraṇa avyāpaka sādhana anumiti upādhi pratiyogi pakṣe vācyam vyartha vyāpakam pṛthivī sat anumitiḥ abhāvāt vyatireki janya vinā viśeṣaṇa bādha vyāpteḥ atyanta avyāpya bahis anumāna dūṣaka sādhaka anyonya daśāyām vipakṣa mātra upādheḥ abhāvaḥ avacchinna hetu vyāpyam anyathā pratipakṣa itara śarīra vyabhicāri niṣṭhā tvayoḥ siddhiḥ ati jñāna vyabhicāraḥ tarka āpatteḥ sidhyati ubhaya asiddhiḥ samāna virodhi atirikta upajīvya vahniḥ anumāne kevala asādhaka grāhaka abhāvena hetvābhāsa sādhyam bādhaḥ dhūme anyatara viraha bala pratibandhaka āśraya sattva anantaram pratyeka parvata sahacāra viruddha anumitau vyatireka adhikaraṇam kartṛka jīvana abhāvavat adhika sandigdha aprayojaka hetoḥ viśeṣa anya vādi apratiyogi saṃśaya gṛha siddhi prakṛta asiddhi nyūna virodha jala vyāvṛtta kartṛ anukūla niyama anaupādhika viśiṣṭa jñānam prameya aṣṭa sakala anaikāntika avṛtti bhāva parāmarśa vahneḥ vyāptim vyāpakaḥ samartha sattvāt prasaṅgāt sāmānādhikaraṇyam siddhau virahaḥ vyāpyaḥ siddha prakāraka doṣa bādhāt vahnau tāvacchedaka niścaya dhūmavat prasiddham vahnimat tvañca niścayāt parāmarśaḥ sādhye yāvat aprasiddheḥ avyāptiḥ abhāvavati avacchedakam anumiteḥ sādhane dhūmavān doṣaḥ saha dūṣaṇa parvate siddheḥ grahaḥ niścaye an graha ābhāsa dvārā ādhāyaka sambandha hetau prabhava ārdra anye dūṣaṇam balena anvayi siṣā bādhakena ajñāne balāt parvatīya uccheda tulya vyatirekasya vyadhikaraṇa viṣaya śyāma bādhaka niyamāt vyāptau vyatirekaḥ parāmarśasya niścayaḥ vivāda nirupādhi tattvam jñānāt aprasiddhyā bādhe jñāne bhūyas ubhayatra vyabhicārāt anumānāt prayojakam asiddhau upādhau etena ta anvayini rūpavat sāmāna ekatra māna bahissattva prakārakaḥ tākaḥ aprasiddhau avacchedaka anupādhi ādāya antaram sādhāraṇa aprasiddhiḥ asādhāraṇa vahnimān samam dhūmaḥ bādhakam saṃyoga viśiṣṭasya śūnya pratirodhaḥ vyāpyasya bhaṅga balam ādhāra prayojaka satya pramiti jīvī pratipakṣe balavat yogyā tarkasya prasiddha asādha niṣṭha sādhāraṇam mātrasya vyatirekī avyāpakaḥ abhimata gatyā vyatirekiṇā āvaśyaka vyāpyate bādhita saṃśayaḥ avyāpakam viśeṣaṇam dravya sahakāri etad sāmānādhikaraṇya lāghava sāmānyatas unnāyaka jñānasya abhāvasya tulyam vyatireke avyāvartaka saṃśayāt janaka grahāt grāhakasya pramātu sattve vyāpakasya avacchidyate tantram tarkaḥ pratyakṣa ghaṭaḥ atirikte kartṛkatva manasā dhūmasya nirastam trayodaśa tvā apāstam sādhyayoḥ vyabhicāre ajñānāt lakṣaṇe pratiyogī pratyekam
35	anvaya pada śakti artha anvayaḥ anvita śaktiḥ lakṣaṇā vinā sādhu padārtha vākya padasya bodhaka vibhakti padāt pade prayoga bodha abhāvāt padam śakya ityādau bodhaḥ rūḍhi tātparya vācyam tīra anyathā itara lakṣaṇa gaṅgā paṅkaja tātparyam śaktyā saṅkhyā dhīḥ padānām upasthitiḥ padma lakṣaṇayā anvaye avayava vṛtti artham lāghavāt arthasya padena anvayāt yogya śaktim prathamam ākāṅkṣā niyamataḥ eka mukhya anya upasthiti upasthitau dhava vyutpatteḥ paramparayā evañca padārthe upasthite kumude prayogaḥ śābda śakta yoga asādhu gauravāt śakteḥ vākye tātparyya prathama sambhavati sambandhi upasthita rūḍhiḥ bodhe yogyatā ānayā kalpanam paratvam prakaraṇa gata kiñca sambhavāt dvi upasthāpaka ayogya anubhāvaka mātra karma prakṛti arthe kalpyate pratyekam padmam vṛttyā nānā bodhāt ādinā labhya kārya vastutas vācya paratve dvitīya apūrva śakyā upasthiteḥ smārita anupapattiḥ gaṅgāyām tīre sādhuḥ upapatteḥ tātparyāt ānayana smṛti bodhyate āpatteḥ kalpayati vyavahārāt ākāṅkṣa lakṣye niyata kriyā anurodhāt sāhitya abhidhāna stha grahaḥ sahita dvaya vācaka mātre bodhayati jñātāt bodhasya upapādaka samudāya viśeṣe sambandhena ucchedaḥ bahu śaktau lakṣaṇāyām vibhaktyā anuśāsana anuśāsanāt niṣāda abhidhāyaka kāryatva upalakṣaṇa grāma anupapattyā dhātu kumuda āpattiḥ khadira gauravam prayogasya vyabhicārāt ṣaṣṭhī viśeṣa sāhityam dvāram rūḍhyā padārthasya śabda jñāpaka lākṣaṇika vākyasya adhyāhāraḥ ghoṣaḥ para ānayanam liṅaḥ maṇḍapa nikartṛ samabhivyāhṛta anvayam upasthitam svarūpa janita tava vibhaktiḥ anvayā prasaṅgāt lakṣaṇīya lakṣaṇāyāḥ samāsa pācaka sambandha vṛttim rāja vyākaraṇa aprayogāt kalpane anupapatti nyāyāt balāt ākāṅkṣāyām rūpeṇa anuśāsanam anyatra dhī gatam smṛta pūrva ānaya jñātasya padārthaḥ vyutpatti lakṣya pratyeka vyutpattiḥ paratva aneka ukte prayogāt śaktam gauṇala lākṣaṇikasya prāthamyāt tīrasya vibhakteḥ nyāyena ghoṣa sambhūya dharmaṇi puruṣam anyonya kalpanā niyamāt vāci dhātoḥ āt pratīteḥ sthāyi dhāna kalpanāt kañca māna tāt ajahatsva apabhraṃśe khadirau paceta samāsasya vilambita anupasthiteḥ aprayogaḥ śabdāt tulya dvandva pratipādya jñātam pūrvam anta arthayoḥ mukhye paṅka anye abhāvena upadarśita gāma vibhaktimat ekatra prātipadikā anvayasya paratvāt dvayasya praveśaya vṛttiḥ padayoḥ balavat anvitam anukūla sākṣāt upanīta vṛddha tvañca nadyāḥ samuccaye lābhāt arthaka gabhīra bahutva jñāne anvitaḥ upajīvya bhramāt nāma agre kalpanātaḥ samabhivyāhāra
36	artham arthaḥ sūtra prayojanam tantra prayojana nyāya śāstra artha siddhāntaḥ lakṣaṇam lakṣaṇa śāstram jijñāsā sūtram codanā dharma parīkṣā bhāṣya sarva veda pūrva anantaram uddeśaḥ abhidhānam pramāṇa vākya vyākhyānam abhyupagama kāraḥ viśeṣa kāreṇa vyākhyā mīmāṃsā uddeśa bhāṣyam śāstrasya grantha ācārya prasiddha sūtrāṇi upāya vidyā sūtreṇa sūtre prakaraṇa adhikaraṇa sāmānya pravṛttiḥ lakṣaṇaḥ prati śāstre padārtha prakaraṇasya kṛtā kāra kṛtam sūtreṣu dharmaḥ adhikṛtya adhyāhāra ānantarya mahā dharmam sūtrakāraḥ pūrvam kṛtaḥ saṃsthitiḥ ādīni anuvāda ācāryaḥ upadeśaḥ namaḥ prakaraṇam yam pradarśana parihāra vyākhyātam siddhānta uttara vibhāga ānantaryam samyak vicāra ityādinā vacanam namaskāra mātra aṅgam vidyāḥ parama ṛṣiṇā lakṣaṇāni sūtrakārasya tantram upayogi manda śabdena anurodhena śruta varṇyate vyutpādana param vākyāni vyākhyāyate śiṣya nirdeśaḥ vyācakṣate vyākhyāna vivakṣitam arthataḥ avadhāraṇa trividhā vistara vākyam granthaḥ bahu ānantarye uktāni yuktam vacana praṇamya grahaṇa vyutpādanam ācāryasya tāni abhidheya vyākhyāne vibhāgaḥ ṛṣiḥ saṃgrahaḥ abhidhānāt guru pṛthak asmāt gauravam kecid adhyayana darśitaḥ uktā vidyānām prakaraṇe saṅgrahaḥ pratijñātam padārthānām matam muniḥ granthasya prasiddhāni prāpta āśaṅkya bhagavataḥ su prathamam ebhiḥ abhidheyam nāma prayojanaḥ kartum bhagavān grahaṇena vistaraḥ adhyāye sūtrakāreṇa vṛtti kena āśrayaḥ viśeṣam uktaḥ parīkṣaṇam uktavān caturdaśa ittham śrī sūtrāṇām jñāpana abhidhāne padena bhagavat namaskāraḥ kariṣyate arthasya parisaṃkhyā aparīkṣita asmin satyam pada matvā loke arthāni ācāryaiḥ śeṣa abhyupagamaḥ ācāryeṇa śrotṛ anyathā śabda prathama praśnaḥ taiḥ vaktum niyamaḥ mūla darśayati vaktavyam uttaratra kimartham samāptaḥ anantara kriyate catvāri vivakṣāyām padārthāḥ alpa kārāḥ yatnaḥ vyākhyeyam ācakṣate pratitantra upadiṣṭaḥ vakṣyati lakṣaṇasya manyamānaḥ uddiśya sūtrasya yuktaḥ prākṛta yatna upadeśa pratijñānam sma śabdaḥ pratipadam prayojanasya niḥśreyasa pratipādayitum vidhīyate udāharaṇa ānvīkṣikī niṣprayojanam parisamāptiḥ parīkṣām tantre nyāyaḥ pratijñāya lakṣaṇena praṇītam uddiṣṭa upasaṃhāra sūtrakāra prasiddhā pūrvakam uktasya upeya saṃkṣepa siddhāntasya parijñāna ucyamānam vyutpattiḥ mīmāṃsāyām parīṣṭiḥ snānasya kāni tattva imam ārabhyate nāmnā kṛta anukta saṃjñā upadeśāt ākṣipati idānīm tantreṇa nivṛttiḥ abhidhānena ktvā caturthī vivakṣayā itaretara anuktam caturvidhaḥ punarukta draṣṭavyam upapattiḥ jana prādhānyam vyākaraṇam grahaṇam padam antar bhūtam codya ārambhe prayojanena ādibhiḥ athavā kasmāt uddiṣṭasya vārttikam
37	bhedaḥ bheda bhedāt bhedena bhede eka abheda bhinna abhedaḥ bhedam bhedasya bhinnam abhede ekam abhinna bhidyate rūpa vyavasthā bhinnaḥ pratibhāsa abhedāt buddhi ekaḥ vyavahāraḥ abhinnam ākāra jāti avāntara nānā abhedau vastu nibandhanaḥ nānātvam deśa parasparam kalpanā paraspara advaita abhinnaḥ bhidyante upādhi ekasmin viśeṣaḥ abhedam bhāvānām abhāvāt abhinnasya āśraya abhedena sarvam anyat śakti bhinnāḥ aikyam pratyabhijñānam pratyayaḥ kṛtaḥ prasaṅgāt bhinne viśeṣa abhedayoḥ aneka ekānta buddheḥ bhedānām avasthā dadhi bhinnasya abhinne ekatvam ananta sarvatra anayoḥ nibandhanam pratyabhijñā vastutas itaretara sphaṭika aviśeṣāt viṣaya abhedasya gakāra kathañcid nimittam sarva tulya svarūpa bhinneṣu aparaḥ siddhiḥ pratyaya viśeṣe bhedakaḥ antareṇa saṅkaraḥ kalpanāyām dṛṣṭaḥ vibhinna ekatva śakyate apara kena nānātve mātre rūpam prasaṅgaḥ itara abhedābhyām yuktaḥ kutaścid upapatteḥ nānātva buddhiḥ pratyekam pratibhāsaḥ golaka santāna svabhāva vyavahāra avabhāsaḥ uṣṭraḥ vivekena anyonya abhinnā viśeṣāt naḥ anupapatteḥ vastūnām vyavasthāpayati vādinaḥ ekatve ekasya bhedavatī ekatra vilakṣaṇa pratyabhijñāyate vyavatiṣṭhate ekatā asati paramārthataḥ mātra advaitam bahu tadvat viṣayayoḥ asat mukham prakāra antarāt upadhāna dārāḥ anyatra vāstavaḥ abhedataḥ āśritya sidhyet sarveṣām dhīra pratyavamarśasya avasthāḥ guḍa hetu viśva anekāntaḥ saṃsargāt dvaitam abhinnatā ātmakasya asambhavaḥ ānantyam sphaṭikaḥ pratibhāsā saṃkaraḥ avyatirekāt sparataḥ anupalakṣaṇāt bhedān bhedinī bhinnānām vailakṣaṇyam ātmānaḥ abhinnāḥ sāmyāt an bhinnau śaktiṣu satyam bhavatu ākārayoḥ sarvathā abhinnena parāmarśa jagat vyavasthitiḥ anekadhā avibhāgaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ sāmye bhinnayoḥ anupalakṣaṇe vibhinne grāhyam mate bhedaka nābheda ṛju anyatva avyatireke viruddham ayaḥ doṣāt dharmāṇām tebhyaḥ anyādṛśa bhedayoḥ avabhāsam bhedā payasaḥ parasparataḥ bhedakam anuvidhānāt matam sādṛśyāt ādibhyaḥ aspaṣṭa vyāvṛtta viśvasya anyathā lakṣaṇa yāvat nakṣatram pratyabhijñāna siddhā ādikām bhedikā nirbhāsa dṛśyate pratyayasya pravibhāgaḥ ādiḥ bhinnāt tattva aviśeṣe anugamāt vicitra paṭaḥ kuṇḍala anekam dvaita prakalpyate kṛpāṇa darśanāt adhyāsāt maṇeḥ pratyayam kalpaḥ yoge dve nibandhana ananya kalpitaḥ atyanta aikyāt rakta ārūḍhena tadvatoḥ nīla viruddha aikye parama vyavasthitaḥ anantaḥ vyāvṛttaḥ antarā anyāḥ bhidyete bhinnān tiṣyaḥ vivekinī anyonyam rūpāṇām ākārāṇām śuklaḥ darpaṇa setsyati traiguṇya buddhyoḥ jīvaḥ atiśayaḥ paraspareṇa śuddhasya pariṇāma siddheḥ abhedaka vivecayati vastuṣu antarebhyaḥ anātma kāriṇām aṃśayoḥ
38	abhāvaḥ abhāva bhāva ghaṭa abhāvasya viśeṣaṇa bhāvaḥ bhū ghaṭaḥ viśeṣya abhāve tala abhāvayoḥ gṛha viśeṣaṇam prāc abhāvena pratiyogi abhāvam viśiṣṭa rūpa abhāvāt bhāvasya pradeśa atyanta pradhvaṃsa kevala vastu abhāvau anya antara tale ghaṭasya bahis talam sambandhaḥ pramāṇa pratīti pratīyate antaram bhāve bhāvena svarūpa bhāvāt anyathā pañcaka sambandha gṛhe pratīteḥ ubhaya uttejaka vyavahāraḥ kevalaḥ vidyamāna anyonya pratītiḥ paṭa upalakṣaṇam pratiyoginaḥ ghaṭe tanmātra viśeṣyayoḥ viśeṣaṇe jīvataḥ sadbhāve adhikaraṇa caitra gṛham bahirbhāva caitrasya bhāvayoḥ daṇḍa mātram ekatra itaretara rūpaḥ pradeśaḥ vivikta kāle kaṇṭaka talasya viśeṣyam bahirbhāvam anyaḥ āsīt ghaṭāt siddheḥ viśeṣaḥ devadattasya jñānam viṣayi pratiyogī buddhi upalambhaka vastunaḥ prameya buddhiḥ caitraḥ pratibandhaka bahirbhāvaḥ mukhena daṇḍī bhāvam viṣaya samavāya prayuktaḥ devadatta viśeṣaṇasya itaretarābhāvaḥ prāgabhāvasya prāgabhāvaḥ tvad yogyā bahirbhāvasya ālambanam viśiṣṭam sambandhe tuccha anupapattiḥ anyat gehe pratiyogini prasaṅgāt aṃśaḥ pradeśasya ghaṭam sidhyati vyavahāra samaye anyatara anabhyupagamāt yuktam geha kāraṇam antarasya pratītau viśeṣye saha pratiṣedhya itaretarābhāva rūpe abhāvānām kalpyate ākhyam kaivalyam ajñānam bhaviṣyati sadbhāva saṃsṛṣṭa pratipatteḥ devadattaḥ liṅgam pratiṣedha viśiṣṭaḥ vyavacchedakam anutpatteḥ viśeṣaṇā asaṃsṛṣṭa āśrayam kevalam prāk vyāvṛttyā kīṭa aṃśasya astita pratiyoginam paratantra kevalasya paṭaḥ saṃyukta darśanena sadbhāvam kara yad anupapatteḥ rūpau dāhaḥ virodhāt asattvam tattva adhikaraṇaḥ samāna nā vinaṣṭa lakṣaṇaḥ asaṃyoga bahirbhāve upalakṣaṇa unmajjana vilakṣaṇa prakṛta anugataḥ sambandhāt āpattau kiṃtu jaṭā bhāvi upalambhe śūnya asaṅkīrṇa tattvam anuraktam vyāvartakam aghaṭam ghaṭavati pramātum paricchidyate vailakṣaṇyāt anutpanna sattve abhāvā samavāyaḥ upapatteḥ niṣidhyate anutpattiḥ sat viraha samavāyayoḥ saṃyoga saṃvittiḥ hetukam prāgabhāve viśeṣyāt rūpasya vyavasthāpyate rūpatā viśeṣaṇena prameye kiñca kena kāka asattve jīvana utprekṣā atirikta manyate pratīyamāne sadbhāvasya abhāvaiḥ aviśeṣaṇa arhati yogya prameyaḥ abhimataḥ upari svarūpam niyatasya viśiṣṭe pratīyamānaḥ vinā adhikaraṇe sadbhāvāt pareṇa śaśe aṃśe pṛṣṭaḥ ādheya saṃbandha abhāvābhyām anurakta tathābhūte vastuni abhyupagame prāgabhāva pratyāyya tadabhāvayoḥ ātmake anubhūyate ādhāra mānam avidyamāna sattā mate prameyam anatiḥ kalpayati janyate saṃyogaḥ caturdhā lakṣaṇānām kṣīre prasaktiḥ daṇḍena upalabdhaḥ daṇḍaḥ abhauva gavā meyam ghaṭavatī kākena pratibandhakasya astitām viviktaḥ nīlaḥ vailakṣaṇyam viviktasya avabhāsanam nivṛttaḥ anyathābhāvam dadhni
39	avayava eka mahat avayavi avayavī aṇu paramāṇu parimāṇa avayavāḥ avayavinaḥ paramāṇavaḥ dvi vartate avayavānām aneka saṃkhyā dīrgha dravya bahu parimāṇam paṭa deśa avayavaḥ avayaveṣu paramāṇuḥ paramāṇūnām sthūla vṛtti deśena ekam hrasva antara citram pratyekam tri kāraṇa samāna parimāṇasya dravyam ekasmin citra ārabdhe samudāyaḥ ārambhaka paṭaḥ alpa paramāṇoḥ avayavaiḥ avayavini parama ghaṭa tantu abhāvāt avayavebhyaḥ avayavasya paramāṇuṣu avayave prasaṅgāt antaram prasaṅgaḥ pṛthak ārabdham aṇuka sarva dravyasya bhāga sthūlaḥ avayavinam tvayoḥ ekaḥ samūha upalabhyate sāvayava deśaḥ ekasya guru cala ārabhyate samūhe rakta tantavaḥ darśanāt kāraṇam dīrgham senā atiśaya saṃkhyāyāḥ apekṣayā ārabdha bahubhiḥ kārya samūhaḥ abhāvaḥ aṇuḥ sañcita mahān avaya mahā adhika mahattva aṇūnām dravye anupapatteḥ sarvasya ārabhante anekam deśāḥ pāṇi saṃsthāna avayavinoḥ hrasvam pracaya yāvat madhya praśithila prakarṣa vṛttiḥ avayavān kampa samudāye anekatra deśe bahuṣu tantūnām āśraya āvaraṇe niravayava apekṣya alpatara parimāṇaiḥ atīndriya saṃhatāḥ utpādyam vartante kāryam vyavahāraḥ saṃghātaḥ pūrvavat rūpam upapatteḥ paṭe ekatra acala vyatirekeṇa aṇukam tantuḥ bahutva saṃyukte anārambhāt anekasya agrahaṇāt dravyavat aṇuke gaurava sūkṣma abhyupagame calati pataṅga vyatibhedāt antarasya varttate sañcaya sthūlam parimāṇāt samudāya kampe saṃkhyaiḥ āvaraṇa taiḥ alpam teṣu paramāṇau prāptiḥ yuktam tebhyaḥ tantubhyaḥ māṣaka parimāṇe hema paṭasya ākarṣaṇe dṛśyate upalabdheḥ dṛśyeta vartamānaḥ atīndriyāḥ palam vi vyavahāra samudāyasya vṛtteḥ avayavam sadbhāvāt saṃyogaiḥ bilva pratyavayavam sañcitāḥ pala saṃyoga kṛtsna āmalaka paramāṇubhiḥ kārtsnyena dhāraṇa rakte aṇukeṣu ṣaṭkena kṛtsnaḥ upalambha citraḥ mahataḥ saṃsthānam prāpnoti prāpteḥ anāvṛta samuccaya caturvidham aindriyakāḥ paramāṇubhyām dravyayoḥ yāvati vṛttyā avinaśyat vastra bhāve antarāṇām aṇavaḥ ārabhya dravyāṇi tasmin mahati kāryāṇām saṅkhyā aviśeṣaḥ yuktaḥ piṇḍaḥ āśrayaḥ avayavinī paramāṇum mūrtimat bahavaḥ sambhavāt alpīyaḥ paṭam ātmanā parimāṇaḥ anupapattiḥ pāṃśu sañcayaḥ atiśayaḥ aśeṣa tantuṣu paraspara anyat upalabdhau samudāyi pracayaḥ upalabhyeta aṇuṣu bhāgena ayuktam agrahaṇam ārambhakāḥ nīla niravayavaḥ gatiḥ dṛśyaḥ alpataram calanasya mahattvasya tūlake bhāgaḥ ā iṣyate avayavena tulya iyat piṇḍayoḥ avayavinām vayavī diśā antar ghana kasmāt avayavinā āśrita gauravam keśa bhūtaḥ upala kumbhaḥ ārambhe anavayava parimāṇena vyapadeśa akṛtam avṛtti rūpāṇi grahaṇam vartamānam
40	rāga duḥkha ātma rāgaḥ doṣa tṛṣṇā abhyāsāt sukha ātmani snehaḥ dveṣaḥ mohaḥ vīta ātmīya dveṣa kṛpā nairātmya doṣāṇām abhyāsaḥ hetuḥ duḥkham sneha rāgasya janma vairāgyam guṇa sattva doṣāḥ darśanam karuṇā moha abhyāsa darśana hetu karmma duḥkhasya para sugata avidyā dṛṣṭeḥ kāya sukham yatnaḥ darśanāt mārga bhāvanā upāya dveṣāt hetoḥ bhāvāt dayā abhāvāt duḥkhāt dṛṣṭiḥ catur kapha virajyate sat tāpa yā kāraṇam snehāt darśanasya abhyāse dveṣau pitta abhyāsena prārthanā rāgī yatna ātmā hāniḥ sakala kṛtaḥ ātmīye icchā parigrahaḥ virāgaḥ bhūta snehasya viraktaḥ prakṛtiḥ vāta muktiḥ tāratamya jagat ātmānam īrṣyā abhilāṣaḥ sampad darśī tāyaḥ sthira bīja rāgāt saṃsāra atyantam kāma grahaḥ aviraktaḥ tṛṣṇāyāḥ bhāvanayā samudaya abhiniveśa utpattiḥ śāstṛ raktaḥ tyāga kṣaya krodhaḥ duḥkhe kṣayāt darśinaḥ dveṣasya mūlam udbhavaḥ prahīṇa rāgāḥ saṃskāra śāsanam kāmaḥ karmmā doṣān satya abhiniveśaḥ sarva avasthāyām āśrayaḥ sthāna prakṛti dṛṣṭi saṅkalpaḥ aham ādiḥ vinā laṃghanam tāyi doṣaḥ prahāṇa malāḥ mahā vairāgya nirdoṣaḥ bhava bhagavataḥ viṣaye bījam sarvatra parigraha laṃghana sambhavaḥ vaktu pratipakṣa karmmaṇaḥ buddheḥ upādāna sātmye āhitaḥ mohasya strī ayoni satkāya svarasa yatnam vipakṣa mama pariṇati amarṣaḥ sugataḥ praśasta yoni nidāna tṛṣṇayā bahudhā sukhāt janmanaḥ hīyate rāgāṇām sneham spṛhā ātmanaḥ graha viśeṣaḥ hetau kṣaye nirdoṣa prāṇi sarvaḥ samāśrayaḥ dṛśyate aśuci amūḍhasya bahulaḥ garbha yatnena dayayā drohaḥ praśama snihyan śoma viṣaya pratipakṣasya yatne utkarṣa hīna prāpti asūyā janaḥ yogāt audāsīnyam maitrī dehayoḥ sahajam abhāve pūrvaḥ rājya nidānam saktiḥ ārya maya sthita ādhipatyam pāpīyān prāṇinaḥ viruddhasya virodhinaḥ garbhe abhyasyataḥ akṣamāḥ prema tṛṣṇāvān prahāṇam tādṛśaḥ praśastam śleṣma citta jaḥ laṅghana premṇaḥ rāgi yuktitaḥ yuktaḥ pīḍā abhyāsataḥ nirhrāsa varjanam dīkṣā satva jāyate bhūtānām prakarṣa yāvat māna nairātmyasya skandhānām upāyam amuktaḥ ātmībhūta lobhaḥ mārggaḥ tṛṣṇām vallabhaḥ mithyā hita pratyanīka tyajati ekasyām udayaḥ prasaṅgataḥ sthitiḥ atyanta ātmaka vṛddhiḥ mohe vāsī kṛt vyavasthita īkṣyate saṃsārī bala alam buddhi parityāga ajñānam sakalam akṣīṇa bhūvam sukheṣu saṃsāriṇaḥ tāratamyam atiśayāt buddhiḥ mūḍhaḥ viśeṣāt prabhavā ātmīyam niḥśeṣa varam heya kurute
41	veda āpta puruṣa artha pramāṇam mūla āgama vedaḥ prāmāṇyam dṛṣṭa upadeśaḥ vedasya apauruṣeya satya upadeśa pramāṇa vede adhyayana smṛti vākyānām āgamaḥ praṇīta pauruṣeya atīndriya sarva loka manu mahā sarvajña vedāḥ vacana vākyāni vākya vāda vedāt sarvajñaḥ mantra prāmāṇya mūlam adṛṣṭa āptaḥ buddha artham pāpa vacanam ācāra vedam vākyam anādi puruṣaḥ apauruṣeyam adhyayanam pratyakṣa laukika adhītya antara rāga vaidika vacanāt vedānām kartṛ vacaḥ prāmāṇyāt viruddham jñātum snāna jana virodha śāstra upadeśasya kartā āmnāyaḥ āyurveda śāstram kartuḥ śruti artheṣu itihāsa loke anumāna śva anumānam āgamasya śākhā anyathā puṇya arthānām bhagavān āgamānām avisaṃvāda sakala virodhaḥ vid apramāṇam jñaḥ upadiśati abhāvāt anṛtam viruddha upadeśāt sāmānyāt praṇetuḥ vedeṣu vaidikam satyam snānam purāṇa vedakaḥ apramāṇa āmnāyasya tulya jñāḥ mantrāṇām asmaryamāṇa snāyāt ācāraḥ yukti śāstrāṇām bhārata andha vidhi puruṣāḥ bhūta pūrvakam ukti vedān puruṣeṇa iṣṭa svarga kartṛka mleccha parigrahāt arthe āgamāt guru asatya śiṣṭa puruṣāṇām apauruṣeyaḥ āptena girām apraṇīta rathyā anuṣṭhānam svayam atyanta smṛteḥ apuruṣa īśvara tāni mithyā aitihyam aṣṭaka paraspara anāpta atīndriyeṣu upadiśyate gotra naḥ nyāya śabdānām mantrāḥ nitya praṇītam kṛtam deśa prasiddhim aviruddha anumīyate athavā hetūnām tattvasya puruṣasya abhiyuktāḥ adhyayanasya sarveṣām anuṣṭhāna adhyayanāt sampradāya avisaṃvādāt śāsanam aprāmāṇyam phala nibandhanam atiśaya avisaṃvādaḥ praṇītāḥ pauruṣeyaḥ para virodhāt īdṛśam antareṣu sākṣātkṛta icchayā arthasya apauruṣeyāḥ anumita pūrva bauddha saṃvādaḥ ṛte keṣāṃcid vadat pracakṣate vacasi ārya iṣyate siddhiḥ avitatham doṣāya abhimata śakya agnihotra upadeśena santi asarva vādaḥ kāvya smaranti sarvam ādibhiḥ vaktṛ māṃsa ācārayoḥ pauruṣeyāḥ adya kalpayitum dūram racanā vaktā dharma āgameṣu sarvajñam nara upadeśe heya vipralambha tāyāḥ sāṃkhya atiśayam āmnāya vacasām āgamena anyatas upadeśi vaidikāḥ kartavyatā upayogaḥ upadiśanti kṛtaḥ sarvaḥ puruṣe mūlā smṛtau eka āgamāḥ bhārate ādimān jñāna smṛtiḥ parokṣeṣu vaidikaḥ kavi mahājana upadeṣṭuḥ vipaścitām sarvasya vādasya mūlāḥ vidita vyākhyānam āśrayāt kasyacid paśyatu prabhāvāt sarvajñasya tulyam tadvat yathārtham upādeya laukikasya praṇītaḥ cikhyā aśakyam vaktuḥ anumānāt ādya mantrān virodham buddhaḥ kecid anumānena ucita siddhe prāmāṇye śrutiḥ saṃvādāt āptānām dvijāti kulāt
42	prāptam uta saṃdehaḥ śrūyate dvādaśa sarva prāpte jyotiṣṭome dharmāḥ brūmaḥ sarveṣām ṛtvijaḥ darśa aviśeṣāt svam adhvaryuḥ kartavyāḥ śeṣa pūrṇamāsayoḥ jyotiṣṭomaḥ ājya udakena yajamāna prakṛtau saṃyogāt yajamānasya soma sarve ṛtvij hotuḥ yajña dīkṣā saptadaśa satram dīkṣitaḥ camasaḥ kartavyam saṃkhyā paśuḥ artham bhakṣaṇam yajamānaḥ samākhyānāt ahar dakṣiṇā vacanāt aniyamaḥ vikṛtau darśanam bhakṣaḥ śatam teṣu yajati barhiḥ adhikāraḥ eṣām darśayati svāmi pūrṇamāsau pratinidhiḥ camasādhvaryavaḥ avadāna bhakṣa daśa pradhānasya prakaraṇa etāni somam sviṣṭakṛt jyotiḥ deyam trivṛt prakṛti bhaveyuḥ prāptāḥ adhvaryoḥ darśanāt dānam hāri liṅgam kartavyaḥ anārabhya prakaraṇe ālabhate bhakṣayanti udakaḥ homa saptadaśaḥ vacanam śeṣāt vākyena satra bhavanti anyaḥ dīkṣayati ṛtvijām anuvādaḥ sarvebhyaḥ padārthāḥ viśeṣaḥ jyotiṣṭoma ājyam uttara camasam pṛṣṭhāni samāmnātāḥ udgātṛ aṅgānām agnayaḥ vidhiḥ kartum kartavyāni somaḥ paśum śeṣaḥ āmnāyate ādīni tadvat avakalpate yajamānena yūpam ājyasya sāmānyāt upadadhāti paśu ahani pṛṣṭha ardhāt satrāṇi udgātā ahe śrūyante hotā some prathama vihitāḥ paśoḥ vedi karma staḥ kāmāḥ grahāḥ ekam prakaraṇāt viśeṣāt prāptaḥ jyotiṣṭomasya bhakṣayeyuḥ dīkṣita maitrāvaruṇaḥ vediḥ vṛṇīte dadāti kalpānām agniṣṭomaḥ vṛṇītaḥ agnīṣomīyam ahaḥ ijyā vidhīyate upapadyate kasmāt tāni prakṛtya paśavaḥ pātre vai ahikam camase hotāram vājapeye kratoḥ kalpāḥ svāminaḥ barhiṣaḥ savanīyānām lohita saṃdihyate upādeyam ahīna camasa artha agnīnām viśvajiti khadira kiṃcid samākhyā yajñasya bahu adhvaryuṇā bhakṣayitavyam camasān camasinaḥ rājanya yājamānam bhakṣayet naimittikam somasya saṃśayaḥ sarvāṇi bahavaḥ vidhānāḥ kuryāt paśyāmaḥ brāhmaṇānām añjana ārabhya anadhikāraḥ praiṣa paśau evamādayaḥ adhvaryu apacchedaḥ parikrayaḥ udgātuḥ āmananti arthāt prayojanam bhaviṣyati lokam sarvam padārthān deyāḥ niyamyate kriyeta dharmāṇām agnīṣomīyaḥ evaṃjātīyakāḥ bahūnām nirdeśāt viśva samāmananti svāmī adhikam prati liṅga dravyam svena abruvan ātithyāyām dīkṣayitvā juhvati yajamānāḥ aśabdam trīn kāryāṇi hutvā āmnātāḥ dīkṣaṇīya navanītam puroḍāśaḥ raśanā kṛtsnam sakṛt camaseṣu niyamaḥ śabdaḥ ṣaṣ kṛtam pātram prāpnuvanti ekaḥ prabhu pravṛttyā avadyati āmnātam ukthya śruti tasmai ādhvaryavam ājyena anubrūyāt avadātavyam dhruvāyām jyotiṣṭomam itareṣām ardham bhaviṣyanti juhoti nimittau adhvaryum anuyājān bhakṣam ekādaśinyām apacāre aha udaka karmaṇām anusamayaḥ samākhyayā sruvaḥ paśūnām tisraḥ pratinidhi upasadaḥ paśūn ekaikasya agnīṣomīyasya pitā samadhigatam
43	saṃyoga saṃyogaḥ vibhāga karma kāraṇa kāraṇam guru ākāśa vibhāgaḥ saṃyogasya jaḥ kārya avayava karmaṇaḥ yuta samavāyi asamavāyi vibhāgāt saṃyukta āśraya vibhāgam gamana saṃyoge saṃyogam ārabhate uttara abhāvāt drava ja apekṣaḥ saṃyogāt saṃyogena tantu utkṣepaṇa patana vibhāgasya dravya adhas pṛthak ārambhaka vibhāgau hasta vega saṃyogi dala patanam akāraṇa karoti vibhāgayoḥ anyatara siddhiḥ calati bhramaṇa vīraṇa vaṃśa ubhaya saṃyogāḥ pradeśa karmaṇā ākāśam saṃyujyate kāryam diś virodhi ārambhe niṣkramaṇa kriyā gamanam karmaṇi hetuḥ akārya deśena samavāyaḥ nimitta āśraye anyatarasya deśāt gatimat abhāve gacchati deśa avayavi akāraṇam vi ārabhante saṃyoginā paraspara nodanam nodana utpannam antaram sama antara vibhāge tantuka pāta utkṣepaṇam pratyaya apekṣate dvayoḥ vibhāgāḥ syandana utpattau samavetasya pradeśaiḥ praveśana sambhavati adarśanāt niṣkriyasya upalabdheḥ pratibandhāt patati vāyu vibhāgeṣu abhāvaḥ abhighāta vegena pratyāsattiḥ kāryaḥ vibhāgān abhighātaḥ tūla kāryeṇa dravyayoḥ prayatna antarāt gata kāraṇayoḥ vyatirekābhyām aprāptiḥ daṇḍa saha upalambhāt vibhūnām pratibaddham āśrayasya samaveta pāda vibhakta pātaḥ pratyāsanna antar syandanam saṃyogānām padma dravye karmaṇām kālam vegaḥ kārye kriyasya saṃyoginaḥ samavāyāt ādinā dravyam parasparam saṃyuktam dravyasya antareṇa tābhyām anityānām deśaiḥ prāpti ākāśayoḥ samam aṅguli jāḥ kāraṇasya ekasya pratyayaḥ sadbhāve jau tulā jāyate śarīra nivṛtte kāraṇeṣu deśe abhisarpaṇam gati ubhayoḥ ajaḥ janyate svatantra pūrvakaḥ patanti mātram gamane ākāśe avayavānām kriyām tantoḥ āśrayi vibhāgena prasaṅgaḥ tantvoḥ vibhāgābhyām vidhāraka ekasmāt śarīrasya itarasya dravyeṇa anutpattau avibhāga saṃyuktānām nirapekṣam avayavasya aniyata apām bherī pratibandhakasya anārambhaka setu kāraṇena ubhayatra bhāvi ūrdhva siddhaḥ samavāyinaḥ prāptiḥ nitya sthāṇoḥ gatam ākhyāyām teṣu aṅgulī yayoḥ anyasya karmāṇi anantaram paramāṇoḥ siddhi sthāṇau vṛtti niṣkramaṇam rodhaḥ sadbhāvāt vyāvartate aprāpti saṃyuktaḥ mahābhūteṣu avadhāraṇāt abhra pratyāsannam niṣkriya kriyāvatā vibhāgānām ākhyam ūhyam paraspareṇa ārambha t samānam turī gacchataḥ viśiṣṭa paṅka samantāt ārambhakaḥ saṃyogayoḥ avayavinaḥ pratibaddhāni prāpteḥ caraṇa āśrayeṣu samasta avasthānāt antare nimna sāmarthya hetoḥ tvāni akāraṇena pratibandhaka pṛthivyām anapekṣaḥ kāraṇe apekṣebhyaḥ carama nimittam samāna jāt apekṣa pradeśe aprāptayoḥ meṣayoḥ niṣkriyāṇām pārśvatas praśithilaḥ saṃyogān vyatibhedaḥ avayavini pāṣāṇa caturṣu udāharaṇam saṃyukte aguṇam yuteṣu asarva kāryasya
44	bhavanti arthāḥ syuḥ śabdāḥ sarve santi dharmāḥ eṣām taiḥ kecid hetavaḥ teṣu viśeṣāḥ yeṣām tān anye ime ucyante viṣayāḥ uktāḥ rūpāḥ tāni jāti santaḥ doṣāḥ bhedāḥ tebhyaḥ ke dṛśyante ādibhiḥ tāḥ pratyayāḥ viśeṣa amī vṛttayaḥ kurvanti svabhāvāḥ guṇāḥ pratīyante ādīni bhaveyuḥ buddhayaḥ arthānām dṛṣṭāḥ bhūtāḥ ātmānaḥ gṛhyante pravartante upalabhyante arhanti apare evamādayaḥ siddhāḥ vyavahārāḥ apekṣante sarvatra lakṣaṇāḥ bhaviṣyanti bhāvāḥ ātmakāḥ niyatāḥ bhāgāḥ trayaḥ sarveṣām āśrayāḥ vartante vacanāḥ iṣyante prasiddhāḥ jātāḥ jāḥ bhavantu bahavaḥ dharmāṇaḥ yāḥ icchanti utpannāḥ apekṣāḥ avayavāḥ vadanti sarvāḥ kṛtāḥ kecana vācyāḥ antarāṇi viśiṣṭāḥ pravṛttayaḥ samastāḥ saṃjñāḥ vyākhyātāḥ padārthāḥ asiddhāḥ śabda bhinnāḥ kalpyante saṃskāra anyatas yaiḥ āhuḥ nimittāḥ yoginaḥ gatāḥ kānicid ratha gamyante kāryāḥ yeṣu bhājaḥ gamyāḥ prāpnuvanti ādīn saha tulya viṣayāṇām vikalpāḥ anarthakāḥ arthān antāḥ prakārāḥ samarthāḥ pratibhāsante janayanti bhavantaḥ pratibhānti sarvāṇi anayā jāyante puruṣāḥ lakṣitāḥ śaknuvanti rūpa vyatiriktāḥ kiyantaḥ sādhāraṇāḥ prayogāḥ śaktayaḥ prabhṛtayaḥ atiśayāḥ svarūpāḥ vipra aṇavaḥ yān nivartante yāvantaḥ bhāvānām dhavala tadvat ityādayaḥ paśyanti anyāḥ svaiḥ yāni para sādhyāḥ laukikāḥ samyak viśeṣeṇa sarūpāḥ gocarāḥ satām sūkṣmāḥ yāvat vyavasthitāḥ apareṣām vyapadiśyante abhidadhati gatānām svabhāvānām kāścid śabdaiḥ upāyāḥ bāhyāḥ jñātāḥ śakyante asantaḥ dvividhāḥ kurvate vidaḥ upādāya sarveṣu kāriṇaḥ tepi cetanāḥ pakṣāḥ kena vidanti janmānaḥ samānāḥ abhihitāḥ pratipadyante yāvatā ṣaḍja sthāḥ mahāntaḥ nirdiṣṭāḥ satyaḥ draṣṭavyāḥ pare ghaṭa traya ādadhati nirapekṣāḥ vayam viśeṣataḥ śrutayaḥ matāḥ asatsu eṣā saṃbhavanti nāma vastūni vaśāḥ antarbhavanti śaktāḥ upalabhyeran dharmāṇām gavā pratidravyam vaktavyāḥ manyante vṛkṣāḥ kāmam mūḍhāḥ phalāḥ dravya buddhi yogī āpannāḥ pratīyamānāḥ etāḥ pravarttante vaidikāḥ lābhaḥ grāhyāḥ asmad bhūvan kriyante buddhibhiḥ ebhyaḥ prakṛtyāḥ vidyamānāḥ viśeṣāṇām rūpāṇi pratipadyamānāḥ uttānāḥ sthitam ebhiḥ vilakṣaṇāḥ ekaḥ pratipadyeta sādhanāni vyavasthāḥ etāni vyāpārāḥ āśraya dṛṣṭāntāḥ niṣṭhāḥ svarasena saṃskārāḥ keṣāṃcid kasmiṃścid anyebhyaḥ tāvantaḥ atad vartinaḥ vidyante vivakṣitāḥ vyāpakāḥ puruṣaiḥ abhidhīyante bhedaiḥ jñāyante tādṛśāḥ etena ityādinā saṃskṛtāḥ avasthitāḥ hetukāḥ yatha virudhyante eteṣu antyāḥ sambhavanti ādibhyaḥ akasmāt kurvantaḥ vaiśeṣikāḥ vyabhicāriṇaḥ lokaḥ darśayati anubhavāḥ janayeyuḥ niyāmakāḥ vyavacchinnāḥ yogāḥ veditavyāḥ atīndriyāḥ sadṛśāḥ arthena virodhinaḥ
45	pratyayaḥ śabdaḥ pratyaya nimittam nimitta śabda upacāraḥ viśeṣaṇa śabdena mukhya ṣaṣṭhī sāmānādhikaraṇyam artha daṇḍī viśeṣya viśeṣaṇam mukhyaḥ guṇa vṛkṣaḥ upacāra vṛkṣa śabdasya gauṇaḥ gauṇa daṇḍa nimittaḥ samāsaḥ viśiṣṭa pradhāna jāti vyapadeśaḥ abhidhīyate pratyayasya rāja arvāc mālā antara puruṣaḥ buddhiḥ samāsa dṛṣṭaḥ nimittasya pradhānam abhidhāna upacārāt eka mukhyam mukhye samāna vanam antareṇa adhikaraṇaḥ daṇḍaḥ yogāt sambandhaḥ bhāktaḥ puruṣa bhāgaḥ upasarjana māṇavake pācakaḥ adhikaraṇa yuktam śuklaḥ śabdayoḥ antaram arthaḥ bhāvaḥ yuktaḥ arhati viśiṣṭaḥ prayogaḥ senā pratyayāḥ abhidheya sambandhe samāse vana tiṣṭhati sambandha śabde pratyayena abhidhānam vyavahāraḥ śukla asati darśanāt nāma bhāga mukhyā upacaryate bheda arthe mañca vartate dravya bahuvrīhiḥ siṃha saṃkhyā padārthaḥ vibhakti krośanti abheda bhavitum prāpnoti samudāya māṇavakaḥ pratyayau adhikaraṇam sāmānādhikaraṇya daṇḍi puruṣe tadvat viśiṣṭam mañcāḥ ṣaṣṭhyā siṃhaḥ ālambanaḥ śabdāḥ doṣaḥ devadattaḥ nīlotpala anyatra paryāya prakṛti viśeṣyam vacanaḥ yogaḥ asambhavāt upādāya bhāva upacārasya pācaka buddheḥ rājā vṛkṣasya puruṣeṣu upacāreṇa ayuktam śabdau viśeṣyate viṣaya avṛkṣa prādhānyena śabdam daṇḍya gauṇam gauḥ mātre utpala pakṣe atasmin dravye strī abhāve svāmi sambandham gauṇe sarvatra vṛttau vyatirikta viśeṣaṇasya karmadhārayaḥ pradhānaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyāt para utpalam upacārataḥ pravartate aupacārikaḥ śabdeṣu tādarthya bhāgam upacaritam hetuḥ skhalat bahu viṣamaḥ hita sāmānyam devadatta antaḥ viśeṣaṇe dravyam anuśāsanam kalpanā śabdaiḥ aneka ādibhiḥ pratyayānām vācya nīlaḥ pratyaye gacchati antarīyakaḥ abhidhāne sādṛśyāt abhidheyaḥ anyathā sāmyāt abhidhīyante sāmāna daṇḍe vyatiriktam atadbhāve tatpuruṣaḥ bhāgasya ukte prayujyate vyākhyeyaḥ upanyāsaḥ bhavanti vṛttiḥ gehaḥ upasarjanam rājñaḥ pañcamī askhalat draṣṭavyam tadvati vane daṇḍam upacaritaḥ kiñca abhidheyam vyapadeśa upacarita apekṣaḥ nimittena sāmānyāt bhaktyā prāsāda vyapadeśasya pratyayāt samāseṣu etau vyatirekeṇa antare ityādiḥ kuṇḍalī mukhyāḥ nimittāt sāmānādhikaraṇyena nibandhanā tādṛśam vyabhicarati prayujyamānaḥ nimittāḥ sāmānya viśeṣyasya putra bhāve prayoga saṃpratyayaḥ yā kasmāt vaiṣamyam kulam laukikīm samasyate śilāputrakasya yaṣṭikā samudāyaḥ pravṛttau vrīhi bhavatu laukikānām ajāteṣu asamāsaḥ mukhyayoḥ bījam puruṣau prādhānyam abhidhāyakaḥ bhāgayoḥ nibandhanaḥ antarāṇi sārūpyāt sambandhi guṇavādaḥ mukhyatas sarve abhidhātum adravya paryāyaḥ prayuṅkte vyapadiśyate upacāre paṅkti nīlam niveśaḥ abhisambandhaḥ sphaṭikaḥ aupacārika bhaktiḥ nīla nirnimittaḥ yaugikaḥ bhāvāt gaja
46	para artha artham vacanam svayam vacana paraḥ anumānam hetu arthe sādhanam pakṣa parasya pratijñā vacanasya pratipādana pratipatti anumāne vacanena arthaḥ vacanāt liṅgam arthasya sākṣāt vākyam sādhana pratipādanam pratipattau anumāna pratipādyate trirūpa param prati pratipattiḥ prayojanam vākyena sāmarthyāt mad abhiprāya pareṣām ākhyānam vacaḥ pratipannam pratipādya sādhya śāstra pratipādayitum mātreṇa avayavena pratipannaḥ ātmānam pratītiḥ mama niścaya niścita sāmarthyam pratīteḥ liṅga dṛṣṭa alam kevalam pratipatteḥ prayujyate vaktuḥ antareṇa hetuḥ pratipadyate pramāṇam pareṇa trirūpam abhidhānam prasiddhiḥ pratipādayati siddhiḥ pañca avaśyam pāramparyeṇa parasmai prayogaḥ prayoga hetoḥ abhidhānāt ātmānau pratipattaye prathamam pratipādanāya pratipādane arthāt abhidhāna anyathā prakāśanam apekṣayā pratipādanāt upanyāsaḥ sādhyam prasiddhena sādhyasya ācaṣṭe parokṣa pratyeti svatas kriyate mātram prasiddham kṛtam asmad pratyāyana prāśnika anumeya vākya prasaṅgena paraiḥ siddham abhidhānena sampad upanaya prakāśayati prativādi kartavyam asmābhiḥ etāvat samyak hetunā mayā anarthakam ātmanaḥ vaktum ubhaya pratītam uktena kasmāt mātrāt pratipādaka sarvam viduṣām vinā kathayati āpādana prasiddhyā pratipādakaḥ parisamāptiḥ iṣṭam yāvat liṅgasya tava avayavam sūcakam anumānena abhidhānayoḥ āgamāt śabdaḥ unmatta tvayā aśaktam pratipattim parārtha satyam vaktavyam kathitam kathyate vivakṣita apratipanna abhidhānasya upadarśanam upāya vyutpādyate viparyasta vyāpāraḥ apekṣate nigamana vyavasthāpya prasiddhi rūpam vacasaḥ kasmiṃścid bhavān vicāraḥ anusāreṇa matam vyavasthām vādi abhiprāyam pravarttate sāmarthya tvad gateḥ abhiprāyasya asmin vaiyarthyāt pratīti pratītau upayogaḥ abhipreta upacārāt ākhyātum yaiḥ ācāryasya niyatam nyāya upadeśa śaktasya pravṛtteḥ yuktaḥ pratipattum rūpāt vyarthaḥ vivakṣā paratvam nigamanena vākyasya asmāt avadhārya bhaviṣyati vādī nivedayati abhipretam sādhayitum prakāśana ityādinā vakti loke niścayam vyākhyeyam yuktam paryanuyoga pāṭhaḥ uccāryate utpādanāya bravīti antar pratipādyaḥ aniścite puruṣān dvāreṇa samartha samādhānam pratipadya nivedane pratipādyāḥ avyutpannaḥ nivartana bhavataḥ kathanam tāvatā lakṣaṇau yāvatā prakāśyate trirūpāt śreyaḥ śakyate kadācid trairūpyam vyutpādana siddhi prekṣāvān liṅgāt nyāye sidhi kāle pratyāmnāyaḥ trairūpyāt uddiṣṭe manvānaḥ kin madhye asmat pratijñāyāḥ upādatte vyācaṣṭe anantaram śaknoti niścitam duṣkaram aparam yukti vaktavyaḥ prāk kiñca sūcaka upadeśataḥ kārī lokasya lokaḥ anumānaḥ upadiśati paryanuyogam upanayena pratipattyā vicāreṇa bhūtam yukta avagatam prastāvāt sāphalyam ḍiṇḍika pakṣoktiḥ prāśnikān sampadam upa niṣidhyate
47	sukha ātma manaḥ śarīra indriya duḥkha ātmā aham ātmanaḥ jñāna icchā manasaḥ śarīram sukham ātmani buddhi śarīre jñānam yugapad dveṣa artha cetanā guṇaḥ dharma prayatna liṅgam deha utpadyate viṣaya mama manasoḥ caitanyam bāhya śarīrasya kāraṇa me sannikarṣāt bhoga karaṇa kāraṇam anutpattiḥ āśraya bhūta duḥkham abhāvāt antara adharma jñānāni manasā pratyakṣa guṇa sannikarṣaḥ manasām buddhiḥ ārambha sannikarṣasya manasi jñātuḥ sannikarṣa darśanāt paratra smṛti yoga nimitta antaḥkaraṇa liṅga utpattau bhoktṛ uparata caitanya jñātṛ yogaḥ duḥkhayoḥ vyavasthā saṃyoga utpattiḥ pravṛtti nimittam dṛṣṭam guṇānām prāṇi indriyāṇi ādibhiḥ ayaugapadyāt antaram prasaṅgaḥ viṣayeṣu asmad sarva guṇāḥ sukhasya itas pralīna viśeṣāt pratisandhānāt bhāvāt viśeṣa pratyakṣāḥ utpatteḥ darśanam antareṣu saṃjñā jānāmi grāmasya nivṛttī saṃyogaḥ nivṛtti pratyakṣam ārṣam pratyakṣaḥ hetuḥ bhāvanā duḥkhe sukhī bahis prātibham aṇu ādhāra caitanyasya upapatteḥ bhūtam indriyaiḥ indriyāṇām viśeṣaḥ samāna vibhu anapekṣam caitanye ātmānam artham ādīni bhoktā ahaṅkāreṇa vyāsakta anugraha jñasya bhūtānām jña utpatti āśrayaḥ saṃvedanam antar cetanāḥ ceṣṭa icchati ceṣṭā upabhoga sannikarṣe prayatnaḥ pratiśarīram satsu liṅgāni jñātari teṣu bhavanti samavāyi vedanā ahaṅkāraḥ anyasya gauraḥ candana hetūnām pratyātma jānām jñātā śvas abhūt ja asatsu eka prayatnāḥ mana dvāreṇa bhrātā sādhaneṣu adharmau buddhayaḥ jñānānām dveṣayoḥ dhāraṇam ayaugapadya sāmarthyāt āyatanam upaghāta cetanaḥ ahaṅkāra ahaṃpratyaya ahaṃpratyayaḥ sānnidhye ajña atīteṣu pratyagātmani nānā duḥkhī sukhena jam anāgateṣu puruṣa abhāve viṣayāḥ samavāyāt viṃśati artheṣu ātmanā strī prīti hetu sukhāt nimitte ahaṃśabdaḥ manaskasya vidau dveṣau śarīriṇām vedanīyam traya catuṣṭaya cetana saṅghāta apratiṣedhaḥ antaḥkaraṇam śarīrāt anyat anumīyate viśiṣyate supta cetanāyāḥ saṃyogāt cetanasya saṅghātaḥ prasāda samavaiti manassaṃyogaḥ dharmāt arthayoḥ anupapattiḥ utpannam tāni sādhanāni ātmaka ayaugapadyam paritāpa prābalyāt graha adharmayoḥ adṛṣṭam ādīn pratibhā ādya pratisandhāna jena antare viprakṛṣṭeṣu antaḥkaraṇasya acetana jñānasya antikam ajñānāt samānam āgamikam sukhayoḥ viśeṣeṇa vaśāt āśu ādyeṣu asvāpsam mātre siddhe saṃskārāḥ saṃvitti saṅkalpāt sthāneṣu kasmāt kāraṇāt pariśeṣāt hetavaḥ asamavāyāt indriye pāda anubhūtavān śirasi janayati yad praṇidhāna pratyaya dṛśyate āgama syātām anubhavanam pāde adhikaraṇa upaghātaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ keśa anumānam prayatnānām saṃvid stham puruṣasya manassaṃyoga
48	indriya cakṣuḥ viṣaya indriyam indriyāṇi grahaṇam indriyāṇām rūpa śrotra prāpya tvac karaṇa pradīpa manaḥ cakṣuṣā grahaṇa kāri cakṣuṣaḥ ghrāṇa vṛttiḥ aprāpya adhiṣṭhāna bāhya indriyasya indriyeṇa antara gandha upalabdhiḥ manasaḥ kuḍya ādibhiḥ artha yugapad grahaṇāt raśmi upalabdhi bhautika ekam vṛtti sparśa rasa karaṇam gṛhṇāti prāpti pradīpaḥ eka viṣayam śabda prakāśa adhiṣṭhānam sphaṭika gṛhyate manasā rasanā artham grāhya tāni bahis antaḥkaraṇam rasana antaḥkaraṇasya antaḥkaraṇa bhautikāni viṣayāṇi sannikarṣaḥ dṛṣṭam nānā pañca kāca āloka viṣayaḥ pradīpena sparśanābhyām upalabhyate bhautikam prakāśakam grāhyāḥ darśana sarva grāhakam vyavahita sannikarṣa prakāśaka anumīyate dīpa paṭala prāpnoti avyakta saṃyukta cakṣuṣi dvāri karaṇāni sparśana pradīpasya indriyaiḥ sparśanena agrahaṇam ādīni ghrāṇam pañcatvāt raśmiḥ antarita raśmeḥ grāhaka paśyāmi upalabdhau śrotram aneka ghaṭa upalabdheḥ śrotre saṅghāta abhautikam prakāśayati abhra dūra viśeṣāt upaghāte prāptiḥ viṣaye jihvā pradīpam kasmāt grahaṇāni nayana ādarśa bhūtebhyaḥ tejaḥ sannikarṣe bhāvāt gati śrotrāṇi ati anupalabdheḥ ādīn dūre sāmarthyam viṣayasya rūpam apekṣate viṣayān niyata karaṇānām vṛttayaḥ dvāra rasanam cakṣuṣoḥ ayuktam aviṣaya tulya bāhyam adhiṣṭhānāt niyamaḥ vyāsaṅgaḥ anyathā vṛttīnām cakṣū ātmā vyatiriktaḥ avighātāt cākṣuṣaḥ santi karaṇaiḥ raśmayaḥ eṣām gṛhyante svām pañcānām sambaddham antike prasaṅgāt prakāśaḥ prāpta arthāḥ aprāptam sadbhāvāt vyavahite buddhiḥ cakṣu candramasoḥ vṛttimatoḥ ghrāṇena golaka śrotrasya rūpāṇi tvacā sadbhāve siddhau ādinā pratyartha abhivyajyate ayugapad gandham cākṣuṣam cetanā karaṇasya badhiraḥ avyatirekāt manasi ādāna grāhyam vyavahitam āditya karaṇena upalabhyante bhūta maṇḍala vṛtteḥ bhavitavyam āvaraṇa dhāraṇam taiḥ pidhāne sambadhyate arthena sparśanam kāriṇī buddheḥ śabdam bahūni grahaṇe tri itareṇa abhautika apratighātaḥ kartṛkau kṛṣṇasāram sāntaraḥ sambhavati añjana gṛhṇīyāt pratipatti adhika prasajyate apekṣam asambaddham prakāśanam grahaṇasya andha karṇa āvaraṇasya prabhā indriyāt vyavasthānāt antarite nikṛṣyate indriyeṣu vibhu antar sarvāṇi ākūtam nāsā sambandhaḥ śeṣāṇi saṅghātaḥ kṛṣṇasāra pradīpe sāṅkhya cikitsā vṛttau trayasya cākṣuṣasya grahaṇānām dvitīyam ubhayam buddhīnām kāryā dvāreṇa dravyam anugrahāt gṛhyamāṇe vidyut kenacid samavāyāt abhibhavāt nirgatya vyāpaka anavasthāyi upalabhante arthaiḥ āśraya kārīṇi vyāpāre anugraham bāhyena buddhi ālocana etāni śeṣeṣu śṛṇoti antika maṇḍalam ulkā ubhaya abhautikāni apavargiṇī raśmīnām tvaci ākūta bhaveyuḥ
49	sat asat sattā sambandhaḥ ādhāra samavāyaḥ sambandha asataḥ sataḥ samavāya viṣāṇa śaśa sattvam ādheya phalam samavāyasya hetuḥ ādhāraḥ prāk paṭaḥ khara abhāvāt pratyaya asattvam viṣāṇam kriyate ayuta vidyate ātmanā vidyamānasya puṣpa paṭa saha paścāt kha kāryam abhivyaktiḥ phalasya asatoḥ tantu sattve ayuktam tantuṣu bhūtasya sattvāt ghaṭaḥ bhūtānām pūrvam hetoḥ satkāryam sattāyāḥ sarvatra sattva asattvāt sāmagryām san hetu ghaṭa kuṇḍe asan bhāvaḥ badara jāyate asattve abhūtam abhāvaḥ paṭasya viṣāṇasya astitvam asattva vidyamānam bhūtam sattvena sambandhi avidyamāna sarvam siddhānām varṣa saṃgatiḥ vidyamāna yogaḥ asatām āśrayi asatī janayet bhāvasya satkārya niyamaḥ yuktam utpadyate sambandhe bhūta gagana sattām ādhārya paramārthataḥ ātma kiṃcid vidyamānaḥ anyat svatas sambandhasya vyapadeśa śakyam satām aviśeṣāt akaraṇāt kuṇḍa kasmāt siddham avidyamānam utpatteḥ tulyaḥ aghaṭaḥ āvaktavyaḥ abhivyakti prasaṅgaḥ prasaṅgāt sattāyām svarūpam bhāva abhūtasya samavāyāt iṣyate mayam kā hetunā phalena matam samavāyam asattvena arthaiḥ vṛttiḥ pratyayeṣu karaṇāt śaśasya sattayā jātu anavasthā prāc janayati tantavaḥ asatā utpattiḥ sāmagryā janayate dravya niyamāt yujyate sambandhāt utpatti āsan tadvatām satā anayoḥ pratyayaḥ vaktum ayutasiddhānām antayoḥ vandhyā kārye carma nityasya ghaṭasya ādhāram kuṇḍam samavetam abhyupagame kusuma bhāve sarvathā pāratantryam ādhāreṇa satī ekānta ādhārasya etena ayutasiddha ihapratyaya yuta buddhiḥ astitve āsat ātapa hetau doṣaḥ kāraṇaiḥ siddhayoḥ janaka parihāreṇa samavāyi siddhiḥ santi dūṣaṇam jala upādāna kārakaiḥ kriyā avidyamānasya badarāṇi niṣpattau sambandhinoḥ pratyayānām vaiyarthyāt aniṣpannasya parikalpyate upalabhyate kalpanāyām sarvasmāt ādheyam naḥ nāma viruddham apratyayāḥ tebhyaḥ sambandhayoḥ vāda sāmarthyāt ātapābhyām bhāvāt asati samavāye kriyamāṇa ajātena buddhyā niruddhaḥ tantūnām jātasya vīraṇa paṭayoḥ atyanta nirvartate atiprasaṅgaḥ śakyate tadānīm gaganam ādibhiḥ sambandhāḥ itas agatīnām saditi anyatra paraspara atītena pratyayebhyaḥ tantubhiḥ traye siddhasya asiddhārtha vastunaḥ avasthitānām matena janyate saṃyogī anupalabhyamāna kartum nivṛttam kāle khapuṣpa āvirbhavati samavāyī saṃśleṣa dvaya abhivyakteḥ phala pratipādayan vyomnaḥ niṣpatti ajāta āhetukam pratibandhataḥ viṣāṇayoḥ mṛd viṣayi apṛthak saṃbandha mūla anupapattiḥ anupakārya vastra anyaḥ siddhānāmādhārya pakṣayoḥ nirudhyate avidyamānaḥ dhāraṇam ākhyām prasaṅga janayiṣyati saṃvṛtyā jātam lakṣaṇaḥ hetutva adṛṣṭvā nirvartakaḥ āropataḥ sadeva śaśaḥ upādāneṣu sattvasya
50	rūpa rasa sparśa gandha pṛthivī drava tejaḥ sparśaḥ rūpam dravya pārthiva uṣṇa vāyu vāyuḥ jala agni sparśasya guṇa rasaḥ udbhūta rūpasya śīta śukla gandhaḥ rūpavat dravyam apām pāka pārthivam tejasaḥ tvac indriya udaka vāyoḥ madhye gandhasya anuṣṇa pṛthivyām pākaja dravyasya ap vāyau sparśavat bhūta tejasi suvarṇa ghrāṇa pṛthivyāḥ āpaḥ anudbhūta taijasa rūpe upalabdheḥ śuklam aśīta avayava guru bhūyas indriyam samavāyāt vyañjakam kaṭhina madhura apsu gata rasana ghaṭa upalabdhiḥ taijasam aneka ārabdham atyanta dravyeṇa sparśam sneha sparśāḥ upalabhyate pratyakṣa niyamena agandham vahni paramāṇu avayavaiḥ saṃyogāt dṛṣṭaḥ grāhya viśeṣa rasasya dravye mahat sarva adbhiḥ āpyam sparśayoḥ jvalana avakāśa spārśana śītaḥ arūpam āśraya uṣṇaḥ arasam pūrvavat viśeṣaḥ tamaḥ naimittika bhūtānām etena rūpāt āloka cakṣuṣā kṛṣṇa pīta viśeṣāt vyañjaka ghṛta ekaika nayana rasavat saṃyogena gandhavat udbhava tejasoḥ paramāṇuṣu tṛṇa jāyante anila cakṣuḥ adṛṣṭa sahakārī saṃyukta surabhi snigdha abhāvāt kāraṇa kleda anala āpya viśiṣṭa sparśeṣu kṣitau sparśe bhūtāni utkarṣāt mṛdu ghrāṇam upalambhāt ākāśasya sarpiḥ upalambhakam prakṛtiḥ ā jñāyate salila puṣpa utkarṣaḥ anārambhaka sparśena avayavānām grāhyaḥ pratyakṣaḥ kārye anabhibhūtaiḥ dhṛti vijātīya tejasā gṛhyate guṇam sāṃsiddhikam vāyunā darśanāt snehaḥ auṣṇya upalabhyamāna kāraṇam vāri apratyakṣa bhū divya cākṣuṣa adhikaraṇam asurabhiḥ himakaraka jatu pārthivānām tanmātrāt prakāśakam guṇasya bahis ja ākāśaiḥ pākāt pītam ādibhiḥ guṇaḥ sparśana dugdha rūpi pratyakṣam rase naimittikam udake bhāsvaram ghrāṇasya kaṣāya viṣṭam mahābhūta rūpāṇām rasam pārthivasya upalabdhi loha āpyayoḥ āditya śarīram upalambhaḥ mātram sāṃsiddhika tasmin bhasma druta prabhā bhūyastvāt paryantāḥ prāṇinām nimittam arthaḥ abhibhūta gandhānām saṃyoge tāmra jalam parṇa upalabhyante ādinā sparśau apaḥ udakam nimittāt prakāram pramāṇam ātapa cākṣuṣaḥ lohita suvarṇam paṭa raśmiḥ grahaṇam rasayoḥ ghṛtam latā anuvidhānāt upalambhāni kṣiti bhūmi saṃgraha dṛṣṭam aśītaḥ pākajaḥ pārthive suvarṇasya śyāmam sambandhāt ārambhāt arūpaḥ gandhāḥ kṣiteḥ vyākhyātam paramāṇūnām abhivyañjaka tapta ācākṣuṣa rasau anyathā vināśāt kampa lavaṇa udbhūtam viṣayaḥ indriyeṇa apāka dṛṣṭānām vaidharmyam anuṣṇaḥ agneḥ śarīre saṃskāra acākṣuṣa saṃyoga prakṛtīni uṣṇam niṣiddham utpatti caturṇām ūṣma ayuktam madhya rūpāṇi gandham śeṣeṣu
51	smṛtiḥ pūrva smṛti smaraṇam saṃskāra smaraṇa anubhava saṃskāraḥ smṛteḥ jñānam jñāna anubhavaḥ anubhūta smaryate saṃskārasya smaraṇāt kāla smaraṇe anubhūtam uttara smṛtyā abhyāsa smṛtim pūrvam antareṇa smarati anubhave anantaram saṃskārāt smṛtau grahaṇa abhāvāt dṛṣṭa pratyabhijñānam smaraṇasya viṣaya kāraṇam eka viṣayam gṛhīta anubhūtaḥ anubhavāt smarāmi adrākṣam anubhavasya mayā saṃskāreṇa janma janita pratisandhānam viṣayā parāmarśa anubhavena antara jñānena anubhūteṣu kāle utpadyate aham janyate kālam saṅketa parāmarśaḥ pratyabhijñāna anubhūtasya bhāvi ananubhūta darśanāt atīta anyathā antare yāvat darśana kāraṇa anubhūte dṛṣṭam krameṇa anubhavam viṣaye darśane vijñānam asmaraṇam pratyabhijñānāt anusmaraṇa āsīt vāsanā arthe anyena gṛhīte anusandhāna janmani buddhi grahaṇam āhita adṛṣṭa praṇidhāna idānīm cira bālasya smaryeta samaya jāyate saṃskāram darśanam jñānasya saha vinaśyat jñāne apara agṛhīta smṛtam kadācid tasyāḥ vijñāna vaśāt anubhūtiḥ viṣayaḥ dṛṣṭasya jñānāni pāṭava prathama abhyāsam tadānīm saṃskārāḥ bhavat artheṣu pratisandhāna pūrve buddhīnām janayati balāt abhyāsaḥ upalabdham smaryamāṇa smaraṇena sambhavati asmaraṇāt indriya tṛtīya ghaṭaḥ antya bhavatu jāta kalpanā prācīna saṃskāre pratyaya udeti ja sākṣāt smaryamāṇe hetu bhāvāt jñāyate atītasya kṛtaḥ sādhanatva devadatta abhilāṣaḥ anantara jaḥ anya asat ananubhūtam ananubhūte bhāvanā sahitena upalabdhe smartā pūrvasya gṛhyamāṇam prāk dina bhāvinām gṛhītam viśiṣṭam smaraṇayoḥ smartavya stanya ātmani prabodhe anusmṛtiḥ smaraṇañca yam smārtam atiśayaḥ smaran prabandha anubhavayoḥ smaryante prathamam gṛhītasya anavasthā ādhatte stana kalpyate bāla amum prāktana abhyasta sahakāriṇā sthitam paramparayā prasaṅgaḥ anapekṣam eṣā purā kalpanāyām antyam janitaḥ grāhiṇi jñānānām pratyutpanna smarataḥ anubhūyate anupapattyā jātaḥ anubhavitā anyaḥ śruta anubhūyamāne siddhā atyantān paśyāmi dṛṣṭā pratyabhijñā adhikam bhavantī cākṣuṣe sakala atīte svayam jñānayoḥ jñānāt ādya saṃskārāṇām anusmaraṇam vivekena apekṣaḥ janmanā smṛtayaḥ saṃvedyate liṅga udbodhakam vartamāna hetuḥ etarhi upapadyate sambhavāt gṛhyate vyavahita pratyakṣeṇa pratyabhijānāti dṛṣṭaḥ smṛtvā apekṣam smṛtīnām uttarottara anusmarati saṃketa prabandhaḥ ūrdhvam buddhiṣu darśanasya pāramparyeṇa bījam antarāle paṭīyān udbodha kauśalam akasmāt paṭu ajñāsiṣam upajāyamānam idantā sañcāraḥ vyavadhānena santāna jñāneṣu dṛṣṭeḥ ubhaya anubhavau smartum anu anuvyavasāyaḥ bhavīya jñātam vivicyate sahasā niyata sannihita bodhe avasthā śiṣya anubhūti pratyabhijñāne mātrasya avadhāraṇe arthavat tṛtīyam
52	upādānam upapadyate gamanam karma yujyate ātmā vidyate gantā pratītya saṃbhavati kṛtam gacchati kārakaḥ pūrvam nāma sadbhāvāt pratipādayan duḥkham darśana upādāna jarā anyaḥ skandhāḥ saṃsāraḥ skandha gamyamānam kleśāḥ saṃbhavaḥ asati vinā idānīm śāśvatam kāraṇam bhaviṣyati gami kiṃcid saṃskārāṇām bhavaḥ bhūtam gamana vedanā bhūtaḥ pudgalaḥ tathāgataḥ pratyayam deva tiṣṭhati ṛte gamyate gati asat utpadyamānam prasaṅgāt ādīni saṃtānaḥ svabhāvataḥ abhiprāyaḥ ahetukam manuṣyaḥ karoti yuktam bandhanam parikalpyeta vijñāna aśubha vyatiriktaḥ badhyate anupādānaḥ manuṣya maraṇa upādātā abhāvāt phala syuḥ skandhān sadbhūtam saṃsargaḥ niruddham kṛtvā ityādinā pūrva gantuḥ tadānīm sadbhūtaḥ parikalpyate gamyamāne draṣṭavya gateḥ prajñapyate gamyamāna skandhebhyaḥ ādibhyaḥ tamaḥ aśāśvatam prasajyate pañcadhā pañca āyatana upādāne vibhavaḥ mucyate vidyete asaṃbhavaḥ śāśvata dvayam abhipravartate upādātuḥ maraṇam gate śubha vidyante rahitaḥ sarvathā pudgala deśaḥ draṣṭā ātmānam saṃsarati adhvānam vandhyā jātiḥ kramaḥ pūrvaḥ bandhana gantṛ saṃsāra nirhetukam arthena kartā dvaya upādāya karmaṇaḥ ārabhyate pravartate baddhaḥ saṃskārāḥ andhakāra gatam ubhayathā gatyā saṃtāna uktaiḥ agatam utpadyate hetubhiḥ nirvāṇe bandha nirhetukaḥ gamane san upādānāt santi agate saṃsaranti ākhyam gamanena nirudhyate avidyamāna vicāryamāṇam phalam saṃbhavataḥ jam anyena pratyākhyāya kartuḥ veditavyam āgataiḥ sadbhūtasya upādānayoḥ devadattaḥ upādānasya samam vinirmuktaḥ akarmakaḥ śravaṇa yayā staḥ vyatirekeṇa rakte ekaikasmāt paraspara pṛthak rūpam rahitasya siddham vyavasthitaḥ vicāryamāṇaḥ ātmanaḥ devaḥ atītam dūṣaṇam avidyamānasya gacchet ajyate pratyayā kriyate dviśas hetukam saṃsārasya tiraskṛtya prakāram vinirmuktam abhivyajyate agantā saṃvidyate ucchinnam iṣyate utpādaḥ saṃskārān kaṃcid vijñānam gatāgata mṛgyamāṇaḥ pūrṇām pūya sarvaśas syātām dhana dhātavaḥ sattvaḥ tṛtīyaḥ kuryāt saṃsaraṇam anutpannaḥ tattvataḥ kriyā gantum vipula gamyamānasya gata pūrvavat parikalpyamānaḥ śrotā vartamānayoḥ astitvam saṃbhavanti akṛtam imān pudgalasya kāryam katamaḥ anupādāya antavān ayuktam aṃśikāḥ askandha devāt kuha saṃpravartate kāmam apratyaya nirvāṇam pravṛttiḥ akartṛkam saṃbandhaḥ anyatva trayāṇām bījāt aṅkura alakṣaṇe sthiti sat athavā mokṣau raktaḥ prasiddhaye doṣaḥ upādatte vacanāt ekatva naraka puṣpa utpadyamānena anyat anutpannam abhūm alakṣaṇaḥ gantāram māraṇa nivṛtaḥ pudgalena saṃsariṣyati upādātṛ uccheda hetukaḥ abhūvam upādānena sarvebhyaḥ vyaya para agantuḥ nirāśrayam skandhā duḥkhena kartṛ hetuka catuṣṭayam nirapekṣaḥ ghaṭāt phale
53	devatā mantraḥ indra indraḥ nirvapet soma uta śrūyate haviḥ śruti eka āgneyaḥ kapālam vai aindra saṃdehaḥ mantra pūrvam artha agnaye puroḍāśa liṅgam pāṭha mantrāḥ tvā mantrasya śeṣaḥ mantreṇa aṣṭākapālaḥ prāptam devatāḥ carum kramaḥ prāpte artham vacanam prajāpatiḥ caruḥ apanayaḥ yājyā kapālaḥ iṣṭiḥ amāvāsyāyām tuṣa peṣaṇam varuṇa paurṇamāsyām gṛhṇāti somaḥ upasthānam arhati liṅga arthaḥ ūrdhvam balīyaḥ atideśaḥ brūmaḥ puroḍāśaḥ paurṇamāsī paśu devatām prayojanam vākya uttaraḥ vādaḥ bhāgaḥ agne vākyam carau yajamānaḥ guṇa āgneya agnīṣomīya dvi kramāt asi mantre darśayati avabhṛthaḥ antam avadyati prastaraḥ puroḍāśam udāharaṇam tasmin itarathā abhidhānam abhidhāna agniḥ viniyogaḥ vidhayaḥ pūrvaḥ vapām ālabheta arthāḥ aśvam liṅgāt somāt laukike ekādaśa upatiṣṭhate saṃyogāt utkarṣaḥ aindram arodīt prati viprakarṣāt virodhaḥ pūrva naimittikaḥ prakaraṇam gārhapatyam sadanam svāhā indrāya viprakarṣaḥ kapāla tvāya aśva devatāyāḥ ekam vaidike gārhapatya vapā bhavitum agni havīṃṣi śaṃsati barhiḥ mukhya aindrāgnam sūktavākaḥ kriyamāṇe bhūti payaḥ agna dadhi āśvinam āyuḥ vibhāge avabhṛtha kiṃcid bādhyeta agre bhaviṣyati bhakṣaṇam krame evamādi sāmarthyāt aindraḥ caru devatānām kapālasya nirvāpaḥ saha bale pāna prakṛtau āgneyasya prākṛtam tāḥ arthavat kṛtsnaḥ mantrāṇām nirvāpa vāc virodhe anuṣaṅgaḥ anarthakaḥ dvādaśa iṣṭakāḥ śrutiḥ pānam anūdyate abhyudaye kriyate karaṇam anuvākyā dadhāti vaditum asmin savanīya caturdhā arthena āgneyam uccāraṇa viniyoga mantreṣu purastāt pratigrahaḥ pūrvedyus pītaḥ aṣṭākapālam devatāyai devatye indram niruptam nirvapāmi prathayati pūṣā avagamyate vaidikaḥ ante devatyaḥ vādinī karmaṇī somasya etam sāmarthyam kramasya codite mantram devasya indrasya upakurvanti dadhani muṣṭinā balīyān agnau sthānāt avabhṛtham bhakṣayāmi dāmi devatayā gārhapatyaḥ pauṣṇam puroḍāśe sāṃnāyya sīdā sūktavākena bādhitam vāyuḥ sarveṣu pūrvasya śṛte varcaḥ viniyujyeta vaśena mātram āmnānam devatāyām krama arthāt catur nirvapati dīyate agnim upāṃśu śeṣeṇa bhakṣaṇe chandaḥ etāḥ taṇḍula saṃyogaḥ gamyate ājyam praṇayanam yajñena stutiḥ agnīṣomau anirupte dadṛśe kṣepiṣṭhā māghī niṣkāsam prājāpatyānām prākṛtībhyaḥ pratigṛhṇāti śrapaṇam syonam trivṛtā varuṇaḥ vaṣaṭkāraḥ vibhajet doṣaḥ adṛṣṭa prayoktavyaḥ brāhmaṇasya dharmāḥ upapadyate hṛdayasya rudra śarāve utkṛṣyate avabhṛthe samāmnātaḥ yāvataḥ eṣā pañca agnīt uru me krameṇa sadana diśaḥ caranti ardham liṅgena apakarṣaḥ prajāpateḥ
54	darśana darśanam niścayaḥ pravṛttiḥ dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa dṛśyate darśanāt anyatra adarśanam darśane niścaya darśanena dṛṣṭaḥ paśyati sarvatra dṛṣṭam artha dṛśya pravṛtti anyathā kadācid adarśana adṛṣṭam dṛṣṭe pravartate darśanasya ekatra sarva niścaye kasyacid adarśane paśyan nāma dṛṣṭā niścayāt abhāvāt ati artham niścayasya pravarteta dṛṣṭasya arthī viveka adṛṣṭaḥ śaṅkā adarśanāt arthasya adṛṣṭe pravṛttau kalpanā antarīyaka aniścayaḥ darśī adṛṣṭasya aniścaya sambhavāt dṛśyeta gatiḥ draṣṭum sarvaḥ yuktā anyat sarvadā prāpti antareṇa niścayam samāropa vidaḥ apravṛttiḥ pravartamānaḥ niścīyate dṛṣṭi arthā anya arthinām kasmāt ayuktam dṛṣṭvā bhūyas pravṛtteḥ vyavahāraḥ nivṛtti sambhavati yuktaḥ āśaṅkā prāptiḥ dūra bhaviṣyati adṛśya arthaḥ pratipatti kiṃcid pratipattiḥ sandeha bhrānti kā dṛṣṭau vyabhicāra bhidā arthe aśakya adṛṣṭiḥ darśinaḥ anartha dṛṣṭiḥ āropaṇam adṛṣṭena sandehāt apekṣate dṛśyam viśeṣaḥ paśyet niścitam bhrānteḥ niścitya vipralabdhaḥ dṛṣṭena draṣṭā kalpyate kārī avyaktam bhūt pravṛttasya dṛṣṭāḥ dṛśyante viṣa niyata niścayena pāṭava dṛśyamāne samāropaḥ tulyam gamyate apaśyataḥ viparyayaḥ dṛṣṭeṣu bhavitavyam arthinaḥ antarīyakaḥ vastu sadbhāvāt kāraṇam prekṣāvān prasaṅgaḥ vyaktam prāk abhāve paśyataḥ tāvatā rūpe nimittam bhramaḥ apekṣaṇāt yujyate viṣaye ādike bhrāntiḥ parān aniścaye aniścitam bhavataḥ draṣṭuḥ pramāṇāt anumānam anyasya adṛṣṭā nivartate sāmarthya dṛśyasya niścāyakam vaikalyāt kriyate aniścita satsu parisphuṭam aparatra upāyasya niścite apravṛtti pravarttate arvāk su dṛśyamāna nivṛttiḥ bhāvasya śakale deśe akasmāt ālokasya kiñca kathaṃcid anala vṛttiḥ apratipattiḥ bhāseta ipi upāya salila tāratamya prāptum bhedena vyavasyanti bādhaka pratiyogī sadṛśa ātmakam vyakta jātīyasya manda adṛṣṭeṣu vyavasyati pratipāditaḥ viniścayaḥ paricchinatti asphuṭam adarśanena arthi darśinām avasāya upahata asati sasya aneka analam hetuṣu vyarthaḥ adoṣaḥ anveṣaṇa avasāyaḥ paśyanti svadhī aniścayāt alam apravartanam darśayat aprāpteḥ āsādya evaṃrūpaḥ abhyupagamya dīpa sphuṭam vācyam adarśanasya darśanayoḥ nibandhane prekṣāvataḥ mā dṛṣṭāt avyakta vaśā apāṭavāt anutpanne āśritya bhavat apratipattau kṛṣi abhilāṣa parīkṣaṇīyam pāṭavam vivekam pravṛttim niścita puruṣaḥ tattva sutarām amutas prasanna adhyavasāyaḥ śrutam āloka akhilaḥ arthitayā āvaraṇāt aviveka dṛśyamānasya dhiyaḥ pratyāsattiḥ aliṅgam bhavantī āsanna anāvaraṇe anveṣate āsanne niścitāḥ kuṇapa dṛṣṭyā sāmarthyena yogyam darśanaḥ sārūpyāt upasaṃhāreṇa viparīta anupalambhe pratipattau adṛśyam arddha prasaktā spṛśyate sambandham
55	prāmāṇyam prāmāṇya svatas pramāṇa doṣa jñāna aprāmāṇyam jñānam artha pramāṇam paratas vaktṛ aprāmāṇya niścayaḥ apramāṇam prāmāṇye kāraṇa āpta niścaya antara mithyā anavasthā bādhaka mithyātvam samyak puruṣa apramāṇa vede yathārtha arthe saṃvāda guṇa jñāne codanā prāmāṇyasya jñānasya veda apekṣam pratyayita duṣṭa vākyam utpattau vākya apekṣā śaṅkā saṃśaya duṣṭam āśaṅkā doṣāḥ abhāvāt jñānāt mithyātva artham anṛta yāvat svarūpa niścaye bādha dvayam apekṣate bādhaḥ adhīna ayathārtha pratyayaḥ vaktuḥ doṣāt anāpta aprāmāṇye abhāva viparyaya vaktra apekṣa saṃśayāt saṃvādāt abhāvaḥ kāraṇam vākye satya śabde mātreṇa viṣayam sarva doṣāṇām bodha pratyaya śrotuḥ prāmāṇyāt jāyate aduṣṭa mātrāt śabdasya jñānena vacaḥ darśanāt bādhyate niścayasya anapekṣa vyavahāra pramāṇasya vākyeṣu niścite jāte aduṣṭam doṣataḥ niścayāt utpannam avadhāraṇāt pūrva bādhakam doṣaḥ apekṣyate anabhyāsa viśvāsaḥ ajñāna pramāṇānām vyabhicāra ayathārtham bodhe para agṛhīta anuvāda abhāve vākyasya viparyeti apavāda niścīyate prasaṅgāt ukti adhīnaḥ asat adhīnam vacasaḥ visaṃvāda ayatha saṃśayaḥ tāvatā bhaviṣyati saṃvādaḥ pramāṇe visaṃvādaḥ sāpekṣam vijñāne doṣebhyaḥ pūrvasya bravīti jñānānām vitatham anāgata samyaktva autsargikam antare doṣān nivartate vākyāt viparyaye vyavahāraḥ indriya viparyayaḥ ajñānāt asaṃsparśi saṃsarga guṇāḥ adhīnā vākyānām mṛṣā saṃbhavāt paricchedāt itaretara vyāpāraḥ antaram avabodha codanānām vadanti karaṇe viṣaye pramāṇena paricchedaka aprāmāṇyāt codanāyāḥ visaṃvādāt aniścita anyonya pravṛttau utpadyate sākṣāt apodyate abhāvena niścita hetuḥ apratyayita pratyudāharaṇe uttha pauruṣeye pratibandha avadhāryate timira avadhāraṇa buddha hasti apravṛttasya niścāyaka āhuḥ viparīta prāmāṇyena doṣaiḥ avadhāritaḥ viparyayau sthitiḥ laghīyasī bādhe apauruṣeya mātre apavādaḥ nivedanāt anavasthānāt saṃbhave doṣeṣu sarvatra duṣṭaḥ udaye nibandhanam ātmaka prathamam gocaram utpatti vaktari yūtha sambhāvyate anāśvāsaḥ apekṣayā avyatireka agre śrotā asaṃsparśī saṃvādena visaṃvādi puruṣasya vedasya abādhita janitam nirapekṣa arthasya virodhāt jāta aprāmāṇyasya arthānyathātva anupalabdhe śuddhi sambhāvanā kutaścid pratibhā āptasya utpannaḥ vipratiṣiddham bādhitam pauruṣeya asatya janmanaḥ vedānām saṃśaye nirapekṣam nirṇayaḥ utpattiḥ nirāśrayāḥ mithyājñāna vibhrama guṇavat śuddha bādhakaḥ paścāt aṅgulī dhīḥ apauruṣeye asandigdham nūnam ātmakam diś avisaṃvādanam niścetum asāmarthyam niṣkampa loke janyate anapoditam asaṃsparśitā āśaṅkasya bhramatu pauruṣeyeṣu puṃvacaḥ puṃvākyam niścayam asamīcīnam guṇaiḥ tīre dṛṣṭam prathamasya asamīcīnaḥ mānatā nirapavādam sthāpanam
56	anitya nitya kṛtaka nityaḥ śabdaḥ anityaḥ nityam anityam prayatna śabda śabde eka vināśa ākāśa ghaṭa vipakṣa śabdasya deśa vyāpakaḥ anantarīyaka anitye hetuḥ nityāḥ vṛttiḥ sarvam anityāḥ ānantarīyaka āvṛttiḥ nityasya amūrta utpatti tvayoḥ mūrta sādhya pakṣa nityeṣu śrāvaṇa nityā nityatā prameya dharmaka nitye utpattimat jātīya sattā avidyamāna anityā anityasya kṛtakaḥ sarvadā abhāvāt prāk aprayatna bhūtvā dharmaḥ vyāpi vipakṣaḥ akṛtaka kṛtakam vidyut vyoma asiddham anityeṣu hetu niṣpattayaḥ upapatteḥ utpatteḥ vastu nityāt dharmasya anittya bhedi aindriyaka sāmānya sāmānyavat sataḥ buddhi anaikāntikam ādiḥ atyantam nityāni amūrtta vināśi anantarīyakaḥ ānantarīyakaḥ kadācid bhāvāt ubhaya sarvasya ātmanaḥ nityānām kāryatvāt viruddha akṛtakam viśeṣaṇa dhvaneḥ abhūtvā sādhāraṇaḥ san pakṣe viśeṣaṇā anityāni anta vyākhyāte tajjātīya ātma ānantarīyakam śabdāt ubhayānta aṅga dharmakam jātiḥ tvābhyām bheda akṛtakaḥ bāhya asiddhaḥ dharmiṇaḥ manase anityayoḥ viśeṣeṇa kūṭastha asmad aniti anabhidheya nityaiḥ asarva viruddhau pradhvaṃsa dharmau niyamāt paramāṇūnām tadvat asparśa avi pakṣaḥ ākāśam viṣāṇi anityatayā tāyām abhiprāyeṇa kāryatvam brūyāt tvā abhidhīyate avidya vyāpnoti abhavan utthaḥ dṛṣṭam dharmā etau sarvatra mūrtta pariṇāmi kṛtā ubhayoḥ nityebhyaḥ utpannasya asiddha sattvāt anuvarttane vināśya udāharaṇam uttha hetumat bhedāt yatna ghaṭasya aśrāvaṇa doṣaḥ sampratipattiḥ viruddham prāptaḥ kṛtakasya ucyamāne pauruṣeyam viśeṣaṇena jyeṣṭha pañcabhūta vijñāyate viśeṣavat parihāra kṛta nityena cākṣuṣa aniṣpadyamāna sāvayava vyāpī lābhāt adravyavat apetaḥ pratiṣedhye draṣṭavyāḥ viśleṣāt bhūta kiñca dhvaniḥ kam anutpanne viśeṣavataḥ prajñāpanīya sādhye prasaṅgāt upalakṣya kāryeṇa vāc bhāvena avyāpakaḥ īdṛśam śarīram āntarīyakam kāpila kṛtakeṣu nityatāyām vināśitā yoḥ vādinam āditi atri apaiti ādikaḥ āśritaḥ bhaṅgi anantaram virodhī anyena adhrauvyāt adhruvam kramajanmanaḥ pratyatna tāvantau viṣāṇavān paramāṇavaḥ avarodhāt anutpatti gaḍunā karaṇa anantarīyakam anityatā asarvaḥ abhavana ghaṭe pakṣīkṛta udāharaṇāni viśeṣya anaikāntika agandhavat apohataḥ dhruvā kāraṇavat niti gṛhyate vaktavyā pratyakṣa nivṛtteḥ vāyunā vidyamāna doṣāt avācyaḥ nāśitā sapakṣaḥ vyavadhi anantara vivakṣita svarūpe avirodhāt ghaṭāt abādhakam pratyākhyātaḥ anityānām ādima yuktau abhihitaḥ anātma sattva upādīyate śeṣaḥ dhvaninā ādimattvāt jātimat akṛtake ānantarīyake aṅgitā anityau catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ sanmātra vidyamānasapakṣaḥ pradhvaṃsaḥ pūrvaḥ dharmakasya viruddhāḥ asambhavi paramāṇu bhedāḥ anityebhyaḥ vyatiriktayā avirodhaḥ dvayam aniyatam
57	janma deha maraṇa utpādaḥ citta dehaḥ utpāda vikāra antara vijñāna āśrayaḥ vinā kāraṇam dehasya prāṇa saha hetuḥ sthitiḥ dadhi śarīra maraṇam vikāraḥ vijñānam pitṛ sthiti pūrva kṣīra putra hetu manaḥ cetasaḥ buddheḥ utpattiḥ saṃbhava āśraya para dehāt cittam nirodhaḥ saṃbhavaḥ santāna bhāvaḥ kadācid prasaṅgaḥ nivṛttau dehe utpādasya kāya vibhavaḥ vibhavau sthiteḥ avasthā hetoḥ vikriyā kāyaḥ bhūta āśritam caitanya madhya yuktam kasyacid staḥ bhāvasya tulyam vikāreṇa indriya cetasi vikāre tiṣṭhati vaikalyāt prajñā cittasya sarvadā avasthāyām buddhi śarīram upalabhyate nivṛttiḥ kāṣṭha utpatti syātām vikārāt loka ādinā janmanaḥ tau utpādayet sambhavaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ putraḥ vijñānasya apānau āśrayi mātā upādāna śakti harṣa prabodha abhāve nirhrāsa prabhā saṃcāraḥ mahābhūta buddhiḥ āgatiḥ caitanyam anivṛtti vikāri anyonya śarīrāt upakāriṇī cetaḥ dṛśyate prahāra iṣyate jvālā vijñānāt abhyāsa nivṛtte avasthānam apara abhāvāt utpādam mṛtasya śarīrayoḥ nakha prāṇāḥ kāraṇa saṃbhavena śaktiḥ sphaṭika pariṇati āyuḥ paścāt jāta apāna puṣṭi aṅga nirodha prāṇi śarīrasya hemni santatau taruṣu śoka saṃbhavam vidyate vartti upādānam avasthayā gati mṛte antareṇa āśrayeṇa adṛṣṭeḥ manda kāyāt cikitsā utpatteḥ kevalasya āśvāsa kṛtaḥ śarīre anāśrayāt dehena taikṣṇya maraṇāt mṛtaḥ ga jāyate utpadyamānaḥ kaṇṭaka avinirbhāga vāsaka cittāt pratisandhāna garbha animittataḥ punarbhāvaḥ śoṣa tāmra citra arthinaḥ sthitam jāyamāna vāsya utpādena asyāḥ vibhavena sannidheḥ sthānam viṣa anutpannaḥ janayiṣyati uttaram matam niranvaya uditam jala vyavasthita sambhave utpādayati antarāt kṣīram maraṇe pitroḥ nirudhyamānasya ujjīvanam abhāvaḥ akṣaiḥ kāyasya madhyastha vaśya anivṛttiḥ pūrvaḥ bhaṅgānām gomayāt utpadyate pradīpa nāma apūrvasya buddhim indriyāt mūla vināśau vaikalyam bhāvāt sthātuḥ tulya viśeṣaḥ nirudhyate kuḍya indriyāṇām varti ādyasya saṃśrayāt santānasya āgataḥ antarasya mada anuvartanam avikāreṇa maraṇayoḥ ujjīvana utpannasya upi anyat iṣṭeḥ dṛṣṭā hema abhava apānayoḥ maulena vicchedaḥ kā jā yuktaḥ sāmya nirapekṣāṇām antaram anuvartate apagacchati anyayā taila karmma mṛta vinaśyati janmani paratas asandhānam jñānaiḥ utpattau anyā buddhīndriya bhāva parigrahe saṃcāra vikāram akṣa śoṇita janayati āśritā naśyet bhāvena śeṣavat maulam saṃjñitasya vibhavam utpādau vijñānānām upādeya dīpa niṣiddhaḥ asat āhāra upaghāta prabodhaḥ sammatam utpannaḥ avidyamānaḥ
58	artha saṃyogāt karma eka prakṛti guṇa darśanāt vikāraḥ liṅga vacanāt śruti kāla vikāra śeṣa pradhāna pratīyeta sarva vighna codanā vidhi nirdeśāt anya aniyamaḥ darśanam aviśeṣāt vidhānāt vikalpaḥ śabda sāmānyāt vaiguṇyāt prayoga bhūta phala bhedāt dravya aṅgānām aṅga pṛthaktvāt karmaṇaḥ tulya mukhya prayogaḥ arthena pratiṣedhaḥ maṅgala vipratiṣedhāt samāpti apūrva arthavat deśa akarma śiṣṭa viśeṣāt ante vaiguṇyam itarat kratu maṅgalam śrutiḥ syuḥ tadvat abhidhāna upadeśāt aśruti arthasya aika niyamyeta prakṛtau guṇānām tantra abhāvāt itarasya iṣṭi kartṛ adhika vidhiḥ vādaḥ samuccayaḥ ākhyā vākya vikṛtau vidheḥ tādarthyāt ikāraḥ arthaḥ anarthakam sarveṣām śruteḥ adhikāraḥ codana vivṛddhiḥ prakṛteḥ mantra pṛṣṭha loka vikārāḥ vacanam nimitta pratiṣedhāt prayoge vipratiṣiddham dharma avikāraḥ kṛta utpatti bhāvāt sama sambandhāt asaṃyogāt pradhāne kṛtārtha nyāya śabdyāt ārambha bhedaḥ pradāna antare codanāt saṃyogaḥ arthāḥ mātram samavāyāt devatā vidhīnām codita sāmarthyāt prakaraṇa saṃskāraḥ pravṛttiḥ antara upadeśaḥ darśayati prayāja śeṣaḥ utpattau avibhāgāt niyamaḥ yakāraḥ śabdaḥ ijyā arthe varṇa dvi śāstram ubhayoḥ lopaḥ pūrvavat niyama anyāya abhisambandhāt ubhaya pradhānam mithas saṃskāra kriyeta itara anuṣṭhānam abhisambandhaḥ bhaktyā abhyāsaḥ niṣpatteḥ abhidhānam tantram nitya gaṇe vikāre samāptiḥ ānarthakyam ekasya aśāstra prākṛta nyāyyaḥ prayukta ātreyaḥ avikārāt sakṛt itareṣām prāyaścitta vyapadeśāt śrutau avipratiṣedhāt antareṣu yajña paśu pūrva yajñe ājya samāpteḥ śiṣṭānām karmaṇi bhāvaḥ ekasmin asamavāyāt artham liṅgāt ānantaryāt lopāt stoma yukte prayogasya hetu anarthakaḥ pātra avibhakta vibhakta abhāve prākṛtasya kriyā abhyāsena sannidhānāt apakṛṣyeta itas arthavān praśaṃsā anyāyya arthānām saṃśaye anuvādaḥ parārtha para dharmaḥ nānā sthāne arthava ārabdha vacana codanāyām ānantaryam saṃskārasya prakṛtyā upapadyate saṃyoge deśaḥ aṅgam abhisaṃyogāt viśaye iṣṭiḥ kāmanayā maṅgale prākṛtānām bhājām iṣṭeḥ samavāye kartuḥ arthāt madhye aśabda ādeśa agni sarvāsām vṛddhiḥ yūpa utpatteḥ codyante śiṣṭam codyate sarvaiḥ pṛthak sthānāt aviśiṣṭa itareṣu pareṣu aṅgeṣu āpatti ācāra ācārāt acodanā madhya avadāna gāmi prabhu apratiṣedhaḥ haviḥ anārabhya virodhe saṃkhyā bādhaḥ vyavasthā arthavāda arthā acodana avibhāge prāripsita tadākhyam pramatta prayuktaḥ tāsām atad yathāśruti bādarāyaṇaḥ āpti vivṛddhau saṃyuktam saṅkhyā anyaiḥ pradhānasya vipratipattau naimittikam dravyeṣu apravṛttiḥ
59	vināśaḥ dvi vināśāt utpattiḥ dravya apekṣā utpatti vināśa utpadyate buddheḥ vināśe utpādaḥ guṇa utpadyamāna saṃyoga vinaśyattā kāraṇa kāle aṇuka saṃyogasya kālam buddhi jñānasya kālaḥ ekaḥ sama tantu tasmin śyāma prakrameṇa piṇḍa buddhiḥ utpattau vinaśyati ārambhaka sāmānya vibhāgāt paratva guṇasya pūrva pāka yasmin aṇukasya rakta paratvasya agni antarāt antara utpanna anantaram saṃyogāt krameṇa yugapad karma dravye dravyasya kāryasya kāraṇam diś utpāde vibhāgasya tri kārya vināśena vibhāga aṇukam asamavāyi nivṛttau utpatteḥ pārthiva uttara kriyate sannikṛṣṭa āśraya aṇuke paramāṇuṣu pūrvam ghātaka kāla samavāyi anutpatti vināśasya vibhāgaḥ apekṣya śata utpadyante paramāṇu avasthāne karmaṇā paramāṇau avasthānam ārabhate dve aṇu virodhi vinaṣṭe smaraṇasya utpadyam avayave nitya ekasmin vadhya abhāvāt jñānāt vinaśyatta utpannam pratiṣedhāt saṃyogebhyaḥ eka vināśau buddhyoḥ jeṣu vibhāgam avayava utpannā pradeśena viprakṛṣṭa ādhāre vibhāgebhyaḥ utpanne pṛthaktva ja dvitīya āśritasya jñāna kṛtvā saṃskārasya kāraṇāt tebhyaḥ ārambhaḥ karmaṇoḥ nivṛttiḥ paramāṇavaḥ prāktana aṃśu apekṣayā saha anutpattiḥ paramāṇunā aparatvayoḥ avaśyam piṇḍayoḥ rūpa jāḥ anupalabdheḥ aṇukāni aṇukayoḥ antare paratvam utpādaka vinaṣṭaḥ antar jaiḥ saṃyogau pūrvarūpa karoti sambhavati sānnidhyam pratikṣaṇam sambandhāt prasaṅgaḥ alpīyaḥ avatiṣṭhate ārabdhaḥ kṣaṇa pakva prādurbhāvāt utpadya paramāṇoḥ pākaḥ samavāyinaḥ anye kriyā kṣaṇe utpādāt ānatā vinaśyanti ghaṭasya vinaśyat saṃyukta pūrvasya guṇayoḥ śvaitya saṃskārāt bhūyaḥ avināśāt sambandhebhyaḥ ucchedaka āśu rūḍha uttarottara anutpattau ādhāra ārabhyate upajātam ava vācyam vināśam ārabdhasya anutpannasya gatau vivaraṇam tvebhyaḥ avadhim avināśaḥ eṣām tiṣṭhati apekṣāt svatantreṣu paramāṇubhyaḥ pākaja kṛtayoḥ utpadyete vinaśyatā yūni nimitta param ekasyām vi avasthānāt jñānañca nirhetuka aṇukaiḥ anutpanna sahitebhyaḥ dravyam aṃśau āma āśutara piṇḍe saṃyogābhyām abhighātāt āśrayayoḥ avasthāyi itaretara adoṣaḥ buddhim anavasthāna kriyāyāḥ pakṣe kāraṇasya jātīyayoḥ aṇukāṇvoḥ ārambhakasya avinaśyatoḥ sthavire utpādikāyāḥ utpādau draṣṭuḥ ārambha etasmāt paraspara bhūte avināśi viśiṣṭam paramāṇuḥ ārambhakeṣu sannikṛṣṭā vināśāḥ paramāṇvoḥ utpāda kapāla dravyeṣu tantuka vināśayoḥ āna bhoginām kramasya asambhavāt nāśāt saṃyogaḥ ākāśa utpadyamānam anyasya deśena pārthivena praveśāt antareṇa karmabhyaḥ mahān vidyamānasya piṇḍasya aparatvasya ārambhake kāṇu karpāse palita śvaityāt vīraṇayoḥ dvāreṇa nyāyena antarasya apareṇa yāvat aśeṣa śveta parivartana tantau vināśābhyām vināśakam
60	nigraha sthānam pratijñā doṣa sādhana hetu doṣaḥ pakṣa uttara vacanam sthāna uttaram vādinaḥ dūṣaṇam artha asādhana vādī udbhāvanam doṣam dūṣaṇa vādi nigṛhyate pratijña parājaya abhidhānam apratipattiḥ nirdeśaḥ anaikāntika mata antaram anujñā pratijñāyāḥ nāma para apratibhā tris pratiṣedhe aṅga pakṣe adhikam kathā abhidhānāt prativādinā vacana prativādinaḥ hetvābhāsa samānaḥ pratijñām avayava ajñānam nyūnam pratijñāta artham ābhāsa vādinā gata vipratipattiḥ abhidhāne prasaṅga pratiṣedha hāniḥ punarvacanam kathām nyūna udāharaṇa sthāne nigrahaḥ ananubhāṣaṇam pratijñāntaram doṣāḥ prasaṅgaḥ antara prakṛta pakṣam nigṛhītaḥ samyak pakṣaḥ jāti sādhanasya prativādī brūyāt parājayaḥ aindriyaka pṛthak vikalpāt pūrva ukte apasiddhāntaḥ aṅgam paryanuyojya vipratipatti sādhane vādinam vaktavyam sādhanam pratijñāhāniḥ abhyupetya jaya kiṃcid abhihitasya upādānāt prayukte aindriyakam abhihitam ṣaṣ upekṣaṇam sthānāni nigraham niranuyojya upanyāsa kathāyām adoṣa vikṣepaḥ aṅgasya prasaṅgam bhavān nirdeśa pratiṣiddhe asarva abhyupagamya abhyupagamāt nirarthakam aparijñānāt vācyam asiddha punaruktam pakṣasya avijñāta parājīyate vākye dvis mayā anuyogaḥ bravīti arhaḥ pratiṣedham nigamanam tṛtīya vipratiṣedhe upādāne hetvābhāsāḥ kālam prapañca vacane hīnam upanaya ādibhiḥ anujānāti samarthanam abhidhānena hetau kṛte anye aprāpta abhidhatte hetoḥ dvayoḥ prayogaḥ vādini arhati ekasya arthāt siddhāntam prayogam asambaddham uttarasya asi apratipatti anarthakam arthasya pariṣadā yuktam jahāti vivakṣayā dvitīyasya dṛṣṭānta ubhayoḥ prativādinoḥ bahu ava anaikāntikaḥ parājayau pareṇa avijñātam kṛtvā adhika pratijñāyām āpannasya uktāḥ hetum nyāya aprastuta dhetu prayuṅkte vacanāt upādānam cauraḥ udbhāvyate vacasi prayoga caturtha nyāyyam eke uttareṇa dve vādinoḥ antareṇa gataḥ prasajyate siddheḥ duṣṭa kasyacid udbhāvana vacanena vāde anubhāṣaṇam anuddhṛtya apratibhayā apratipattyā apratyuccāraṇam nigamane anabhidhānāt avaśyam pariṣad vyartham uttare upanyāsaḥ sāmarthya bhidyate parājitaḥ dūṣaṇe anyat anyatarasya viśeṣam anyatamena bruvan vadati asāmarthyāt pratyavasthitaḥ ayukta adoṣaḥ prayogāt apekṣi prayoge pūrvasya uttarāṇi vaktuḥ pratipādita śiṣyaḥ dvāreṇa vivāda pralāpa pratipattiḥ ekena ajñāna doṣasya anigraha apratipattyoḥ dvāviṃśati pratijñāsannyāsaḥ abhūta sādhanāya vivādaḥ aviśeṣāt avacanam dharmam asamyak udbhāvanā udbhāvayati udbhāvite asāmarthyam pratijñāya nirdeśe anityaḥ tādavasthyāt tūṣṇīm udbhāvanāt samarthana bhūta aniyamāt viparyāsa sarvam pratipādana puruṣa veditavyam udbhāvane doṣān pakṣī karoti antā saṃgraha avayavānām atidruta parṣadā vijñātasya virodhaḥ jayaḥ abhyanujñā aparasya siddhaye
61	kriyā kāraka kartṛ karaṇa karma artha vyāpāra vyāpāraḥ dhātu karaṇam karoti pacati kriyāyāḥ kriyām kārakam bhāvanā kartā kriyāyām ākhyāta arthaḥ karmaṇi yatna pāka kartuḥ phala kriyayā vyāpārasya vyāpāreṇa vyāpāram pākaḥ phalam kartari ghaṭam sādhanam mātram sādhakatama kartrā karaṇayoḥ kārakāṇām yā karmaṇaḥ pratyaya kriyāḥ tasyāḥ kārakāṇi arthasya anupapatteḥ pratīyate prayojaka vartamāna upasarga paraśu sthālī vyapadeśaḥ devadatta ākhyātasya abhidhīyate sādhana karaṇasya antareṇa prati odanam antara ākhyātam kriye dhātoḥ dhātunā kṛtam jvalana karaṇe caitraḥ taṇḍula karttṛ kārakasya sādhakatamam kāle chinatti mātreṇa bhūtā acetane gamana pākam apākṣīt pakṣyati phalasya savya pradhāna vṛkṣam kāṣṭha karmaṇā chidi bhāvanāyāḥ vācyaḥ gacchati upādānāt dhātuḥ kartāram pacanti atiśayaḥ vya yuktam artham akriyā prayojya prayojakaḥ abhidhīyamāna dhātvarthaḥ jani viklitti sambandhaḥ puruṣasya kurvanti ādinā sākṣāt anukūlaḥ samartham pratītiḥ jānāti vyāpāravat abhidhānāt yatnaḥ yatnasya bhāvāt dvidhā ati mātra caitreṇa sādhanānām vṛkṣaḥ vyatirekeṇa anukūla kriyaḥ sārtha yajate pratītau vivakṣāyām odana saṅgatiḥ dadhānam taṇḍulaḥ viklidyanti vyāpāre akārakam taṇḍulam jñāpakaḥ ekasyām utpādayati vibhāgena svātantryam rathaḥ spanda ātmanā upādānaḥ ādīni īpsitatamam niṣpatti kārakeṇa paraśoḥ matam aparā utpattau utpādaka viśeṣaṇa jñāpakam pacyate ākṣepāt avyāpāra karoteḥ kriyāṇām bhūta apāram kārake ākhyātena kriyāsu vācinaḥ bhāvyate antasya kriyātaḥ devadattaḥ doṣaḥ arthāt ātmā kuṭhāra bhāvya yad pratyayena abhidhānam adhigamana adhiśrayaṇa dhātvartha karotinā kāṣṭhaiḥ nipātāḥ pratyayavatī saṃpradāna śīghratara tiṅanteṣu sādhane kasya kāritva puṃsaḥ tulya anumeyā chidā bhavana svātantrya kārakayoḥ udyamana utpādanā viśeṣaḥ mā sthitau āptum karttuḥ vaśāt vyāpriyate arthā pratīteḥ vācye vācyā ābhāti apāra avacchedāt bhāvanām kariṣyati labdha pākasya viṣaya bhāvayati bhavantī paceḥ paraśunā udyamya bhuṅkte pāke tasyām karmaṇām vācya pumān abhyupagamāt sarva kartṛkeṣu taṇḍulāḥ ātmanaḥ vidyate ādiḥ prasaṅgaḥ anādhāra anyat pratipadyate adhikaraṇyena nirvyāpāra odanasya pacyante jānāmi aneka sakala svātantryāt karmaṇī antarebhyaḥ ityādayaḥ vivakṣā yogāt akāraka pratyayayoḥ vivakṣyate svayam avyāpāre śu parispanda sarveṣām nibandhanam vāci sādhyam chedana vihanti kartāraḥ prādhānyena bhedāt parispandaḥ atirikta jñātṛ garbhaḥ ātmani ākhyaḥ apādānam sarvasyāḥ vivaraṇāt yam patati īpsitatama karmatā nirvṛtti ubhayatra arthena ādhāraḥ lopaḥ abhipraiti pracayasya cetana
62	kāla yugapad kālaḥ krama pūrva diś apara deśa kṣaṇa krameṇa eka sakṛt aneka kālasya kramaḥ kālam kāle pratyaya dīrgha kṣaṇika yaugapadya uttara ekaḥ cira antara varṇṇa kṣaṇaḥ kālayoḥ buddhīnām niyamaḥ āśu kālena vartamāna samāna diśaḥ aviśeṣāt avicchinna kramāt ayugapad buddhiḥ pratyayāḥ sarva abhāvāt vicchinnam kṣipra āditya kṛtam antare patra vartamānaḥ ekasya abhimānaḥ utpatti jñānāni bhāvi yaugapadyam uttaraḥ pratyayānām apekṣayā viccheda bhāvinaḥ ākrama tulya kālau saha parāpara utpāda akrama nānā yaugapadye cireṇa vyavadhāne nirantara avasthā cakra nimitta kramavatī udayaḥ laghu liṅga avadhi bhavanti utpattiḥ nimittam ūrdhvam vṛtteḥ nānātva kriyā graha alāta vyākhyātā bhinna atītaḥ tau grāhi pūrveṇa kramam mātrā asambhavāt ekena avicchinnam ekaika mataḥ kramavat sphaṭike kālāḥ ekasmin atīta māsa savituḥ yaugapadyena kṣaṇikāḥ vicchinna diśi ekā abhimāna kāryya varṇṇaḥ utpanna aparaḥ prācī śata ekadā jñānānām krame acira nānātvam sāmarthya lava pūrvaḥ ciram akrameṇa buddhayaḥ sama kālatā vyapadeśāt bahūnām paurvāparya pūrvam vajra kṣaṇena bahu utpannayoḥ hrasva vṛttau dvau dhvaniḥ dvayoḥ vyavadhānena kṛta utpala avadhim anantara vyapadeśaḥ bhāvinoḥ sakala yuga liṅgānām utpattimatām vyavadhānāt liṅgāni anyatva bhāgaḥ kadācid bhaviṣyati udayāt akramāt aparatvam uttareṇa jñāna viṣaya dakṣiṇa tila ā dvaya bhedena avirodhāt vibhramaḥ astamaya pradīpa prathama paścāt sambhavaḥ akramaḥ nimeṣa vyavadhānam anyatra prabandha pratikṣaṇam antya padārtha vicchedaḥ kṣaṇe kṣaṇāt aniyamāt kṣaṇayoḥ vyavahitasya aviccheda pratyayaḥ kalā atītasya buddhim avabhāsaḥ kārya āsakti vyatikara vijātīya jñānayoḥ yad sthāyi samānam dīrghaḥ paurvāparyam utpannaḥ sthiti lāghava lāghavam diśām manvantara unnāma uttarasya hetuḥ kṣipram kṣaṇasya kālāt manasaḥ dvis upacaya upādhi viśeṣeṇa avasthita varṇṇānām daśa vyavahāraḥ devadattasya sthāyinaḥ dakṣiṇena udaya traya anudayaḥ āsakta ante anutpattiḥ nakṣatra sthitiḥ ādiḥ kriyāḥ pratyuktam kāryāṇām aikyam ālayāt kramavantaḥ kramiṇaḥ eke bhavataḥ adhyavasāyaḥ janmanoḥ sthite sarvāḥ vyavasyati nartakī nirantaram mūrteṣu vṛtti aparā jñānaiḥ anekam pratyayau dṛṣṭau pañcabhiḥ saṃvatsara vicchinne ekam kramasya yaugapadyāt pūrvasya sthitaḥ vayaḥ avasthitasya kiñca akramam vilakṣaṇānām śṛṅga kāraṇe pratyayasya utpadyante vyavahāra siddhāḥ avicchedaḥ aniyata bahavaḥ bhavantī dīrghagrāhikā muhūrta purva unnāmau pratyāyakam jātīye ekatra bhedāt
63	vākya pada artha varṇa padārtha vākyam padam arthaḥ varṇāḥ padāni krama varṇānām vākyasya artham padānām saṃsargaḥ antya saṃsarga padasya padārthānām kramaḥ divā ānupūrvī sphoṭa padārthaḥ samūhaḥ pratīti rātri vivakṣā sphoṭaḥ pūrva varṇaḥ dvitīya vākyāt uccāraṇa pratipattiḥ vākye padārthāḥ padaiḥ vākyena padeṣu pade arthasya pratītiḥ bhuṅkte varṇeṣu daśa uccāraṇam saṃhatya prathama pratīyate kriyā antara vyutpattiḥ racanā śabda samudāyaḥ antaram arthe gauḥ padārthebhyaḥ pratipatteḥ aśvaḥ pratyayaḥ gakāra vākyeṣu anvita abhihita padena varṇebhyaḥ viśiṣṭa padārthe padārtheṣu antareṇa vācaka śabdaḥ ākāṅkṣā anye pratipādaka saṃskāra varṇe padebhyaḥ dāḍima pratipatti mātram kramasya padāt avagamyate pratyekam kārya gām bhojana vācakam kalpanā eka padārtham dhvani pīnaḥ eṣām puruṣa abhidhānam ekam śuklaḥ vākyānām mā pīna krameṇa sarva antyaḥ śabdāt avagati pṛthak avagatiḥ śrutau padārthaiḥ pratīteḥ dhāvati prayujyate samudāya avagamaḥ gamayanti saṃsṛṣṭaḥ samūha samasta sāmastyam ākāṅkṣa saṃbandha vyutpatti pratyaya anukrama varṇasya padārthasya anupapatteḥ bhūt apārthakam āvāpa pratipādanam dvāreṇa uddhṛtya vākyāni siddheḥ akṣarāṇi kṛṣṇa viśiṣṭaḥ vyavasthānam avadhāraṇam śvetaḥ satyam bhavantī pratyāyaka yauga abhidhīyate vācakaḥ pūrvaka pratipādakāḥ samastānām vācakāḥ varṇṇānām dhvanayaḥ anyaḥ śravaṇe udeti śruta vyasta śukla paurvāparya uccāraṇe vākyayoḥ prayujyamānam asaṃbaddha abhidhātrī racanāyāḥ ānīyatām varṇān asatyām padārthān ananvita āśrīyate abhidhāne anvitam abhidheyasya avagacchati udvāpa avācaka abhidadhati ekaḥ yad paraspara anuvādaka prakṛti vibhāgaḥ arthena āśrayā śrotra ekām pratipādana saṃkalanā varṇṇebhyaḥ arthavat samanvayaḥ buddhau janita abhihitānām prativākyam aṅgam ānupūrvyā svara vaśāt vyāpāra viparyayeṇa sarvatra arthāpattiḥ avagamāt abhyāja ityādiṣu uccāraṇāt pratipādane prathamam pratipattim abhidhāya kāraka avabodhakāḥ sphoṭam sphoṭasya śuklām buddhyā anyathā vikalpa cintyate kramāḥ gakāraḥ bhāga devadatta kṛtsna ākhyāta kramam saṃsṛṣṭa rātrau buddhiḥ prayuktam atiriktaḥ abhāvāt vyavahārāt antar pika prakaraṇa viṣayām yaugapadyam kalpanayā abhidhāyi śrute avasthite saṃsṛṣṭāḥ rūpam itaretara tulyā saraḥ anugamaḥ pāramārthikaḥ aukāra avācakam avagatāḥ bhedaḥ ānarthakyam anupapanna asatyam apratisambaddha prativarṇam racana vyāpārāṇi guṇa anuraktaḥ anantara bhāvena nivṛtta śrutyā pratyāyakaḥ parasparam śravaṇāt anvayaḥ anavagata akṣāḥ padya ādhikyam aśravaṇāt padā samūhasya vyāpāre ādadhāti asaṃsargaḥ varṇāt lipi pauruṣeyī bhojanam uccarita pratipādakam avarṇa sārthaka sāmarthyam khura
64	citta cittam kleśa cittasya vijñānam kāya samādhi dharma aham prajñā ālaya kuśala mārga vijñāna sarva karma kleśāḥ cetasaḥ nirodha samādhiḥ ālambana vedanā dāna moha pariṇāmaḥ dṛṣṭi dhyāna vijñapti pañca puṇya vipāka yoginaḥ mārge saṃjñā ātma akuśala utpadyate dharmāḥ kula śānta saṃniśraya rāga mahā vāc bhagavān yoga avasthā vimukti yāvat upaśamaḥ kāma kāyasya kliṣṭam jñāna karmakaḥ manaḥ asmi saṃskārāḥ dhātuḥ darśana cetanā duḥkha mānaḥ arhat viveka mañjuśrīḥ prahāṇam ālambanam avacara sākṣāt śraddhā grāha nirodhe nāma adhyātmam śīla asmitā mṛdu ārūpya kṣānti samāpattiḥ sat yā eṣām kuśalāḥ avipraṇāśaḥ prahīyate duḥkhe mārgeṇa vijñānasya pravartate pratipakṣaḥ kuśalaḥ dagdha puṇyam kṛtyam gati caturthaḥ phala avidyā dhāraṇā upāyaḥ pudgala aṅgāni catvāraḥ āyuṣmantaḥ kuśalānām saṃprayujyate lakṣaṇaḥ sadā prahāṇāt saṃyamaḥ vipākaḥ cetaḥ mitra tṛtīyaḥ ākāra saṃyamāt mārgaḥ vāsanā kṛtvā bījam bhūmiḥ nirodhaḥ bandhaḥ dveṣa cittena kliṣṭa mate bhāvanā parijñā samāpatti āvaraṇa skandhāḥ kuśalam uparaktam bhava upekṣā āśaya ālambane saṃkalpa madhya etāḥ labhate nairātmya anuśaya kleśeṣu vijñaptiḥ daśa prasādaḥ vijñaptimātra bhaya jātaḥ adhimātra caittāḥ nivṛta saṃskāra tṛṣṇā vicikitsā ālambanaḥ mā ekāgra karmikā jñeya ātmānam kāyaḥ lābha ādibhiḥ ṣaṣ arhan saṃsāram bīja avijñaptayaḥ samudaye bhikṣu jayaḥ kleśānām kṣaṇāḥ karmakam vyutthāna pratyayaḥ karmaṇaḥ dharmam avocan lābhaḥ anugraha avocat veditavyaḥ sparśa mama pratipakṣa bhavanti jāla sattvānām rūpa yathābhūta caturbhiḥ adhivacanam āsrava kliṣṭe sakṛdāgāmi satkāra upadhi saṃsāra vipākam satya vijñānāt ākhyam bahis daurmanasya koṭim prahāṇataḥ vitarka imām vāsanāḥ me nirvāṇa bhūta sattvāḥ sapta kṣaṇaḥ pratyāhāra spandana cittaḥ kṣīṇa pañcabhiḥ dvaya eṣā manasi cakṣuḥ dvitīyaḥ bhagavantam svarūpa āgamya akuśalāḥ cetayitvā kaukṛtyam kleśaiḥ kṣāntiḥ maitram paribhoga pathāḥ prāṇāyāma samāpannam unnatiḥ trividhaḥ śeṣaḥ imam sūkṣmaḥ bhūmi kalyāṇa kleśān saṃjñinaḥ sthiti vidhūta krodha āyatana śruta kāyena śvāsa tasmin jñānam yogena vīryam uktaḥ parāvṛttiḥ pramādaḥ ānantarya utpannaḥ dhyānam vihāraḥ yathākramam bhagavataḥ prakāraḥ avidyāyām kumāra duścarita nirmitakau pratyāhāraḥ saṃtrāsam skandhasya upaśamasya samudaya sattvaḥ sattveṣu cetasi mānasam pariṇāma dṛṣṭvā vijñāne ālayavijñānam utthāya yogaḥ ayan vikṣepa ātmīya sukhā traidhātuka dharmaiḥ vāsanām
65	śabda deśa śabdaḥ śabdasya śrotra ākāśa ākāśam sarva deśe vyañjaka śrotram santāna deśaḥ samāna karṇa tīvra abhivyakti manda bherī dūra deśam śabdam ākāśasya abhivyaktiḥ santānaḥ vāyu śaṣkulī sarvatra upalabhyate śabdānām nabhaḥ dhvani śabde saṃyoga vyaṅgya pradeśa saṃskāraḥ abhivyaktau abhivyajyate vṛtti vīṇā varṇa āvaraṇa tāra śaṅkha anyatra chāyā vyajyate vyaktiḥ śrotreṇa anupalabdheḥ
