stham abhāvāt guṇaḥ prayatna sarvaiḥ vyaṃjaka gatvā pratiniyata ākāśe samīpa avyāpya ghaṇṭā mandaḥ eka vyañjakam pavana deśasya śravaṇa śabdāḥ gṛhyate mandam vyañjakaḥ gata avasthita upapatteḥ indriya sthasya antaram gatam nāda ghaṭa sarveṣām upalambhaḥ abhibhavaḥ antare śabdāt saṃskāra vāyoḥ asambhavāt daṇḍa antara śuka vyañcaka vāyuḥ yugapad vāyunā uccāraṇāt nānā gakāraḥ vīcī niyamaḥ sparśavat gakāra vyavadhāna tālu saṃskṛtam upalabdheḥ stha antarāla pradeśaḥ avacchinne śabdeṣu ādhāra śabdān vyaṅgyaḥ prayatnena upalabdhiḥ avasthitam pradīpa śrūyate nitya dūre upalabdhi śravaṇam vyoma anupalabdhi vyāpaka samavāyena prasaṅgaḥ pakṣe pradeśāḥ nyāyena ārabhate nabhasaḥ āgamanāt mukha antarāṇi sthaḥ sthena utkarṣa deśeṣu gataḥ kolāhala tāraḥ śruti deśāḥ pāṭana avasthānam yuktam avacchedena vṛttyā grāhya ādiḥ ākāśaḥ mukham deśān veṇu nikaṭa abhivyañjaka anantara pāṇi śabdena vyakti upalabhyeta āgamanam asarva śīghra ekaḥ niyata abhivyaktaḥ deśānām grahaṇam saṃskṛta dhvanīnām vyaṃjakaḥ vyañjakena vyāpi dṛṣṭam pratyāsatti dhvaneḥ kuḍya guṇa kakāra upalabhyamāna saṃskāram sarve prāpnoti antarāle avarṇa vyañjakasya sthāna kalpanā deśena agrahaṇam abhivyakteḥ upapadyate pradeśe utpatti vartinaḥ abhibhava santānena mandasya sanniviṣṭaḥ vyañjakānām ekatra gacchati grāhyaḥ prayatnasya vaktṛ śrotrasya ārambhaḥ bhāvena anupalambhāt upalambha teṣu abhāvaḥ saṃyogasya pūraṇa vyomnaḥ paṭa nimitta abhi śrotre dīpa grahaṇa tīvraḥ saṃśleṣaḥ uccāraṇe vyāpinaḥ kaṇṭha bhāve mukhasya vyavahitānām kalakale tantrī avasthitaḥ jvālā vṛttinā māruta tīvram sataḥ ādhāraḥ aśravaṇa deśā vyajyante āśrayaḥ antya stimita āloka anantaram upalabdhaḥ niyamena marutām pratyabhijñā upacārāt anavayavam chāyāyāḥ śaṣkulīm vyañjakeṣu kṛtvas ādyaḥ ālokaḥ vyavadhānam vibhu abhāve ādya grāhyāṇām vṛttiḥ ati diś amūrtā kala vyañjakāni udaka preritaḥ ambara vyañjakāḥ avacchinnaḥ preraṇam anya dṛśyate mūrta abhisambadhyate anaikāntaḥ vibhāgāḥ aviśeṣāt gṛhṇāti dūrāt dṛṣṭaḥ aindriyaka saṃskṛtaḥ vāyavaḥ utpannaḥ ātmakena saṃskṛtasya sphuṭam grahaṇāt jātīya vigamaḥ
66	saṃśayaḥ viśeṣa saṃśaya dharma samāna viśeṣaḥ sāmānya sthāṇu dharmaḥ darśanāt ubhaya asādhāraṇaḥ upapatteḥ aneka saṃśayasya sādhāraṇa saṃśaye artha viruddha apekṣaḥ saṃśayam viṣaya ubhayathā sthāṇuḥ puruṣa antara viśeṣasya avyavasthā asādhāraṇa vipratipatteḥ viparyaya puruṣaḥ ubhayoḥ hetuḥ vimarśaḥ kāraṇam sādhāraṇaḥ anupalabdhi tulya nirṇaya dṛṣṭa dṛṣṭam adhyavasāyāt upalabdhi sandeha anavadhāraṇa avyavasthātaḥ hetu viṣaye nirṇayaḥ sandehaḥ ūrdhva pratyayaḥ āhosvit dharmi śabde anyatara dvaya dharmasya dṛṣṭaḥ śiraḥ dharmiṇi uta arthaḥ ātmakaḥ saṃśayāt vipratipatti ekatra viśeṣam sāmānyam samastam viśeṣān darśanam śrāvaṇa tasmin mātra asamāna pada sādhāraṇam padena sāmānyena asādhāraṇasya niścaya viparyayaḥ dvayoḥ sthāṇau puruṣayoḥ asādhāraṇam koṭi asparśavat sandigdhaḥ samānaḥ san gandhavat anusmaraṇāt jātīyeṣu kāraṇa anadhyavasāya pratyekam vipratipattiḥ pāṇi bhūteṣu avadhāraṇa saha darśana vyāvṛtta atyanta śāstre lakṣaṇam ubhayatra antaram ātmaka upalabhyate pṛthak viśeṣeṣu darśane anupalabdheḥ viśeṣāḥ anadhyavasāyaḥ jātīya ādibhyaḥ gataḥ viśeṣāṇām parigraheṇa lakṣaṇaḥ viruddhayoḥ dharmāt anyatarasya samānam pratyakṣāt vicāraḥ vakra avyabhicāri sannipāte ākāṅkṣā gata saṃśayena pratyayasya upalabdhaḥ anayoḥ dharmam mātram smṛti smaraṇa sūtra antare avadhārayati kiṃsvid viśeṣeṇa apratyakṣāt vimarśa anekaḥ hetū prati anadhyavasitaḥ ekasmin ātmani satyām upalambhāt anyaḥ smṛteḥ sādhaka adhyavasāyaḥ sambhavati jāyate eke dvaita dvividhaḥ dvayasya saṃśete sādhāraṇasya kecid dvaividhyāt anupalambhāt anavadhāraṇam adharmāt ayathā viśeṣaiḥ grahaṇāt kriyāvat pūrva svarūpa udāharaṇam anupalabdhe vakṣyāmaḥ dharmayoḥ bhavatu upalabdhe dvābhyām dharmī svid viśeṣe koṭara janaka antar sahacaritaḥ aviśeṣa hetutvāt hetutvam samyak viparyayau parīkṣyate vyabhicāri anyatra sampratipattiḥ asambhavāt upalabhamānasya vacanaḥ anutpādaka sthaḥ jātīyayoḥ abhidhānam avyavasthāyāḥ saṃhatayoḥ viparyayābhyām sarveṣu viparyastaḥ anirṇītaḥ asaṃśayaḥ puruṣe vipratipattau dṛṣṭe anavasthita smaraṇāt anupalabdhī utpatteḥ upalabdha acākṣuṣa atasmin sāmānye kinnu dharmiṇaḥ āho utpattau abhipretam anupapannaḥ upanipātaḥ yathādṛṣṭam mātrāt sāmānyasya mātrasya ekatara saṃbhāvanā ubhayasya anupalabhyamāne tulyam pratyaya jñātṛ sampratyayaḥ vyāvṛttaḥ avaruddhaḥ keli ūhā dhanam jātīyebhyaḥ pratyakṣa samasta nivartate apekṣā ja puruṣeṇa nirṇayasya āroha vyastam etāvatā dharmiṇam asādhāraṇe dvaye sāmyena vaśena dharmiṇī samāne amūrtam vilakṣaṇaḥ anyataram avyabhicāriṇau puras agrahaṇāt upādīyate vyākhyātam anupalabdha dṛṣṭvā chatra jātīyam yuktaḥ ṣaṭsu ācāryāḥ saṃdehāt ūha vicārasya manaḥ bahis mukta labhyate nirṇayāya sampratipatteḥ kathayati sūtram ānītaḥ pariṇāha
67	sādhya dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādharmya samaḥ sādharmyāt dṛṣṭānta udāharaṇa vaidharmya śabdaḥ udāharaṇam hetu anityaḥ sādhana sādharmyam dharma pratyavasthānam vaidharmyāt dṛṣṭam anityam hetuḥ vaidharmyeṇa ghaṭaḥ dṛṣṭānte sādharmyeṇa ubhaya r kṛtakam viparīta dṛṣṭāntasya ghaṭa nityaḥ kṛtakaḥ ā upanayaḥ kṛtaka amūrta dharmaka sādhanam vaidharmyam hetau ukte aviśeṣa anitya dharmakaḥ nidarśanam upapatteḥ nigamanam nitya sādhyam h y pratidṛṣṭānta vacanam utpatti udāharaṇena upasaṃhāraḥ hetoḥ sādhyena d ābhāsāḥ i sādhyasya prakaraṇa vikalaḥ nityam nidarśana v prayatna uttaram sama samā dharmakam vaidharmyābhyām pratiṣedhaḥ viśeṣa upasaṃhāre anutpatti t udāharaṇe prayoge aviśeṣaḥ sādhye bhāvī avyāvṛttaḥ k apratiṣedhaḥ p vacana siddheḥ s pañcamī kriyāvān samāḥ prasaṅga dṛṣṭāntena samau kriyāvat abhāvāt mātram prayogaḥ aprāpti anantarīyaka ṇ vaidharmye ahetuḥ jātiḥ pratijñā amūrtam dṛṣṭāntayoḥ ś vyāpti prayukte dṛṣṭāntam sthālī niravayava upapatti mūrtam upasaṃhāra sādharmye sādhakaḥ kiṃcid vākye sarva utkarṣa pratidṛṣṭāntaḥ n samasya parīkṣakāṇām upapadyate viparyayāt vikalpa laukika bhidyate b ākāśa kṛtakāḥ paramāṇuḥ upanaya loṣṭaḥ upasaṃhriyate asparśa doṣāḥ apakarṣa vacane sādhanayoḥ siddhi dravyam nirodha ghaṭena avayava niṣkriyaḥ anityena sādhanasya svarūpa ābhāsaḥ sādhyaḥ m pratiṣedha ṣ dharmaḥ ātmā kṛte prakriyā vikalpāt dharmiṇi ubhayoḥ nirdeśaḥ pradarśanāya g l tasmin paraḥ mūrta dhetu ubhayathā sāmyam avi prayoga dharmasya dharmayoḥ apekṣayā dvividhaḥ avyatirekaḥ sūtram viparītam asiddhaḥ saṃśaya nidarśyate siddhiḥ apadeśāt vikalpaḥ pratidṛṣṭāntasya asādhaka arthāt vaidharmyasya vyatirekaḥ ākāśam pratijña pradarśanam pratyavasthānāt artham pradarśanāt ahetu arthāpattyā ghaṭe tamaḥ prakṛta ukti nityena pratidṛṣṭāntena upanayāt anvayaḥ pratijñāyāḥ draṣṭavyam ādinā āvṛttaḥ nigamana dvividham pradarśyate bhavitavyam ubhayatra sādharmyasya pratyavatiṣṭhate apekṣaḥ iṣyate karma siddhim asādhakaḥ mūrtaḥ āpadyate jātayaḥ yasmin pratipakṣa punarvacanam upapattiḥ veditavyaḥ anuktasya anuṣṇam mūrttam ṛ varṇyāvarṇya sādhaka prayuktaḥ sadbhāva hetutaḥ sthāpanā prasaṅgaḥ vyāvṛttam niṣkriyam āśrayā asu ekatra liṅga viruddhānām doṣau pratiṣedhyena ghaṭayoḥ siddhau anukta viparyaya dṛṣṭāntāt anugamaḥ abhāve upādīyate asarva prayoktavyam ābhāsānām paṃcamyā pīḍane varṇyaḥ ananvayaḥ anumeya arthaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ prabhedaḥ udāharaṇāt upanayasya vaktavye prāpti upādadate anutpattyā dvividhasya paṃcamī prajñāpana arthāpatteḥ upādeyaḥ prayojaka sattva kid tulya apadeśa anupādānāt prāpnoti anugatāḥ lakṣaṇam sādhayet bhāvi aviśiṣṭa asiddha bhāṣye
68	svapna vāsanā mithyā jāgrat pratyaya avidyā satya bhāvanā bāhya parama svapne tattva loka pratyayaḥ vyavahāra bādhaka avasthāyām sarva ālambana artha anādi yoginām bhrāntiḥ vyavahāraḥ advaita saṃvṛti stambha nirālambana jñānam vidyā abhimānaḥ asatya saṃvṛtiḥ pratyayāḥ upaplava sphuṭa paramārthataḥ mātra advaitam upaplavaḥ pratyayasya su tattvam sarvam māyā buddhiḥ bala jāgrataḥ vijñāna timira yogi upapluta abhāvāt vāc pratyayānām vāsanāyāḥ bahis bādhya sarve jñāna avasthā keśa anālambana nidrā prakarṣaḥ prabodha vyavahāram vādinām buddhi buddhīnām cintā vibhrama antar hasti abhyāsa sarpa jñeya rekhā dṛḍha bheda tattvataḥ vāsana svapnaḥ spaṣṭam asatyam satyam loke vastu indrajāla abhimāna pratibhāsaḥ viplavaḥ avidyām mithyātvam pravāha dṛśyate ālambanam alāta sattya bhaya prakarṣa balāt bāhyasya avidyāyāḥ ābham kṣaṇika ābha kāma jñānānām darśanam adarśanāt artham saṃtāna brahma mṛṣā abhūtam yuktyā śoka gaja viśeṣaḥ ālambanā gandharvanagara śakala nirālambanaḥ avabhāsaḥ vādinaḥ pratiyogi viparīta nirālambanāḥ kathaṃcid īdṛśī spaṣṭa prabodhaḥ dṛṣṭa tasyāḥ nirālambanatva taiḥ jāyate pāramārthika anādya mahān vāsanām āśraya dhiyām mṛgatṛṣṇā buddhayaḥ asattve vikalpa mātram yoginaḥ laukika bādhakaḥ kṣaṇikam samāne anupapluta dvaitam satyāḥ vedānta pratisādhanam vitatha mānasī itaratra vāsanānām arthavat gīyate pāramārthikam antarātmanā taimirika viparyaya dhīḥ me pratiyoginī upalabdha sādharmya atattva unmāda nikhila prati buddheḥ yā apekṣayā lākṣā sthitiḥ sakala apahnavaḥ alpaḥ cakṣuṣām avasthitaḥ va upalabdhānām sarvathā avabhāsi caura upahatam anumāna laukikam vyavahārasya āsīt atyanta santāne mṛga paśyanti śūnyam maruṣu vaikharī doṣa bhrānti bāhyam avabhāsate mantra bādha uditam anubaddhasya saṃhṛtya svapnasya pratyaye sthitaḥ akṣa saṃvṛtyā ucchedaḥ astitva vyavasthā darśanāt saṃvṛttyā darśinām jala abhūtān puratas nirvikalpa anyathā bhavanti āyātā saṃvṛtti bāla upaghātaḥ madhyamā strī śūnya bhūtam udbhavā darśana mayam mithyātvāt prabodhāt vaśāt nirālambanatā arthān sarveṣām pariniṣpattau upaplavaiḥ māna pratibhāsam viṣayāḥ vidbhiḥ pratibodhe cakra niṣidhyate taimira vivāda prāk asyāḥ ārya upahata nirālamba vibhāga phalaḥ vidhūta jñānena anumeya aviśeṣaḥ ālambanāḥ avabhāsante padārthānām nirmalam saṃvṛteḥ āyāta abhūta ahi pratyasta gocaram advayam mithyātve ābhāti asantaḥ dhī hīnā vivartate nāma bhedam bhūta vaḥ hetuḥ saṃvṛtya arthena avidyāyām vāsanātaḥ niranvaya dṛṣṭā saṃyamāt abhibhāvyate
69	śarīra karma icchā prayatna śarīram saṃyogāt ātma hasta prayatnaḥ apekṣāt adṛṣṭa nimitta saṃskāra prāṇa kriyā musala asamavāyi śukra ūrdhva śarīre artham jīvana apekṣamāṇāt kāraṇam saṃskārāt saṃskāraḥ utpadyate vāyu tiryak saṃyoga śarīrasya manaḥ jāyate manasoḥ jam āhāra upabhoga karoti gamanam anantaram karmāṇi ahita haste saṃskāram vāyoḥ ūrdhvam saṃyogaḥ utpatana nodana jyā dharma antar pūrvakaḥ śoṇita yoni vaśāt prāpti dhanuḥ prāṇinām kāritam gamana śarīrāt kāle ayonijam iṣoḥ karmaṇā dveṣa ayaskānta musale nimeṣa adṛṣṭāt tṛṇa apāna tasmin utpattiḥ kāraṇāt ākarṣaṇa manasaḥ pūrvaka suptasya adharma anumīyate prayatnena prāṇaḥ preraṇa hita ādyam viśeṣāt unmeṣa prayatnāt sthiti āśaya śarīrāṇi cakra deva manasi prayatnam māṃsa adharmābhyām upasarpaṇam apratyayam apekṣamāṇaḥ vṛddhi saṃyogāḥ mahābhūtānām śarīraḥ dvividham darśayati dūram asthi apasarpaṇa labdha vāta paṭu nodanāt ceṣṭā bhastrā adhiṣṭhitam utpatti vyākhyātam aṇḍa yantra kalala aṇu anuvṛttiḥ vāyau apasarpaṇam jarāyu ādara saṃhāra viśeṣa bhūteṣu vikṛta śarīreṇa mātuḥ sahitebhyaḥ jīvanam harṣa hastena śubha antara parigṛhīta śara ratha gati maheśvara avayaveṣu ayasaḥ maheśvarasya apekṣam mukha parihāra arthaḥ ātmā mūtra upaṣṭambhāt yāvat upasarpaṇa sthita viśiṣṭa samartham smṛti ārabhate mṛta vāyuḥ iṣau vṛtti vega saha ārabdha jīvat sṛṣṭi lakṣaṇaḥ śoṇitam prāyaṇa garbha aṅguli viśiṣṭam hetuḥ sambaddheṣu ulūkhala utpattau samavāyi avasthāyām sarga bhavanti utpannam nimittam jyāyām pelaka viśrāma prabodha adhas bālya padma kṣata viśeṣaḥ aṇubhyaḥ jvalanam ākhyaḥ kampa pūrvakam mātā dāru vṛkṣa yasmin tomara ayonija kāritāni musalayoḥ karmaṇī tiṣṭhati antaḥkaraṇa prayatnasya sannipātaḥ adṛṣṭena āhāraḥ jāni snāyu prerakaḥ pitta aśita prayatne vegam karmaṇaḥ abhimata kāryā abhighātāt abhighāta ākhyāt bhūtebhyaḥ dhanuṣi nāḍī nodane prayatnavān apakṣepaṇa paṭuḥ akṣi pāṇi āparamāṇu bhramaṇam kāruṇyam kṣudra prayatnābhyām upadhā vyāyāma bhoga antareṇa anubandhāt vegaḥ upajāyate ṛṣi darśanāt musalam smita vibhāga sthāpakaḥ pavana mahatā viduṣaḥ gṛhītvā ārohaṇa sveda udare anuvidhāyi śramaḥ sthāpayati aśubha patanam pariṇāma niśi upasaṃhāram ādibhiḥ ādīn saṃrohaṇa tiryyak san uttarasmin bhavataḥ gamanena mala dūṣitaḥ adṛṣṭasya vṛttiḥ āhārasya ātmavat bhedāt varṣa trividham pūrva gatim pāṭavāt tābhyām uktāt loke jantūnām sammīlana iṣu ārabhante anna
70	brāhmaṇa vai brāhmaṇaḥ sāma vidyā aṣṭa agni catur ha veda brahma pitṛ ādhānasya ṛc ādhānam yajñaḥ trayī pavamāna yajña gāyati brāhmaṇasya ādadhīta ṛcaḥ rathantaram karma brāhmaṇam ṛṇa sahasra anuvādaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ devānām devāḥ śūdrasya iṣṭi uccais nindā darśayati vādaḥ praśaṃsā agniḥ kavatīṣu śākhā śrūyate vidvān vasante ante evamādi saṃvatsara agnim karmāṇi manuṣya anāhitāgneḥ mantra trayāṇām prātar vacanam manuṣyāṇām ādhāna amṛta vratam deva brahmacaryam jāyamānaḥ juhoti caraṇa hotavyam karmabhiḥ sarvān śatam upanayanam brahmaṇaḥ āśrama eṣā patnī ādhāne etāni vedāḥ gṛhasthaḥ ācārya stutiḥ rājya divi madhye sma āyuṣaḥ agneḥ eti tri aupabhṛtam gṛhasthasya priyaḥ jarā adhikāraḥ ekaḥ dve kecid adhyayana madhu atharva kṣatriya vāva darśanāt iṣṭayaḥ yajuḥ bhavanti pañcadaśa prajā saṃsthānām udite tarati vid uta yajūṃṣi tāni vrata śūdra dvādaśa devaḥ dṛśyate kāmān apatya rathantara catvāraḥ citiḥ agniṣu atithi gīti śata sarva saṃskṛteṣu saṃvatsaraḥ āhavanīya apatyam śūdraḥ anuyāja etam bhūta uttarayoḥ brahmacārī mṛtyum loke adhyayanam udāharaṇam vacanāt brāhmaṇena ṛṣayaḥ āhutim arthavāda dāra pakṣaḥ brāhmaṇe śrāddha adhyāpanam cayana devān rathakāraḥ upabhṛti varṣāṇi sam śravaṇāt antarikṣam gītiḥ śuśrūṣā yajñānām caturtha agnīn trayaḥ saṃvatsaram svarasya pratyayam vede agnihotram aṣṭau arthi yajñam paṭhyate vāsaḥ jarayā sapta āhuḥ me gṛhṇāti bhāryā artha bṛhat trīṇi pañca vaiśyasya soma adhīte adhyāpana anudite atharvavedaḥ brahmacāri gānam nigadāḥ pañcāśataḥ prārthayante sāmidhenīṣu yajurvedaḥ udita etāḥ enam anuvāda upanīya sāmāni śraddhā ṛtu anuvacanam āśramiṇām yati upadeśaḥ śabdaḥ yāvat gṛhastha rājyam vasanta vihitāni homaḥ anuyājebhyaḥ audgātram caturgṛhītam caturgṛhīte cinutaḥ jauhavam mṛtyunā pākayajña prayāja vidhīyate varṣam tapaḥ grāvāṇaḥ vādāḥ ahe sthapati ādityaḥ punarukta kāle ādhānāt asaṃskṛteṣu vedaḥ bhojanam śeṣaḥ yajñasya lokāḥ prajayā gaḥ mayaḥ sāyam vanaspatayaḥ vihitam upadeśāt ādhattaḥ aditiḥ bhrūṇa dhāyyāḥ dyauḥ eṣaṇāyāḥ nigadaḥ prāpakāṇi pravrajet ṛcam ṛṇaiḥ upanayīta yajuṣā tris lakṣaṇā upakramya viśuddha adhikārāt yoni ācāryakam sāmnā viśvatas etena ācāryaḥ mātā hotra vidhayaḥ tāsām aṅgirasaḥ antarikṣe prajāḥ śravaṇāni saṃstavaḥ vayam vidyāyām svādhyāya kula prayuktam nāma juhuyāt brahmacāriṇaḥ lokān uttamaḥ purā jāyate pitā vihita gāna
71	grahaṇam gṛhyate grahaṇa grahaṇe grahaṇāt agrahaṇam sarva grahaḥ gṛhītam agrahaṇe gṛhyeta mā upakāraka upādhi agrahaṇāt bhūt agrahe grahaṇasya prasaṅgaḥ agrahaṇa sakṛt antara grahaṇena gṛhītaḥ pratītiḥ paścāt pratyakṣeṇa deśa upakārya mātra ātmanā vyāpi saha grahe gṛhīta sakala eka graha upakāra ekayā gṛhyamāṇe yāvat pṛthak prāk gṛhyante antare grahītum antareṇa gṛhyamāṇaḥ rūpa grāhyam agrahāt pūrvam upādhayaḥ grāhikā āśraya agrahaḥ yugapad upakārakaḥ gṛhyete yuktam upādhīnām anavasthā gṛhyamāṇam gṛhīte gṛhyamāṇa anyathā kena śaktam śakti dūrāt grahāt dvayoḥ sambandhi agṛhītam naḥ viśiṣṭa kāle mātrasya doṣaḥ krameṇa gṛhyamāṇasya dṛṣṭam indriyeṇa vyāpitayā taila tvayā tāḥ vivikta grāhakam buddhyā anya grāhyaḥ aśeṣa bhūta gṛhītā vyāpita vivekena upādhinā abhyupagantavyam kṛte niyamaḥ kāla arthasya dhiyā anantaram mātram bhinnāḥ gṛhṇāti dvaya gṛhyamāṇā aprasaṅgaḥ ekā vastunaḥ vivekaḥ avyatirikta bhavatu gṛhītasya samartham grāhī śakyam upakāraḥ aṅga agṛhyamāṇe tāsām asakṛt tvad aneka rahitasya agṛhīta agṛhītaḥ grahaṇaḥ kevalam krama prasaṅga vyavadhānāt agrahaṇena grahaṇāya tyajyatām ayogāt apekṣa apekṣam śaktīnām aṅgaḥ nānā ādibhiḥ vyavahite viviktam bhedaḥ aviśeṣatas tulyam ekasya pratyuktam ārāt viviktayoḥ asat kadācid svāmi avasthaḥ dhī bheda mataḥ svarūpataḥ kevala abhāvāt guroḥ nirvikalpakena grāhayati vaktavyam mukhena prasajyate niyamena bhedasya vinā aśaktam gṛhītum gṛhīteṣu sūrya vāryate upakārake upakāryasya pratipattum bhāvāt pratipattavyam āgrahaḥ anuvidhāyinī śaktayaḥ anyadā cetasoḥ vaśena śakyate upakaroti taiḥ udbhavā sarveṇa mate agṛhītayoḥ gṛhītayoḥ upādhīn upalabhyamānāḥ abhāvaḥ pratyekam ekadā tadānīm grahīṣyate upakārī bhāgasya avasthitānām mecaka grāhakaḥ abhimānaḥ abhyupagamyate tāvatām sthasya arūpa pratīyeran abhyaṅga śaktīḥ sarvadā eta iṣyamāṇe aniścitaḥ grahaṇan smaran agṛhīte agrahaṇasya upādhim pariccheda gṛhītvā apratītau grāhye grāhakeṇa dhiyam dūra kevalasya ādīn sambandhāt apohānām upakārakam asamarthāḥ darśanaḥ anekayā avabhāsinoḥ avyaktī saṃsiddhaḥ asamyak bhūtam kasmāt ati udakena upādheḥ ubhayathā aparaḥ upāttam janane agṛhyamāṇa anākṣepāt grāhyān smaryamāṇayoḥ agratas sanniveśa trailokya upakāri ekena rūpeṇa guru apohe abhimataḥ kṛtā agṛhītasya anyāḥ dvayasya āsya svīkriyamāṇe aniṣṭhā chinnam sārthakam draṣṭṛ grāhiṇaḥ dhīḥ avadhi sannihitaḥ svabhāvam dṛṣṭe ātma rūpañca puruṣau ka saṃskārataḥ netra grahaṇepi upādhimat indriyāt parihārāya apaṭu vārtā icchatā adoṣaḥ apekṣayā abhyupagamyamāne
72	artham tattva pakṣa sādhana nirṇayaḥ upālambhaḥ chala pṛthak tarka vāde pratipakṣa pramāṇa prayojanam artha avadhāraṇam vādaḥ vāda tarkaḥ sādhanam jalpa para grahaṇam ati siddhi nigraha nirṇaya siddhānta pañca sthāna avayava jñāpana jalpaḥ vitaṇḍā pakṣaḥ ūhaḥ arthe upapannaḥ avijñāta chalam pratipakṣābhyām pakṣasya arthaḥ nyāyaḥ upālambha dūṣaṇa prakaraṇa kathā pratiṣedha nyāya tattvam anarthakam saṃśaya sthāpanā tattve pramāṇaiḥ sūtram adhikaraṇa vīta aviruddhaḥ pratyāyanam prayojana kartavyam vakṣyāmaḥ niyama yukta ja asiddhi avadhāraṇa vākya śiṣya parigrahaḥ upapanna ayukta samāsaḥ lakṣaṇe hīnaḥ vimṛśya vaktavyam dūṣaṇam pramāṇāni vacanam sthānānām vitaṇḍa tarkeṇa upapattyā sthānāni pravartate prayogaḥ ābhāsa kila asiddhī pratipakṣau vitaṇḍe vighātaḥ lābha avadhāryate nirṇaye labhyate buddhvā kriyate vākchalam viśeṣataḥ sāmānyacchalam saṃrakṣaṇa tarkasya pratipakṣaḥ niyamaḥ śāstre pratijña ukte nirākaraṇa vicāra asmin adhyavasāya etasmin pade prakaraṇam jalpe viruddhau parīkṣā sūtre avayavam bheda saha jijñāsā dvidhā apare vādasya avayavāḥ nyāyam aṅga vacana upapattitaḥ dharmau tābhyām vijigīṣu vādī prathama uttara vicāraḥ tau adhigamaḥ pradarśana ekatara samāsa sukaraḥ hetvābhāsa niḥśreyasa abhidhānam gamyate ādhikyam lakṣaṇa viṣaya gamyamāna avakāśaḥ parivarjanam arthasya sāmānyatas vimṛṣya vitaṇḍayoḥ lakṣaṇaiḥ dvāreṇa sambhāvanā sāmarthyāt atidiśyate apadiṣṭaḥ upadiṣṭaḥ vākye kartavyaḥ ṣaṣṭhī viṣaye vikalpa grahaṇena jāti upādānam upacāra pakṣayoḥ cintā sāmānya nigamanāni upālambhau vaitaṇḍikaḥ prameya viṣayam padena ābhāsaḥ ādibhiḥ pratipakṣayoḥ svarūpam anyathā lakṣaṇam nyūna avasānaḥ codanīyāḥ uddeśāt vādam parīkṣyate eke etau itaraḥ āgamau pakṣau vastu pravādaḥ nyāyasya rakṣaṇa sthānebhyaḥ vitaṇḍāḥ vākyam samasta hetvābhāsāḥ anugrāhaka tattvasya draṣṭavyaḥ anujānāti upadiṣṭāḥ vādi pakṣam jahāti prayojanā sambhavati sambhavataḥ ābhāse asat avijñātam sādhanena upadeśaḥ codanīya dūṣaṇābhyām nivartate apasiddhānta sūtra vyudāsaḥ traye paramaḥ kathāḥ anabhijña asambhavena ubhayoḥ anyatara ṣoḍaśa vicāre chalasya sambadhyate pravartayati sādhanīya dvitīya kaṇṭaka saṃgṛhītaḥ mūla dūṣaṇaiḥ abhidheyam paribhāṣā sajātīyaḥ jaya svarūpataḥ padārthāḥ prayojanasya pūjā sama abhyanujñāna ekataram nirṇayau sthāpanayā upālambhasya upālambhāya upālambhayoḥ śabdau adhikaraṇau tattvaḥ jāteḥ viśeṣau mumukṣoḥ nirṇīte pratipakṣāt upekṣaṇīyaḥ syātām pratipādaka karaṇam ekaḥ vivecanāt praroha viṣayaḥ arthataḥ sthāpana prameye ni viśeṣa arthau anavadhāraṇāt jñātvā trividham śakya jñāpanam sādhanīyaḥ sthāpayati etāni upadiśyante anugraha yatate
73	anya anyat agniḥ vyavacchedaḥ vyavaccheda siddhiḥ pṛthak anyasya indhanam eka ayoga anyaḥ vyavacchedena apekṣya sahabhāvaḥ saha ananya yoga anyam apekṣā agni agneḥ antara avadhāraṇam anyasmāt anyatra vyavacchinatti indhanāt pūrvakaḥ dhanurdharaḥ vyavacchedasya vyavacchede apekṣate vyavacchedāt indhana sarvasya caitraḥ anapekṣya tattva deśasya auṣṇyam kasyacid pārthaḥ bhāj ayogam paraspara vyavacchidyate anyatva apekṣayā kutaścid itaretara indhane pṛthaktve raktayoḥ vyavasthāpanāt ananyat anyatas vinā idānīm itara bhāvaḥ parihāreṇa paricchedāt avācya yayoḥ anyasmin kam bhaviṣyati saṃbhavati dahati anyā tulya viśeṣaṇa ātmanaḥ jvālā yogam vai vidyate siddhaḥ avadhāraṇe uditaḥ dhanurddharaḥ sarojam nīlam tulyā ekasya agninā atyanta indhanasya asaṃkīrṇa padārtha viśeṣaṇena ākhyam parikalpyate sahabhāva sidhyati āśrayam kriyate avadhāraṇasya itaraḥ anayoḥ aparicchedāt syātām nipātaḥ rūpasya vaiyarthyam anyatayā matam nirapekṣaḥ paricchedaḥ kṛtvā hetukaḥ uktena viśeṣaṇāt agnau apṛthak indhanayoḥ prasaṅgāt apekṣasya asaṃbhavāt liṅgābhyām aprayoge aparaiḥ ṛte prasiddheḥ artham pratiṣedhāt viśeṣaṇam aviśeṣeṇa avyavacchede pṛthagbhāvaḥ deśaḥ vihāya bhāvena nirapekṣa dharmasya saṃkete ekatve yuktam tebhyaḥ apradīpana sthitam pradarśya ani avyatirekeṇa saṃkīrṇa apekṣa ayuktam paricchinatti anukārāt sāmarthyāt vyapadiśyate ukteḥ vācyam apratipattau karmaṇoḥ devadattaḥ kriyayā parihāraḥ yogasya dhvaneḥ sthala pratipādyate apekṣyate sahabhāvam anyonya mātram asiddhayoḥ auṣṇyāt dhakṣyati pathika prameyān yujyate vivakṣā pratiṣiddha apekṣitavyaḥ tulyayoḥ ubhayathā asaṃsargaḥ phalam vartate dahet nipātasya nyāyena nirapekṣasya agnim itarasya atulya viśeṣaṇasya niyatam vilakṣaṇam doṣa abhimateṣu asmāt ananyasmin ayoge indhanābhyām indhanavān srughnam viśeṣyābhyām vyatirecakaḥ vyavacchedanam auṣṇyasya dvividhaḥ rūpāṇām apara bhavitavyam vivakṣātaḥ viśiṣṭā vāraṇāt karaṇam vyavacchedya saṃsargiṇaḥ siddhau ārambha asambhavi pratīyate vṛddhyā ayogasya pakṣāṇām siddhayartham paratra nigamayan puras asaha deśa prapadyate pratiṣedhayoḥ vyavacchedaka tāyāḥ viyoga ananyaḥ sarvaḥ vastu āgacchati pūrvaḥ dhvaninā in pratiniyataḥ anugamāt abhāvāt abhāvam avadhāraṇīyam dhanurdhara ekībhāvena idhyamānam nirupakramam pradīptaḥ pratiniyatāt pṛthagbhāve vyavacchedye udakam andhakāram vidhi ānaya yāyāt yaugapadyam viṣayāt apariccheda indhanāni liṅgavān ātmanā prakramāt pūrvatra siddhasya prasaṅgataḥ ghaṭena sakala icchasi bhāvam prayoge anyān vyavacchedam samuccaya prāpteḥ nibandhanām upakramam viruddhāt prāptaḥ upeyam avadhāraṇāt kevalam anta nyāya apekṣyaḥ gamiṣyati vākyasya tattvam niranvaya vākyam eṣaḥ pratipāditam auṣṇya vyavahāre apākaroti śītam pratipadyate vihitaḥ atidiśan abhyupetam
74	dharma atīta hiṃsā dharmaḥ śyena adharma vartamāna phala anāgata phalam anartha kāla adharmaḥ codanā vihita niṣiddha sādhana anarthaḥ atītaḥ śyenaḥ sādhanāni vartamānaḥ adharmayoḥ anāgatayoḥ anāgataḥ anāgatam sādhanam anuṣṭhānāt dāna phalasya niṣedha adharmau dharmasya śāstra vidhi atītam kālaḥ vidyate vartamānam vidheya ahiṃsā pravṛttiḥ pīḍā pratyavāya tīrtha vidhāna dharme uddeśena japa kāle nimittam yāga guru abhyudaya hiṃsāyāḥ abhāve vartamānasya atīte prayogaḥ tri anṛta bhaviṣyat dānam anāgate lakṣaṇa śuci kartuḥ pratyavāyaḥ vadhaḥ jāta śyenasya hita kriyā pitṛ pratyutpannaḥ hiṃsāyām hiṃsyāt surā śāstreṇa vyāpāraḥ phale anyeṣām pratiṣiddha varjanam niyamāḥ anubandhi pratyutpanna jyotiṣṭoma caitya pratiṣiddhā hetuḥ abhicaran vidhinā prīti śyene sarvadā anugraha dharmam paśu adhvā abhūt yamāḥ prabhavati abhyudayaḥ anna pāna vandana anāgatau viṣa adhva yoginām atītāḥ ācaraṇa brahmahatyā sākṣāt prayogāt etāni prāpnoti dhārmikaḥ steya patita vartamānā adharme anāgatānām daikṣa anuṣṭhāna codanayā vidyamāna bhavadbhiḥ aṅga bhāvanā kriyāṇām dāra anuṣṭhānam pratigraha putra anurūpa karmasu pratiṣṭhā śyenena naraka dhārmika pratiṣedhane śāstrāt gamana hantṛ brahmacarya abhicāra aṅganā patataḥ vihitā pratiṣedha hitam aniṣṭa śauca lakṣaṇaḥ iṣṭa uddiśya satya tadānīm vidhīyate tava anāgatasya niyama anāgatābhyām anupadhā aviśuddhiḥ hiṃsām pratibandhāt upapannam apavāda saṃskārāḥ kālāt anarthasya niḥśreyasāya śreyaskaraḥ tīrthe antaḥkaraṇa aṃśa dāne duṣṭam atīndriyaḥ anurūpam abhyudayāya phalaḥ akaraṇam kartavya vidhīyante vidhānam kriyāḥ mātraḥ gāminī kriyate vidhau kāraṇam sevā tyāgaḥ vartamānena śāstre abhiprāyeṇa vyaṅgyaḥ śāstrasya uktvā anāgatāḥ hiṃsāsu patitavya śreyaskara karmaṇām ādīni raṇa sampradānam vidheyam krodha ādīn ācaraṇam nipatya niṣiddhā pratiṣedhanam prīyate pūjya bhojana dharmatā kūpa dvaye upāyena prāṇinām adharmam lakṣaṇābhyām priyam eṣaḥ svadharma phalānām vrata sāmānyatas sugati vijñāyante kriyamāṇam tādṛś śūdraḥ icchet bhrātṛvyam vihitānām bhaktiḥ hṛdaya patati apekṣau khaṅga ādatte devatā hitvā samāśrayam anuṣṭhīyante apekṣakam asādhāraṇāni aspṛśya asteyam haniṣyāmi hiṃsānām hiṃsitum hiṃsyamānasya nirbījasya pratiṣṭhāyām sevanam svakīyāḥ upavāsa upekṣakam pāpam dharmiṇam upapatteḥ paramparayā trayam vācā aduṣṭe coditā pratimā vyutthānam niṣedhe prāṇi phalāni kṛṣi lagna pibet pīḍām bhūtāyām dṛṣṭānām phaleṣu dharmāṇām akaraṇe śarīreṇa viviktam kartavyatā hīna anantarya jātīyaiḥ puṇyā vidheyasya atītasya saṃkalpa sthitam nara
75	go sādṛśyam gauḥ sādṛśya gavaya upamānam saṃjñā sadṛśa upamāna gavayaḥ sadṛśaḥ gavi saṃjñi aśva prasiddha aśvaḥ gavā sadṛśam upamānasya goḥ piṇḍa avayava sādṛśyasya sādharmyāt viparyayaḥ sārūpya antaram agauḥ sadṛśī gavaye sambandha jñānam gopiṇḍa sādṛśye sādṛśyāt bhūyas upamānena viṣāṇī atideśa sādṛśyena pramāṇa gata upamānāt anadhyavasāyaḥ pratipattiḥ eka aprasiddha sāsna sāsnā deśa sāmānyāni gavayasya pūrvam viṣāṇa gām panasa śruta vākyāt upamīyate sadṛśasya vācyaḥ pratipadyate upamā buddhiḥ loke atyanta sañjñā viṣāṇi ādimān piṇḍam hasti aṭavyām gavayam dharmavat adhyavasāyaḥ śṛṅgam sārūpyam gavayatva śākya antare prasiddham vane bahu abhimānaḥ darśanam phalam dṛṣṭvā upalabhamānaḥ su manda prāya aprasiddhasya darśane madīyā sadṛśāt śṛṅgi citra sadṛśe upamāne viśiṣṭa dvīpa aśve ga aśruta viśiṣṭaḥ upadiśatsu antara avagamyate nimittaka vyāsaṅgāt pratīti sāsnādi vāsinaḥ tādṛśaḥ saurya artheṣu apratyakṣe yādṛśaḥ vanecara saṃjñām dṛṣṭe akṣi siddheḥ sādharmya pratyayāt apekṣām antarbhāvaḥ samākhyā avagata hitam gatam ittham rāma upasaṃhārāt nirvikalpaka pratyakṣe śṛṅga nimittakam smṛti anaśvaḥ gopiṇḍe rāvaṇayoḥ viparīteṣu yamayoḥ bhūyaḥ anarthi viṣaye karabha vāhīkaḥ śreyaḥ ahitam mahiṣa apohaḥ smaraṇāt anyathā pṛṣṭaḥ āmra sādharmyam alpa anantaram mahiṣaḥ ekatra buddhyā nagara samāhāraḥ eṣā abhāvāt siṃha asiddhiḥ kīdṛś mīmāṃsakānām piṇḍasya gavayena gavīti nagare pratiyogikam pūtīkāḥ śṛṅge sāmānyaiḥ upa pratītiḥ nara yava pratīteḥ darśana ākhya vyakti upadeśa danta pratiyogi bahirbhāvāt gavya pariśiṣṭa sadṛśeṣu trayī gaurava apacāre prāṇī stham prasiddhena atiricyate ullekha mudga spaṣṭā prāyas vaya sadṛśā nu jāti pratyakṣāt darśinaḥ ambaram vilakṣaṇena darśanāni bhūyasām samāna ālocanāt nārikela vācyam piṇḍaḥ agāvaḥ dvais gopiṇḍeṣu mātra nimitta upayogaḥ gamyate viparyayam vākya asadṛśa sadṛśena vaiśeṣikeṣu pratiyogini gāvaḥ nimittena aviśeṣaḥ sāmānyānām bodha nimittam upādāya viparītāni saṃjñakaḥ vākyaḥ pratipādanāt etad piṇḍe pradhāna pratyakṣa bodhe avagatam gavām gṛhyate pratyayaḥ sarvam viṣāṇam animittaka anudhāvanti anuvyañjana asadṛśaḥ gavayatvam gavayayoḥ kinnāmā mṛdgavakaḥ mudgaparṇī panaseṣu sādṛśyantu saṃjñinam śārvaram tadbhyām vaisādṛśye yuddha avagate param asiddheḥ vākyam aśvam anupapatteḥ anumāna bhūyāṃsi gagana adhikam aprasiddham gopiṇḍasya sadṛśāni bāhulyena paricchinne anumāya samavetam kṛta sarveṇa abhā sadṛśāḥ vivekāt vana alaukikam adhyāra gurubhiḥ māṣa paśyataḥ samīpa
